### [1] [Birth, Death, and Replication at Surfaces: Universal Laws of Autocatalytic Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21586)
*Denis S. Grebenkov*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个关于表面介导自催化过程（surface-mediated autocatalytic processes）的一般理论框架，通过推导更新型非线性积分方程（renewal-type nonlinear integral equation）与带有非线性Robin型边界条件（nonlinear Robin-type boundary conditions）的Fokker-Planck方程，揭示了表面复制与损失之间的相互作用如何导致丰富的种群动力学（population dynamics），并识别了不同的动力学区间（dynamical regimes）与普适标度律（universal scaling laws）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自催化过程（autocatalytic processes）广泛存在于多类系统中，例如固体基底上的多相催化（heterogeneous catalysis）、膜上的酶活性、病毒感染、生物膜生长及空间结构化生态系统，但其在表面介导情况下的通用理论框架尚不完善，需要系统理解表面复制与损失之间的竞争如何驱动种群动力学行为。

Method: 推导了一个关于种群大小生成函数（generating function）的更新型非线性积分方程，从而给出种群大小的完整概率分布（probability distribution）与统计矩（statistical moments）；同时建立了与之等价的、带有非线性Robin型边界条件的Fokker-Planck方程描述，以编码表面反应（surface reactions）机制。

Result: 识别出不同的动力学区间与普适标度律，并提供了一个统一框架，用于预测表面活动何时促进种群灭绝（extinction）或爆发式增长（explosive growth）。

Conclusion: 该框架为空间异质环境中催化效率（catalytic efficiency）、代谢调控（metabolic regulation）和种群持续（population persistence）提供了定量洞察。

Abstract: Autocatalytic processes underlie diverse systems in which replication is triggered at interfaces, including heterogeneous catalysis on solid substrates, enzyme activity at membranes, viral infections, biofilm growth, and spatially structured ecosystems. In a typical scenario, particles move in a bulk medium and interact with surface regions, where they may either disappear or reproduce through branching, splitting or fission. Here, we develop a general theoretical framework to understand such surface-mediated autocatalytic processes. We show that the interplay between loss and replication at surfaces gives rise to rich population dynamics. For this purpose, we derive a renewal-type nonlinear integral equation for the generating function of the population size, providing access to its full probability distribution and statistical moments. We further establish an equivalent description in terms of a Fokker-Planck equation with nonlinear Robin-type boundary conditions that encode surface reactions. Our results identify distinct dynamical regimes and universal scaling laws, and provide a unified framework to predict when surface activity promotes extinction or explosive growth. These findings offer quantitative insight into catalytic efficiency, metabolic regulation, and population persistence in spatially heterogeneous environments.

</details>

# math.NT [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Residues of a tropical zeta function for convex domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21709)
*Nikita Kalinin,Ernesto Lupercio,Mikhail Shkolnikov*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 本文定义了凸域上的 $\operatorname{SL}_n(\mathbb{Z})$ 不变热带ζ函数（tropical zeta function），在二维情形下建立了 Farey 对（Farey pair）边界狄利克雷级数表示，证明了 $C^3$ 严格凸域上该函数可亚纯延拓至 $\Re(s)>3/5$，在 $s=2/3$ 处有单极点且留数与等仿射周长（equiaffine perimeter）成比例，并利用 Tauber 型论证导出了波前晶格周长（wave-front lattice-perimeter）在 $t\rightarrow 0$ 时的 $t^{1/3}$ 渐近行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有热带几何（tropical geometry）与ζ函数的交叉研究较少，缺乏对凸域热带不变量解析性质的系统性刻画。本文旨在定义一种新的 $\operatorname{SL}_n(\mathbb{Z})$ 不变热带ζ函数，并揭示其解析延拓、极点结构与凸域几何量（等仿射周长）之间的深层联系。

Method: 定义具有 $\operatorname{SL}_n(\mathbb{Z})$ 不变性的凸域热带ζ函数；在二维情形下将其展开为以 Farey 对为指标的边界狄利克雷级数（Dirichlet series）；利用 $C^3$ 光滑严格凸性条件，通过解析延拓技术将定义域延拓至 $\Re(s)>3/5$；最后应用 Tauber 型定理（Tauberian argument）推导渐近公式。

Result: 对于 $C^3$ 严格凸域，热带ζ函数可亚纯延拓到 $\Re(s)>3/5$，在该区域除 $s=2/3$ 处有一个单极点外全纯，极点的留数与凸域的等仿射周长成正比。Tauber 型论证进一步导出波前晶格周长在 $t\rightarrow 0$ 时的 $t^{1/3}$ 渐近增长率。

Conclusion: 本文建立的热带ζ函数为凸域的算术与几何性质之间提供了新的桥梁，其解析结构（极点位置与留数）直接编码了等仿射周长等经典仿射微分几何量，并为波前晶格周长渐近行为给出了严格证明。

Abstract: We define an $\operatorname{SL}_n(\mathbb{Z})$-invariant tropical zeta function of a convex domain. In dimension 2 it admits boundary Dirichlet-series representation with summands indexed by Farey pairs. For $C^3$ strictly convex domains, it extends meromorphically to $\Re(s)>3/5$, holomorphic there except for a simple pole at $s=2/3$, with residue proportional to equiaffine perimeter. A Tauberian argument yields the $t^{1/3}$ wave-front lattice-perimeter asymptotic for $t\rightarrow 0$.

</details>

### [3] [Double circular dichroism high harmonic spectroscopy: An ultrafast probe for topological photocurrents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21121)
*Osamah Sufyan,Ofer Neufeld*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文提出双圆二色性（DCD）谐波光谱学作为一种全光学探针，用于研究拓扑材料中的超快动力学。通过独立控制泵浦和探测脉冲的螺旋度，DCD能够区分体态与边界态对光电流的贡献，并在破缺时间反演对称性的体系（如陈绝缘体）中有效工作。模拟结果表明，体态和边缘态对DCD贡献符号相反、量级相近，从而可实现二者贡献的高效分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解拓扑物质的光学响应对于实现基于拓扑物理的光电器件应用（如光电流控制与光谱学）至关重要，但目前缺乏感知超快光电流并将其体态/表面贡献分离的方案。

Method: 引入双圆二色性（DCD）谐波光谱学：泵浦和探测脉冲均为圆偏振光，其螺旋度可独立调控，从而测量“圆二色性的圆二色性”，即探测诱导的二色性如何依赖于泵浦螺旋度的时间分辨响应。通过在Haldane纳米薄片中进行模拟验证该概念。

Result: DCD在对称系统中消失，但在破缺时间反演对称性材料（如陈绝缘体）中存在。体态和边缘态对DCD的贡献符号相反、量级相近，但振幅标度不同；电子结构与激光参数的变化还揭示了可能用于探测光电流拓扑属性的异常现象。

Conclusion: DCD可能成为一种有效分离破缺对称性量子物质中体态/边界光响应的强大方法，并可推广至基于光电子和吸收的其他泵浦-探测光谱学以及其他手性系统。

Abstract: Understanding optical responses of topological matter is a central problem for enabling optoelectronic applications based on topological physics, which is of fundamental concern for photocurrents control and spectroscopy. Currently, schemes for sensing ultrafast photocurrents and separating their bulk/surface contributions are lacking. We introduce here double circular dichroism (DCD) harmonic spectroscopy as an all-optical probe of ultrafast dynamics in topological materials. In this scheme, pump and probe pulses are circular with helicities that are independently controlled, yielding the circular dichroism of the circular dichroism -- a time-resolved response evaluating how probe-induced dichroism depends on pump helicity. While DCD vanishes in symmetric systems, it survives in broken time-reversal symmetry materials including Chern insulators. We theoretically demonstrate this concept through simulations in a Haldane nanoflake, where a pump laser manipulates chiral current-carrying states, and intense probe pulses drive harmonic emission. We show that DCD originates from both bulk and edge-localized states, but these have opposite signs, similar magnitudes, and a different amplitude scaling. Hence, DCD could allow efficient separation of bulk/edge contributions to photocurrents. Variation of the electronic structure and laser parameters further reveals anomalies that might be useful for probing topological attributes of photocurrents in select harmonics. Overall, our work introduces DCD as a potentially powerful approach for disentangling bulk/boundary photo-responses in broken-symmetry quantum matter, and could also be implemented in other pump-probe spectroscopies based on photoelectrons and absorption, as well as other chiral systems.

</details>


### [4] [Physics of Computation and Behavior in Plants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21763)
*Yasmine Meroz*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一的物理学框架，通过分布式物理计算（distributed physical computation）、具身机械智能（embodied mechanical intelligence）和功能性随机性（functional stochasticity）三个互补原则，将植物的趋性响应、回旋转头运动等行为解释为时空动力系统，从而将植物视为活性物质中分布式计算（decentralized computation）的模型系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 植物在没有中央控制的情况下解决复杂问题，依赖生长驱动的动力学来感知环境、导航并优化资源获取。现有研究缺乏一个统一的物理学框架来系统理解这些行为背后的机制。

Method: 本文以综述形式提出三个互补原则：①分布式物理计算——信息在生化和力学场中编码，经时空整合转化为差异性生长；②具身机械智能——机械相互作用将形态与环境约束耦合，通过材料特性实现计算；③功能性随机性——从分子到有机体尺度的随机涨落作为功能资源，增强感知、探索和集体组织。

Result: 趋性响应和回旋转头运动被解释为时空动力系统（spatio-temporal dynamical systems）。随机涨落被证明在多个尺度上作为功能性资源起作用，而非单纯的噪声。植物行为与结构来自于生长、运输、力学和噪声之间的相互作用。

Conclusion: 植物可作为活性物质（active matter）中分布式计算（decentralized computation）的模型系统，其行为和结构在生长、运输、力学和噪声的相互作用中涌现。

Abstract: Plants solve complex problems without centralized control, relying instead on growth-driven dynamics to sense, navigate, and optimize resource acquisition. This review presents a unified physical framework for understanding plant behavior through three complementary principles: distributed physical computation, embodied mechanical intelligence, and functional stochasticity. Tropic responses and circumnutations are interpreted as spatio-temporal dynamical systems in which information is encoded in biochemical and mechanical fields, integrated over space and time, and translated into differential growth. Mechanical interactions couple morphology to environmental constraints, enabling computation through material properties. Stochastic fluctuations, from molecular to organismal scales, act as functional resources that enhance sensing, exploration, and collective organization. Together, these processes position plants as a model system for decentralized computation in active matter, where behavior and structure emerge from the interplay of growth, transport, mechanics, and noise.

</details>

# cond-mat.quant-gas [[Back]](#toc)

### [5] [Magnetic-field control of interactions in alkaline-earth Rydberg atoms and applications to {\it XXZ} models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21206)
*Masaya Kunimi,Takafumi Tomita*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了碱土（类）里德伯原子88Sr和174Yb之间相互作用的磁场依赖性，发现有效哈密顿量可写为XXZ型量子自旋模型。174Yb在零磁场下的各向异性参数行为显著不同于其他原子，源于其强自旋-轨道耦合。系统计算了有磁场下的相互作用参数，并展示了在一维大各向异性体系和二维正方晶格中的量子多体问题应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解碱土（类）里德伯原子（alkaline-earth(-like) Rydberg atoms）间相互作用的磁场依赖性，并探索其在量子自旋模型中的可实现性，为量子多体物理提供新的可控平台。

Method: 基于88Sr和174Yb的里德伯态|ns,³S₁,m_J⟩与|(n+1)s,³S₁,m_J⟩，推导有效哈密顿量并映射为XXZ型量子自旋模型（XXZ-type quantum spin model）；系统计算有磁场下的相互作用参数，并分析一维和二维晶格系统的基态性质。

Result: 174Yb在零磁场下的各向异性参数（anisotropy parameter）行为显著不同于其他原子，源于其强自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）。相互作用参数可通过磁场调谐。在一维大各向异性区可实现折叠XXZ模型（folded XXZ model）而无需精细调谐磁场；在二维正方晶格中，平均场水平下基态可涌现超固相（supersolid phase）。

Conclusion: 碱土（类）里德伯原子系统的相互作用具有丰富的磁场可调性，174Yb因其强自旋-轨道耦合提供了独特的量子模拟平台，可用于实现折叠XXZ模型和超固相等新奇量子多体现象。

Abstract: We study the magnetic-field dependence of the interactions between two alkaline-earth(-like) Rydberg atoms, ${}^{88}$Sr and ${}^{174}$Yb. Considering the pair of Rydberg states $|ns,{}^3S_1,m_J\rangle$ and $|(n+1)s,{}^3S_1,m_J\rangle$, we show that the effective Hamiltonian takes the form of an {\it XXZ}-type quantum spin model, as in the alkali-atom case [M. Kunimi and T. Tomita, Phys. Rev. A {\bf 112}, L051301 (2025)]. We find that the behavior of the anisotropy parameter for ${}^{174}$Yb at zero magnetic field is significantly different from that for other atomic species. This behavior originates from the strong spin-orbit coupling in ${}^{174}$Yb. We systematically calculate the interaction parameters of the {\it XXZ} model in the presence of a magnetic field and show that they can be tuned by the field. As applications to quantum many-body problems, we investigate one-dimensional systems in the large-anisotropy regime and show that the folded {\it XXZ} model can be realized in ${}^{174}$Yb systems without fine-tuning of the field. We also investigate two-dimensional square-lattice systems and show that a supersolid phase can emerge in the ground state at the mean-field level.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.supr-con'></div>

# cond-mat.supr-con [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [Healing of topological defects while crystallizing nanocrystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21105)
*M. I. Dolz,A. B. Kolton,Y. Fasano*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过朗之万动力学模拟（Langevin dynamics simulations），研究在约束（confinement）条件下涡旋纳米晶（vortex nanocrystals）的结晶动力学和低温结构性质，发现边缘愈合效应与实验数据定量吻合，并证明拓扑缺陷（topological defects）的低温径向分布是由涡旋结构内在性质和约束效应共同决定的稳态剖面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解约束对纳米晶（nanocrystals）结晶过程的影响，对于准确预测其晶体结构和物理性质至关重要。作者旨在揭示涡旋密度、系统弹性及样品尺寸等因素如何影响受限纳米晶的结晶动力学和低温结构特性。

Method: 研究采用朗之万动力学模拟（Langevin dynamics simulations），以微米级超导体中成核的数百个涡旋作为模型系统，模拟在场冷（field-cooling）条件下涡旋纳米晶的结晶过程，并系统改变涡旋密度、系统弹性和样品物理尺寸等参数。

Result: 模拟获得的低温快照显示，边缘存在愈合效应（healing effect），该效应与Bi₂Sr₂CaCu₂O₈₊δ微米级样品的实验数据定量一致。进一步发现，拓扑缺陷的低温径向分布是一个稳态剖面（stationary profile），其冻结温度由涡旋结构的内在性质和约束效应共同决定。

Conclusion: 这些关于拓扑缺陷动力学和空间分布规律的研究结果，可推广用于描述受限软凝聚态纳米晶（confined soft condensed matter nanocrystals）的物理性质，为更一般化的受限体系提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Understanding the role of confinement while crystallizing nanocrystals is very relevant for predicting their structure and physical properties. With this aim we perform Langevin dynamics simulations of nanocrystals of the model system of few hundred vortices nucleated in micron-sized superconductors. We study the crystallization dynamics and the low-temperature structural properties of vortex nanocrystals nucleated in field-cooling conditions when changing vortex density or elasticity of the system and physical size of the samples. The low-temperature snapshots obtained in simulations present a healing effect at the edges that is in quantitative agreement with experimental data in Bi2Sr2CaCu2O8+δ micron-sized samples. We show that the low-temperature radial distribution of topological defects is a stationary profile frozen at a temperature below the melting line tuned by intrinsic properties of the vortex structure and on the confinement effect. These findings on the dynamics and spatial profile of topological defects can be applied to describe the physical properties of confined soft condensed matter nanocrystals in general.

</details>


### [7] [Controlled Manipulation of Intermediate State in a Type-I Superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21499)
*Xin-Sheng Gao,Qun Wang,Ya-Xun He,Xing-Jian Liu,Jun-Han Zhang,Kang-Hong Yin,Jia-Ying Zhang,Jun-Yi Ge*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究利用低温磁力显微镜，在I类超导体（type-I superconductor）钽单晶中实现了磁通结构（flux structure）的直接成像与可控操控，揭示了从磁通管到条纹的形态演化、拓扑迟滞（topological hysteresis）现象，以及交流激励下的可逆条纹-网格-条纹转变，建立了主动操控磁通结构的途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: I类超导体的中间态（intermediate state）是涡旋间短程吸引与长程排斥竞争导致的经典调制图案（modulated pattern）范式，但长期以来，对这些磁通结构的直接可视化与主动拓扑及动力学操控仍面临重大挑战，限制了其基础研究与潜在应用。

Method: 采用低温磁力显微镜（low-temperature magnetic force microscopy）对高纯钽单晶（high-purity tantalum single crystal）中的磁通结构进行直接成像与可控操控，系统追踪磁通进入与排出过程中的形态演化，并利用磁力探针进行局部拖拽、合并以及全局交流（AC）激励下的动态重组实验。

Result: 观测到磁通形态从磁通管到条纹的系统演化，发现由几何势垒（geometric barrier）引起的显著拓扑迟滞；实现了利用磁力探针对单个磁通管的拖拽、合并以及对整个条纹区域的重新构型；在交流激励下发现了可逆的条纹-网格-条纹（stripe-grid-stripe）转变，其阈值电流随磁场增大而减小，随交流频率增大而增大。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一条在I类超导体中主动操控磁通的途径，揭示了丰富的动力学行为，为基于磁通（flux-based）的超导器件发展奠定了基础。

Abstract: The intermediate state of type-I superconductors presents a classic paradigm of modulated pattern formation, arising from the competition between short-range attractive and long-range repulsive vortex-vortex interactions. However, direct visualization and, more importantly, active control over the topology and dynamics of these flux structures have remained significant challenges, limiting our ability to manipulate them for fundamental studies and potential applications. Here, using low-temperature magnetic force microscopy, we achieve direct imaging and controllable manipulation of the flux structures in a high-purity tantalum single crystal. We systematically track the evolution of flux morphology - from tubes to stripes - during flux penetration and expulsion, revealing a pronounced topological hysteresis originating from the geometric barrier. Furthermore, we demonstrate precise local control by using the magnetic tip to drag and merge individual flux tubes and to reconfigure entire stripe domains. Under global alternating current (AC) excitation, we discover a reversible stripe-grid-stripe transition, a dynamic reorganization driven by current-induced flux penetration and pinning effects. The corresponding phase diagram shows that the threshold current decreases with magnetic field but increases with AC frequency. Our work establishes a pathway for active flux manipulation in type-I superconductors, revealing rich dynamics and paving the way for flux-based superconducting devices.

</details>


### [8] [Pairing mechanism and superconductivity in 1313 phase La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21533)
*Cui-Qun Chen,Ming Zhang,Fan Yang,Dao-Xin Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过DFT+DMFT和RPA方法系统研究了加压下1313型La₃Ni₂O₇的电子性质和超导机制，发现超导主要存在于三明治（TL）子系统中，具有$s^{\pm}$-波配对对称性，并揭示了空穴掺杂和层间约瑟夫森耦合是导致其超导转变温度低于块体La₄Ni₃O₁₀的两个关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验发现加压下1313型La₃Ni₂O₇的超导转变温度约为3.6 K，引起了广泛关注，但其超导机制以及为何超导温度相对较低（相对于块体La₄Ni₃O₁₀）尚未清晰，因此需要对其进行系统的电子性质和超导机制研究。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论加动力学平均场理论（DFT+DMFT）计算电子结构，并基于DFT+DMFT导出的低能有效哈密顿量，使用随机相位近似（RPA）分析超导配对对称性和配对强度。

Result: DFT+DMFT计算表明，单层（SL）子体系表现出近绝缘行为，$d_{z^2}$轨道呈现莫特物理（Mott physics）；三明治（TL）子体系保持金属性，其Ni-$e_g$轨道相对于块体La₄Ni₃O₁₀为空穴掺杂。RPA分析得出TL子体系内为$s^{\pm}$-波配对对称性。空穴掺杂降低了配对强度，同时SL子体系作为连接相邻超导TL子体系的桥梁形成S-N-S约瑟夫森结，层间约瑟夫森耦合进一步压制了全局超导转变温度。

Conclusion: 1313型La₃Ni₂O₇中超导转变温度受限于两个因素：TL子体系的空穴掺杂导致的配对强度降低，以及SL子体系形成的S-N-S约瑟夫森结对相干的压制。因此，该家族中的高温超导相应归因于2222型La₃Ni₂O₇而非1313型。

Abstract: Recently, the observation of superconductivity (SC) with $T_c$ $\approx$ 3.6 K in the pressurized 1313 La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ has attracted considerable interest. Here, we systematically investigate the electronic properties and superconducting mechanism of 1313 La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ using density functional theory plus dynamical mean-field theory (DFT+DMFT) and random phase approximation (RPA). Our DFT+DMFT calculations reveal that the single-layer (SL) subsystem exhibits nearly insulating behavior, with the $d_{z^2}$ orbital showing Mott physics, while the trilayer (TL) subsystem remains metallic. This indicates that SC primarily resides in the TL subsystem, whose Ni-$e_g$ orbitals are found to be hole-doped relative to bulk La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$. Based on DFT+DMFT-derived low-energy Hamiltonian, RPA-based analysis yields an $s^{\pm}$-wave pairing symmetry within the TL subsystem. Importantly, we identify two key factors that contribute to the significant suppression of $T_c$ in 1313 La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ compared to bulk La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$. First, the hole doping in the TL subsystem, as established by DMFT, leads to a decreased pairing strength, as confirmed by RPA calculations -- a trend resembling that in bulk La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$. Second, the SL subsystem acts as a bridge connecting adjacent superconducting TL subsystems, thereby forming an S-N-S Josephson junction. The resulting interlayer Josephson coupling governs the phase coherence between TL subsystems and further suppresses the global $T_c$. Combinedly, our findings suggest that the high-$T_c$ phase in the RP La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ family should be attributed to the 2222 La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ rather than the 1313 La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$.

</details>


### [9] [Superconductivity induced by altermagnetic spin fluctuations in high-pressure MnB$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21561)
*Danylo Radevych,Mercè Roig,Daniel F. Agterberg,Igor I. Mazin*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 针对MnB₄在158 GPa下高临界温度（约14 K）超导现象与传统电声子耦合理论预测（低于1 K）的矛盾，本文提出超导电性由交变磁自旋涨落（altermagnetic spin fluctuations）驱动，并通过双轨道紧束缚模型（two-orbital tight-binding model）识别出扩展-s（extended-s）配对对称性为主导不稳定性。若获证实，这将是交变磁自旋涨落驱动超导的首个实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验在非磁性MnB₄中发现约14 K的高温超导，但基于电声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）的第一性原理计算给出的临界温度低于1 K，说明传统常规机制（conventional mechanism）无法解释该现象，亟需探索新的超导驱动机制。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（DFT）计算分析能带与磁不稳定性；构建双轨道紧束缚模型，将费米面附近的硼态积分掉（integrated out），降维处理电子结构以分析配对不稳定性。

Result: DFT计算显示MnB₄接近交变磁不稳定性（altermagnetic instability）；通过有效模型识别出扩展-s对称性为主导配对不稳定性。

Conclusion: 提出MnB₄中的超导由交变磁自旋涨落驱动；若被实验或进一步理论验证，这将是首次报道的交变磁自旋涨落驱动超导的案例。

Abstract: Recent experiments found superconductivity in nonmagnetic MnB$_4$ with a high critical temperature ($T_{c}$) reaching 14 K at 158 GPa. However, ab initio calculations of the electron-phonon coupling predict a $T_{c}$ below 1 K, suggesting that a conventional mechanism cannot explain this phenomenon. In this Letter, we find that MnB$_4$ is close to an altermagnetic instability in density-functional theory calculations. We propose that the superconductivity is driven by altermagnetic spin fluctuations. To verify the pairing symmetry, we have constructed a two-orbital tight-binding model, where boron states at the Fermi level are integrated out. Using this model, we identify an extended-$s$ symmetry as the leading pairing instability. If confirmed, this will be the first reported case of superconductivity driven by altermagnetic spin fluctuations.

### [10] [Two-gap to Single-gap Transition and Two-dome-like Superconductivity in Alkali-Metal Intercalated Bilayer PdTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21635)
*Yu-Lin Han,Shu-Xiang Qiao,Kai-Yue Jiang,Jie Zhang,Bao-Tian Wang,Ping Zhang,C. S. Ting,Hong-Yan Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 基于全各向异性Migdal-Eliashberg框架的第一性原理计算，该研究揭示了碱金属插层可显著增强双层PdTe2的弱超导电性，使超导转变温度（Tc）从1.4 K提升至5.0–13.5 K，并呈现双穹顶演化；铷插层实现最高Tc达13.5 K，双轴拉伸应变可进一步将其提升至14.5 K。研究还发现层间相互作用与超导能隙存在系统性关联，锂插层诱导双能隙态，而大半径碱金属插层导致单能隙态，该转变源于插层引起的层间膨胀对层间耦合的调制。此外，原始及Li/Na插层双层体系具有非平庸能带拓扑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验上已合成厚度可控至单层极限的PdTe2，但其弱超导电性有待提升；同时，理解各向异性电声耦合（EPC）机制以及超导与拓扑物性的共存条件，对于在层状PdTe2体系中实现更高超导转变温度（Tc）和丰富物性至关重要。

Method: 采用基于全各向异性Migdal-Eliashberg框架的第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations within the fully anisotropic Migdal-Eliashberg framework），系统研究了碱金属插层和双轴拉伸应变对双层PdTe2超导性质的影响。

Result: 碱金属插层使双层PdTe2的Tc从1.4 K提升至5.0–13.5 K，呈双穹顶（two-dome-like）演化；铷插层Tc最高（13.5 K），在双轴拉伸应变下可进一步升至14.5 K，应变依赖的Tc也呈双穹顶行为。锂插层诱导双能隙（two-gap）超导态，而Na、K、Rb、Cs插层则产生单能隙（single-gap）态。原始及Li/Na插层体系表现出非平庸能带拓扑（nontrivial band topology）。

Conclusion: 研究结果为层状PdTe2体系中增强Tc和实现多样化物性提供了各向异性电声耦合（EPC）的详细理解及可行的调控路径，并表明该体系是探索超导电性与非平庸拓扑共存的理想平台。

Abstract: PdTe2 has been synthesized with controllable thickness down to the monolayer limit. Based on first-principles calculations within the fully anisotropic Migdal-Eliashberg framework, this work reveals that alkali-metal intercalation markedly enhances the weak superconductivity of bilayer PdTe2, boosting the transition temperature from 1.4 K to 5.0 -13.5 K and yielding a two-dome-like evolution of Tc. Rubidium intercalation induces the highest Tc of 13.5 K, which can be further increased to 14.5 K under biaxial tensile strain. The strain-dependent evolution of Tc also exhibits a two-dome-like behavior, reflecting the interplay between strain-induced band structure modifications and electron-phonon coupling (EPC). Moreover, a systematic correlation is identified between interlayer interaction and superconducting gap. Lithium intercalation induces a distinct two-gap state, whereas intercalants with larger atomic radii (Na, K, Rb, and Cs) drive the system into a single-gap character. The two-gap to single-gap transition originates from the modulation of interlayer coupling through intercalation-induced interlayer expansion. In addition, pristine and Li/Na-intercalated bilayers exhibit nontrivial band topology, suggesting that layered PdTe2 provides a promising platform for realizing the coexistence of superconductivity and nontrivial topology. These results provide detailed anisotropic insights into EPC and offer viable pathways for enhancing Tc and achieving diverse properties in layered PdTe2 systems.

### [11] [Effect of Mn Substitution on Superconductivity in PrFeAs(O,F): Role of Magnetic Impurities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21684)
*Priya Singh,Konrad Kwatek,Tatiana Zajarniuk,Taras Palasyuk,Cezariusz Jastrzębski,A. Szewczyk,Michał Wierzbicki,Shiv J. Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过结构、拉曼光谱、密度泛函理论（DFT）、输运和磁性测量，系统研究了PrFe₁₋ₓMnₓAsO₀.₇F₀.₃体系中Mn替代Fe的效果。结果表明，Mn优先掺入FeAs平面，导致晶格膨胀并抑制Fe相关振动模式；超导转变温度从48 K（x=0）降至x=0.1时完全消失，低温电阻率呈现绝缘体行为；Mn作为高效磁性杂质强烈扰动FeAs层的电子与磁性环境，且Pr基体系表现出相对更强的超导鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Mn替代Fe位对铁基超导体PrFe₁₋ₓMnₓAsO₀.₇F₀.₃的结构、电子输运和超导特性的影响，明确Mn作为磁性杂质的扰动机制，以及稀土元素依赖的电子关联效应在杂质影响中的角色。

Method: 结合X射线衍射、拉曼光谱、密度泛函理论（DFT）计算、电输运测量与磁化/磁输运测量，对PrFe₁₋ₓMnₓAsO₀.₇F₀.₃（x=0至0.1）体系进行多维度表征。

Result: Mn优先掺入FeAs平面，引起晶格膨胀并抑制Fe相关振动模式；超导转变温度从48 K（x=0）系统性降至x=0.1时完全消失，低温电阻率回升并呈现绝缘体行为；磁化与磁输运测量显示超导相干性、临界电流密度、上临界场和涡旋激活能随Mn含量增加而退化。

Conclusion: Mn作为高效磁性杂质，强烈扰动FeAs层的电子与磁性环境，从而抑制超导性；Pr基体系相比其他稀土体系表现出相对更强的超导鲁棒性，表明稀土依赖的电子关联效应在杂质效应中起重要作用。

Abstract: We investigate Mn substitution at the Fe site in PrFe1-xMnxAsO0.7F0.3 (0 to 0.1) using structural, Raman, density functional theory (DFT), transport, and magnetic measurements. X-ray diffraction and Raman analyses confirm preferential Mn incorporation into the FeAs planes, accompanied by lattice expansion and suppression of Fe-related vibrational modes. Electrical transport reveals a systematic decrease of the superconducting transition temperature from 48 K (x = 0) to complete suppression at x = 0.1, together with low-temperature resistivity upturns evolving toward insulating-like behavior. Magnetization and magnetotransport measurements show degradation of superconducting coherence, critical current density, upper critical field, and vortex activation energy with increasing Mn content. The results demonstrate that Mn acts as an efficient magnetic impurity, strongly perturbing the electronic and magnetic environment of the FeAs layers. Comparative analysis indicates relatively enhanced robustness of superconductivity in the Pr-based system, highlighting the role of rare-earth-dependent electronic correlations in impurity effects.

### [12] [$3d_{z^2}$ orbital delocalization and magnetic collapse in superconducting (La,Pr)$_3$Ni$_2$O$_{7-δ}$ films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21899)
*Xiaoyang Chen,Wenliang Zhang,Fei Peng,Ting Cui,Guangdi Zhou,Zezhong Li,Jaewon Choi,Lizhi Xu,Yiu-Fung Chiu,Stefano Agrestini,Sahil Tippireddy,Haoliang Huang,Heng Wang,Xianfeng Wu,Peng Li,Jin-Feng Jia,Mirian Garcia-Fernandez,Yi Lu,Er-Jia Guo,Qi-Kun Xue,Zhuoyu Chen,Donglai Feng,Ke-Jin Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过X射线吸收谱和共振非弹性X射线散射，独立调控(La,Pr)₃Ni₂O₇₋δ薄膜的应变和氧含量，揭示了一条从母相到超导相的两步演化路径：首先Ni 3d_{z^2}和O 2p_z轨道离域化，随后长程自旋密度波（SDW）序被抑制而短程磁振子（magnons）保持稳健，建立了轨道选择的RP型镍酸盐超导机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RP型（Ruddlesden-Popper）镍酸盐薄膜超导体的发现开辟了非常规超导电性的新前沿，但其从母相到超导相的微观路径尚不清楚，作者试图通过独立调控应变和氧含量来追踪这一演化过程。

Method: 在(La,Pr)₃Ni₂O₇₋δ薄膜中独立调控应变（即压缩外延应变，compressive epitaxial strain）和氧含量（oxygen content），并结合X射线吸收谱（X-ray absorption spectroscopy, XAS）和共振非弹性X射线散射（resonant inelastic X-ray scattering, RIXS）进行表征。

Result: 发现了显著的两步演化：第一步，应变异或氧含量调控均导致谱权重从上哈伯德峰（upper Hubbard-like peak）转移到与O 2p_z态相关的空穴峰，同时局域的Ni 3d_{z^2}轨道变得巡游（itinerant），伴随dd轨道激发的展宽和减弱；第二步，长程自旋密度波（spin-density-wave, SDW）序的强度和关联长度均被抑制，而短程磁振子（magnons）虽被阻尼但带宽保持不变。

Conclusion: 应变和氧化共同驱动RP双层镍酸盐走向超导不稳定性，其关键在于层间3d_{z^2}-2p_z-3d_{z^2}分子轨道的离域化以及SDW序熔化后短程磁振子的稳健存在，为理论和镍酸盐超导体设计提供了强约束和路线图。

Abstract: The recent discovery of Ruddlesden-Popper (RP) nickelate thin-film superconductors has opened a new frontier in unconventional superconductivity. Its realization requires both compressive epitaxial strain and highly oxidative growth conditions, yet the microscopic pathway from the parent phase to the superconducting phase remains elusive. Here, X-ray absorption spectroscopy and resonant inelastic X-ray scattering are employed to track this evolution by independently tuning strain and oxygen content in (La,Pr)$_3$Ni$_2$O$_{7-δ}$ thin films. We uncover a remarkable two-step evolution. First, signatures of delocalization emerge in the same way upon two independent tunings: spectral weight transfers from an upper Hubbard-like peak to the hole-like peak associated with the O $2p_z$ state, and in parallel, the initially localized Ni $3d_{z^2}$ orbital becomes more itinerant, accompanied by the broadening and weakening of $dd$ orbital excitations. Second, as itinerancy increases, long-range spin-density-wave (SDW) order is suppressed in both intensity and correlation length, indicating direct competition with superconductivity. Yet, short-range magnons persist: they become damped, but their bandwidth remains unchanged. Our results paint a coherent picture in which both strain and oxygenation drive the RP bilayer nickelates towards superconducting instability, where the O $2p_z$ and Ni $3d_{z^2}$ orbitals become delocalized. Concomitantly, the long-range magnetic order loses coherence and is suppressed. These findings establish an orbital-selective route to RP nickelate superconductivity, in which the delocalization of the interlayer $3d_{z^2}$-$2p_z$-$3d_{z^2}$ molecular orbital and the robust short-range magnons upon the melting of SDW order are prerequisites, providing strong constraints for theory and a roadmap for designing nickelate superconductors.

</details>

# math.PR [[Back]](#toc)

### [13] [Discontinuous transition in 2D Potts: II. Order-Order Interface convergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21669)
*Moritz Dober,Alexander Glazman,Sébastien Ott*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文首次严格证明了 $q>4$ 时方格上 $q$-态 Potts 模型在临界点 $T_c(q)$ 的润湿现象（wetting phenomenon）：两个有序相之间出现无序层，其边界在扩散标度下收敛为一对条件不相交的布朗运动。该结果基于随机簇表示、Ashkin-Teller 模型耦合及熵排斥机制，并推广了此前仅适用于大 $q$ 的表面张力构造。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: $q$-态 Potts 模型是相变理论中的经典模型，其在方格上 $q>4$ 时发生不连续相变。此前关于临界点处界面性质的结论（Bricmont--Lebowitz '87, Messager 等 '91）仅局限于大 $q$ 情形下表面张力（surface tension）的构造与性质，尚未建立精确几何形式的润湿现象（wetting phenomenon）且未覆盖整个不连续相变区域 $q>4$。

Method: 本文通过随机簇表示（random-cluster representation）将 Potts 模型与 Ashkin-Teller 模型（ATRC）耦合，进而与六顶点模型（six-vertex model）关联。在此基础上，将一对有序-无序（order-disorder）Dobrushin 界面（interface）构成的系统耦合到一对条件不相交的随机游走上，利用严格推导的熵排斥（entropic repulsion）机制建立耦合。同行工作（arXiv:2502.04129）发展了类 Ornstein-Zernike 的更新图景（renewal picture），为 Potts 界面的研究提供了核心工具。

Result: 在 $q>4$ 的整个不连续相变区间内，于临界点 $T_c(q)$ 处建立了润湿现象的精确几何形式：两个有序相之间出现无序层（disordered layer），在扩散标度（diffusive scaling）下该层的边界收敛为一对条件不相交的布朗运动（Brownian motions conditioned not to intersect）。此外，还证明了 FK 逾渗模型（FK-percolation model）在 $p_c(q)$ 且 $q>4$ 时界面的收敛性。

Conclusion: 本文在 $q>4$ 的整个不连续相变区域严格证明了临界点处的润湿现象，显著推广了此前仅适用于大 $q$ 的表面张力结果。该结论与亚临界（$T<T_c(q)$）行为形成鲜明对比，为理解 Potts 模型中有序相之间的界面结构提供了完整几何描述。

Abstract: The $q$-state Potts model is an archetypical model for various types of phase transitions. We consider it on the square grid and focus on the regime where it undergoes a discontinuous transition, that is $q>4$. At the transition point $T_c(q)$, there are exactly $q+1$ extremal Gibbs measures (pure phases): $q$ ordered (monochromatic) and one disordered (free). This work establishes for the first time the wetting phenomenon in a precise geometric form and in the entire regime of discontinuity $q>4$: at $T_c(q)$, between two ordered phases a disordered layer emerges and, in the diffusive scaling, its boundaries converge to a pair of Brownian motions conditioned not to intersect. This is starkly different from the subcritical ($T<T_c(q)$) behaviour. At $T_c(q)$, previous results (Bricmont--Lebowitz '87, Messager--Miracle-Sole--Ruiz--Shlosman '91) were limited to the construction and properties of the surface tension for large enough $q$.
  In a companion work, arXiv:2502.04129, we provide a detailed study of the Potts model under order-disorder Dobrushin conditions. That work also develops a ``renewal picture'' à la Ornstein-Zernike for a suitable percolation model, which plays a central part in our study of the Potts interfaces. The latter is the random-cluster representation of an Ashkin--Teller model (ATRC), and is related to the Potts model via a chain of couplings going through the six-vertex model.
  In the current work, we extend the analysis to a pair of interacting order-disorder interfaces forming the separation between the two ordered phases, and couple them to a pair of well-behaved random walks conditioned not to intersect. The construction of the coupling is based on rigorously deriving entropic repulsion between the two interfaces. We also prove convergence of interfaces in the FK-percolation model at $p_c(q)$ when $q>4$.

</details>

# astro-ph.HE [[Back]](#toc)

### [14] [Probing Supermassive Black Hole Mergers with Pulsar Timing Arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20975)
*Hippolyte Quelquejay Leclere*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文证明脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）可通过引力波信号的“脉冲星项”（pulsar term）探测在计时观测开始前就已合并的超大质量双黑洞（SMBHB）系统，即“僵尸双星”（zombie binaries），并基于当前PTA约束下的种群模型预测，平方公里阵列（SKA）有望在将来检测到若干此类信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前PTA主要搜寻纳赫兹频段内由正在旋近（inspiraling）的SMBHB产生的引力波信号，但尚未系统探讨那些在观测开始前就已合并的SMBHB是否也能被PTA探测。

Method: 利用GW信号计时残差波形中的“脉冲星项”（pulsar term），识别在计时观测开始前已合并的SMBHB（称为僵尸双星，zombie binaries），并使用符合当前PTA约束的SMBHB种群模型进行探测概率评估。

Result: 现有PTA数据集检测到僵尸双星的概率仍然较低；但平方公里阵列（Square Kilometer Array, SKA）预计将达到足够灵敏度，在其数据中可拥有数个信噪比超过3的僵尸双星候选体。

Conclusion: 尽管对僵尸双星的可靠识别可能具有挑战性，但这类新PTA源为研究本地宇宙中最重的SMBHB开辟了新的窗口。

Abstract: By monitoring the times of arrival of radio pulses from millisecond pulsars, Pulsar Timing Arrays (PTAs) serve as unique gravitational wave (GW) laboratories in the nanohertz band. To date, the primary astrophysical sources of GWs targeted in this frequency range have been inspiraling supermassive black hole binaries (SMBHBs) on circular and eccentric orbits. In this work, we demonstrate that, thanks to the so-called pulsar term in the timing residual waveform of GW signals, PTAs can probe individual SMBHBs that merged before timing observations began. We refer to the latter as \emph{zombie binaries}. Using SMBHB population models consistent with current PTA constraints, we find that while the probability of detecting such systems in existing PTA datasets remains low, the Square Kilometer Array observatory is expected to achieve sufficient sensitivity to have a few zombie binaries with a signal-to-noise ratio exceeding 3 in its data. Although their confident identification might be challenging, this new class of PTA sources opens a novel window for studying the most massive SMBHBs in our local universe.

</details>


### [15] [Gravity Echoes from Supermassive Black Hole Binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21010)
*Qinyuan Zheng,Bence Bécsy,Chiara M. F. Mingarelli*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）中的“脉冲星项”可作为引力回波，用于探测超大质量双黑洞（SMBHB）的长期演化。通过结合μHz波段的地球项直接测量与nHz波段脉冲星项的历史快照，可获得单一探测器无法实现的长时间基线，从而实现双黑洞演化速率测量、独立天区定位及后牛顿演化相干追踪。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）主要利用地球项探测引力波背景，但脉冲星项携带双黑洞早期演化的历史信息，尚未被系统地用作演化探针。本文旨在展示未来μHz波段引力波任务（如μAres）可将脉冲星项转化为针对双黑洞演化的定向探测工具。

Method: 采用引力回波（gravity echo）的类比框架，将每个脉冲星项视为双黑洞在早期旋近阶段的时间快照。结合μHz波段地球项直接测量与nHz波段多个脉冲星项的历史回波，构建跨频段联合分析。对于典型等质量双黑洞（总质量10⁹ M⊙、距离80 Mpc），计算脉冲星计时阵列回波的信噪比（SNR），并分析单脉冲星回波灵敏度的角依赖性和脉冲星项频率对旋近速率的约束能力。

Result: 对于参考双黑洞系统，脉冲星计时阵列回波联合信噪比达33，最多24颗脉冲星可在50年基线中独立分辨回波信号。单脉冲星回波灵敏度可实现10–100平方度的独立天区定位。分辨出的脉冲星项频率可直接测量数百至数千年前的双黑洞旋近速率。若脉冲星距离测量足够精确，少量锚定脉冲星可相位连接整个阵列，实现跨越千秒差距（kpc）基线的后牛顿演化相干追踪。

Conclusion: μHz波段探测可显著增强PTA脉冲星项作为引力回波的诊断能力，将双黑洞演化研究从统计背景推进到单个源的定向演化追踪。所需源种群与观测到的纳赫兹（nHz）随机背景来源一致，表明该方法在现有宇宙学框架内具备可行性。

Abstract: Pulsar timing arrays record gravitational waves from supermassive black hole binaries at two spacetime points: an Earth term, measured when the wave passes the Earth, and a pulsar term, measured when the wave passed each pulsar at an earlier epoch. We show that a future $μ$Hz-band detection of a nearby massive binary by a mission such as $μ$Ares would turn PTA pulsar terms into targeted probes of binary evolution. In analogy with supernova light echoes, each pulsar term acts as a gravity echo: a dated snapshot of the binary at an earlier stage of its inspiral. Together, the $μ$Hz Earth-term measurement and the nHz pulsar-term echoes provide a temporal baseline that neither detector could access alone. For a fiducial equal-mass binary with total mass $10^9\,M_\odot$ at 80~Mpc, we find a combined pulsar timing array echo signal-to-noise ratio of 33, with up to 24 pulsars individually resolving the signal among pulsars with 50-year baselines. The angular dependence of the single-pulsar echo sensitivity alone enables independent sky localization of the source to $\sim$10--100~deg$^2$, and the resolved pulsar-term frequencies directly measure the binary inspiral rate hundreds to thousands of years ago. With sufficient pulsar distance precision, a small set of anchor pulsars could additionally phase-connect the array and trace the post-Newtonian evolution coherently over kpc baselines. The source population required for gravity echoes is drawn from the same massive-end census responsible for the observed nanoHertz stochastic background.

</details>


### [16] [Archival Multiband Gravitational-Wave Signals from Massive Black Hole Binary Mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21013)
*Alexander W. Criswell,Stephen R. Taylor,Kris Pardo,Alberto Sesana,David Izquierdo,Silvia Bonoli,Daniele Spinoso*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文发现超大质量双黑洞（MBHB）在引力波频段高于脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）灵敏度带时，会在PTA的“脉冲星项”（pulsar term）中留下孤立的低频贡献，并提出如何在全PTA阵列中叠加这些信号并进行多波段联合搜索的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PTA通常无法直接探测高频合并的MBHB引力波信号，但脉冲星项作为时间延迟探测机制可能保留这些信号的残余低频成分，然而此前缺乏系统的理论研究。

Method: 分析了脉冲星项因光传播时间延迟而表现出的频率响应特性，该响应依赖于MBHB的起源方向和内禀属性；提出了一种跨全阵列叠加这些孤立脉冲星项的方法。

Result: 展示了MBHB的啁啾合并（chirping merger）在PTA脉冲星项中留下的孤立的低频贡献及其频率响应机制；给出了在全PTA阵列中叠加这些信号的具体思路。

Conclusion: 该方法有望与天体测量数据或空间干涉仪（如LISA）观测到的MBHB合并事件结合，开展归档性的多波段搜索（multiband search）。

Abstract: While massive black hole binaries (MBHBs) merge at gravitational-wave frequencies above the pulsar timing array (PTA) sensitivity band, we show that they leave orphaned low-frequency contributions in the PTA pulsar term. Due to the light-propagation time between each pulsar in the array and Earth, the pulsar term acts as a time-delayed probe of a chirping merger with a specific frequency response determined by the direction of origin and intrinsic properties of the MBHB. We provide a detailed consideration of how such a multiband signal would manifest in a full PTA, demonstrate an approach to stack these orphaned pulsar terms across the array, and discuss prospects for an archival, multiband search in conjunction with MBHB mergers observed in astrometric data or spaceborne interferometers like LISA.

### [17] [Mitigating Systematic Errors in Parameter Estimation of Binary Black Hole Mergers in O1-O3 LIGO-Virgo Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21859)
*Sumit Kumar,Max Melching,Frank Ohme,Harsh Narola,Tom Dooney,Chris Van Den Broeck*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种数据驱动的参数化模型方法，通过放宽不确定性参数的先验分布来有效减少引力波参数估计中的系统性误差。该方法使不同波形模型和不同数据处理流程下的推断结果趋于一致，并在GW191109_010717和GW200129_065458等事件中得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波并合事件的参数估计（parameter estimation）常受多种系统性误差（systematic errors）影响，包括波形系统学（waveform systematics）、噪声表征不准确、数据分析伪影（data artifacts）等，需发展有效方法加以识别和校正。

Method: 选用LVK前三次观测运行中已被其他研究标记为可能存在系统性误差的事件，使用前期工作中开发的参数化模型（parametric models），该模型在波形相位（phase）和振幅（amplitude）中均引入不确定性参数，并采用足够宽松的先验分布（broad priors）以涵盖潜在系统性误差，从而进行数据驱动的重分析（data-driven reanalysis）。

Result: 该方法有效减少了系统性误差，包括由信号附近的毛刺（glitches）和去毛刺处理（deglitching process）引起的数据伪影；不同波形模型之间原本不一致的结果在本框架下趋于一致。对于GW191109_010717，反自旋（anti-aligned spin）特性保持稳定；对于GW200129_065458，旋进参数（χ_p）在不同波形模型间取得非零且一致的数值：IMRPhenomXPHM为0.60^{+0.31}_{-0.33}，IMRPhenomXO4a为0.58^{+0.30}_{-0.29}，NRSur7dq4为0.56^{+0.31}_{-0.28}。

Conclusion: 所提出的数据驱动参数化模型框架能有效抑制多种来源的系统性误差，提升引力波参数估计的鲁棒性和一致性，特别适用于存在数据伪影或波形模型差异较大的事件。

Abstract: Systematic errors in the parameter estimation (PE) of gravitational wave (GW) mergers can arise from various sources, including waveform systematics, noise mischaracterization, data analysis artifacts, and other unknown factors. In this study, we analyze selected events from the first three observing runs of the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) collaboration. We choose events that have been flagged in various studies as potentially affected by systematic errors. Here, we reanalyze these events using a couple of parametric models developed in previous work that incorporate uncertainties in both the phase and amplitude of the GW waveform. In this data-driven approach, we apply sufficiently broad priors on the uncertainty parameters to account for potential systematic errors. Our findings show that the proposed method effectively reduces systematic errors, even those arising from data artifacts, such as glitches occurring near a signal and the deglitching process in GW frame files. Similarly, inconsistent results from different waveform models become much more consistent in our framework. One noteworthy event we examine is GW191109\_010717, which is particularly interesting due to its anti-aligned spin properties. We report that, within our framework, the event still exhibits anti-aligned spin characteristics, but the inference results become consistent across raw and deglitched frame files, as well as across the waveform models used for this event (IMRPhenomXPHM, IMRPhenomXO4a, and NRSur7dq4). A similar trend is observed for the event GW200129\_065458, which previously yielded a high, but inconsistent precession parameter among different waveform models. In contrast, we observe a non-zero and consistent value of $χ_{p}=0.60^{+0.31}_{-0.33}, 0.58^{+0.30}_{-0.29}$ and $0.56^{+0.31}_{-0.28}$ for the IMRPhenomXPHM, IMRPhenomXO4a, and NRSur7dq4 waveform models, respectively.

</details>

### [18] [The CriticalSet problem: Identifying Critical Contributors in Bipartite Dependency Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21537)
*Sebastiano A. Piccolo,Andrea Tagarelli*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了网络科学中的CriticalSet问题（在二分依赖网络中识别关键节点），证明其为NP-hard且目标函数为超模函数使贪心算法无近似保证；通过博弈论建模推导出ShapleyCov中心性指标，并设计了线性时间的迭代剥离算法MinCov，在大规模真实网络上达到接近最优的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图挖掘方法主要关注单类节点网络的全局覆盖或传播机制，但针对二分依赖网络（bipartite dependency network）中“全有或全无（all-or-nothing）”覆盖机制的关键节点识别问题尚未得到充分探索。

Method: 形式化定义CriticalSet问题，证明其NP-hard性并揭示目标函数为超模函数（supermodular set function），导致前向贪心算法无近似保证；将该问题建模为联盟博弈（coalitional game），基于Shapley值推导出闭式中心性指标ShapleyCov（表示某贡献者离开后预期孤立的项目数）；据此提出MinCov算法，一种线性时间迭代剥离（peeling）算法，显式处理连接冗余，优先选择独特支持最多项目的贡献者。

Result: 在合成数据和包含超过2.5亿条边的Wikipedia真实大规模图上，MinCov和ShapleyCov显著优于传统基线方法；MinCov达到接近最优的性能，其AUC与随机爬山元启发式（Stochastic Hill Climbing metaheuristic）的差距仅为0.02，同时运行速度快数个数量级。

Conclusion: 面向二分依赖网络的CriticalSet问题可以通过博弈论方法有效求解；提出的MinCov算法在保证接近最优效果的同时具备极高的计算效率，为大规模二分依赖网络中的关键节点识别提供了实用方案。

Abstract: Identifying critical nodes in complex networks is a fundamental task in graph mining. Yet, methods addressing an all-or-nothing coverage mechanics in a bipartite dependency network, a graph with two types of nodes where edges represent dependency relationships across the two groups only, remain largely unexplored. We formalize the CriticalSet problem: given an arbitrary bipartite graph modeling dependencies of items on contributors, identify the set of k contributors whose removal isolates the largest number of items. We prove that this problem is NP-hard and requires maximizing a supermodular set function, for which standard forward greedy algorithms provide no approximation guarantees. Consequently, we model CriticalSet as a coalitional game, deriving a closed-form centrality, ShapleyCov, based on the Shapley value. This measure can be interpreted as the expected number of items isolated by a contributor's departure. Leveraging these insights, we propose MinCov, a linear-time iterative peeling algorithm that explicitly accounts for connection redundancy, prioritizing contributors who uniquely support many items. Extensive experiments on synthetic and large-scale real datasets, including a Wikipedia graph with over 250 million edges, reveal that MinCov and ShapleyCov significantly outperform traditional baselines. Notably, MinCov achieves near-optimal performance, within 0.02 AUC of a Stochastic Hill Climbing metaheuristic, while remaining several orders of magnitude faster.

</details>

### [19] [Chern-Simons couplings, modular duality, and anomaly cancellation in abelian F-theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20880)
*Mir Faizal,Arshid Shabir*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，在F-理论（F-theory）紧化中，将理论紧化在一个圆圈（circle）上后，三维理论中的量子化Chern-Simons耦合能够以单圈精确且与方案无关的方式编码所有四维阿贝尔反常（abelian anomalies），包括混合规范-引力项及其Green-Schwarz抵消机制，并通过M-理论对偶和显式单圈积分两种独立方法验证了这一结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: F-理论紧化中具有非平凡Mordell-Weil群的结构通过有理截面实现阿贝尔规范对称性（abelian gauge symmetry），但其一致性最终依赖于量子有效作用量（quantum effective action）的表述。本文旨在将这一抽象陈述具体化，证明圆紧化后的三维Chern-Simons耦合可以完整编码四维阿贝尔反常及其Green-Schwarz抵消。

Method: 首先将F-理论紧化在圆圈上，得到三维有效理论；然后通过两种独立方法确定其中的量子化Chern-Simons耦合：其一是从M-理论（M-theory）对偶描述中的流诱导项（flux-induced terms）导出，其二是对完整的重谱（massive spectrum）包括Kaluza-Klein塔（Kaluza-Klein towers）和Coulomb支态（Coulomb-branch states）进行显式单圈积分。最后，在引入已知的十维对偶抵消项（duality counterterm）后，验证与IIB型模对偶（type IIB modular duality）的兼容性。

Result: 三维Chern-Simons耦合以单圈精确且与方案无关的方式编码了所有局域四维阿贝尔反常，包括混合规范-引力反常（mixed gauge-gravitational anomalies）及其Green-Schwarz抵消（Green-Schwarz cancellation）。两种独立方法的结果一致，固定了所有归一化，并阐明了大规范变换（large gauge transformations）如何重组谱结构。此外，在引入十维对偶抵消项后，该框架与IIB型模对偶兼容，并在三维投影空间（projective three-space）上给出了一个完全显式的秩二示例。

Conclusion: 通过圆紧化，F-理论紧化中阿贝尔反常的量子一致性可以被三维Chern-Simons耦合精确捕获，这为理解更高维反常结构及其抵消提供了统一且计算方法无关的框架，同时通过对偶和显式积分的一致性验证了框架的正确性。

Abstract: F-theory compactifications with a nontrivial Mordell-Weil group realize abelian gauge symmetry through rational sections, but their consistency is ultimately a statement about the quantum effective action. We show that compactification on a circle makes this statement concrete: the quantized, parity-odd Chern-Simons couplings of the resulting three-dimensional theory provide a one-loop exact and scheme-independent encoding of all local four-dimensional abelian anomalies, including the mixed gauge-gravitational terms, together with their Green-Schwarz cancellation. We determine these Chern-Simons couplings in two logically independent ways, first from flux-induced terms in the M-theory dual description, and second from an explicit one-loop integration over the complete massive spectrum, including Kaluza-Klein towers and Coulomb-branch states. The agreement fixes all normalizations and clarifies how large gauge transformations reorganize the spectrum. We then show compatibility with type IIB modular duality once the known ten-dimensional duality counterterm is included, and we present a fully explicit rank-two example over projective three-space.

</details>


### [20] [SubTropica](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20954)
*Mathieu Giroux,Sebastian Mizera,Giulio Salvatori*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一个名为 SubTropica 的 Mathematica 软件包，它利用热带几何（tropical geometry）的最新进展，对多对数值积分（multi-polylogarithmic integrals）进行符号积分，重点处理线性可约的欧拉积分（如费曼积分），并采用热带减除方案展开。同时文档说明了其底层的 HyperIntica 包，并引入了一个由 AI 驱动的费曼积分库，该库配有在线图形界面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现高效自动化符号积分，尤其是针对费曼积分（Feynman integrals）等线性可约欧拉积分（linearly-reducible Euler integrals）的计算，以减轻理论物理中的手工计算负担。

Method: 基于热带几何（tropical geometry）方法，结合热带减除方案（tropical subtraction scheme）对积分进行展开；底层依赖 HyperIntica 包实现超对数积分（hyperlogarithm integration）。此外，构建了一个 AI 驱动的费曼积分库，并开发了在线图形用户界面。

Result: 完成了 SubTropica 和 HyperIntica 两个 Mathematica 软件包的开发与文档编写，并通过多个物理学应用示例展示了其用法。在线费曼积分库已在 https://subtropi.ca 上线，支持图形化输入与记录检索。

Conclusion: SubTropica 及其配套包为符号积分（symbolic integration）提供了一套自动化工具，结合 AI 驱动的数据库，有助于系统化整理与获取费曼积分结果。

Abstract: We present SubTropica, a Mathematica package that performs symbolic integration of multi-polylogarithmic integrals using recent advances in tropical geometry. It focuses on the class of linearly-reducible Euler integrals, such as Feynman integrals, and expands them using a tropical subtraction scheme. The engine behind it is HyperIntica, a native Mathematica package for hyperlogarithm integration that can be used independently.
  This paper documents both packages and illustrates their usage on examples from across different physics applications. Additionally, we introduce an AI-driven library of Feynman integrals, which catalogs diagrams discussed in the literature and serves as a database for computed results. Its online version is available at: https://subtropi.ca and features a graphical user interface for diagram input and retrieval of records.

</details>


### [21] [Twisted traces and quantization of moduli stacks of 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ Chern-Simons-matter theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20959)
*Leonardo Santilli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文猜想并举例论证，三维N=4 Chern-Simons-物质理论的球面配分函数可以表示为真空模空间量子化上的Verma模张量积的扭曲迹之和，将Gaiotto-Okazaki猜想推广至Chern-Simons-物质理论，并展示了带高阶荷的Abel规范理论的配分函数具有此类扭曲迹分解，揭示了有无Chern-Simons耦合的理论之间的新Abel对偶性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Gaiotto-Okazaki关于三维N=4超对称理论球面配分函数与扭曲迹关系的猜想，从非Chern-Simons型理论推广至更一般的Chern-Simons-物质理论（Chern-Simons-matter theories），以建立更广泛的配分函数代数结构。

Method: 通过大量例子（a plethora of examples）进行验证与展示，并针对带高阶荷（higher charges）的Abel规范理论（Abelian gauge theory）进行显式分解证明。

Result: 证明了三维N=4 Chern-Simons-物质理论的球面配分函数可分解为真空模空间（moduli spaces of vacua）量子化上的Verma模（Verma modules）张量积的扭曲迹（twisted traces）之和；所有带高阶荷的Abel规范理论均具有该扭曲迹分解结构；并发现了有无Chern-Simons耦合的理论之间的新Abel对偶性（Abelian dualities）。

Abstract: We conjecture, and show in a plethora of examples, that the sphere partition function of 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ Chern-Simons-matter theories equals a sum of twisted traces on tensor products of Verma modules over the quantization of the moduli spaces of vacua. This extends a conjecture of Gaiotto-Okazaki to Chern-Simons-matter theories. We also show that the partition function of every Abelian gauge theory with higher charges has such twisted trace decomposition, and uncover new Abelian dualities between theories with and without Chern-Simons couplings.

Abstract: We present a dual gravity interpretation of the complex reparametrization mode $ψ(u)$ that governs the soft dynamics of double-scaled SYK in the presence of a time-dependent Maldacena-Qi coupling. In this note, we apply the chiral algebra bootstrap to the simple example of self-dual 4d $\mathscr{N}=4$ super Yang-Mills (SDSYM). We use a combination of twistor space input, Koszul duality, supersymmetry, and associativity to obtain the all-loop holomorphic collinear splitting functions for SDSYM. We also use associativity to provide a simple proof of the conjecture that there are no double-poles in the loop-level OPEs for this theory. Conclusion: 全局德西特时空中的全息复杂度结果因设置（边界CFT与膜上CFT）不同而存在差异，且与文献中德西特局部坐标片段下的结果有显著区别，表明全息复杂度对时空全局几何与对偶设置敏感。

Abstract: We compute the holographic complexity of conformal quantum fields in rigid global de Sitter spacetime (dS$_{d}$) using the volume and action prescriptions. First we consider AdS$_{d+1}$ spacetime in global dS$_{d}$ foliations, and compute the complexity of the CFT supported on the global dS$_{d}$ conformal boundary. Next, we consider CFT supported on a global dS$_d$ (UV) brane embedded in AdS$_{d+1}$ spacetime, and compute the holographic complexity in this brane set up.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于$O(d,d)$对称ansatz的作用量，该作用量被论证可描述弦理论的经典NSNS扇区。在此框架下构造渐近AdS$_5$黑膜解，并分析曲率修正对奇点行为以及膨胀子动力学的影响。

Result: 曲率修正无法消除视界后的奇点（singularity），但会改变趋近奇点时的Kasner指数（Kasner exponents）；在非平凡膨胀子的存在下，曲率修正可在小耦合区域动态生成负宇宙常数（negative cosmological constant）。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，所考虑的曲率修正虽不能解决奇点问题，但能改变奇点附近的几何行为；同时，通过动态生成的负宇宙常数，为弦理论对偶中渐近自由的产生提供了一种可能的机制。

Abstract: We construct asymptotically AdS$_5$ black brane solutions in a theory of gravity with an infinite series of curvature corrections. The action is based on an $O(d,d)$ symmetric ansatz which has been argued to describe the classical NSNS sector of string theories. We find that, for this general class of theories, the singularity behind the horizon is not resolved by the curvature corrections. The approach to the singularity is however generically modified, being characterized by different Kasner exponents. We also show that, in the presence of a non-trivial dilaton, a slight generalization of these types of curvature corrections can generate dynamically a negative cosmological constant in the region of small coupling. This provides a mechanism through which asymptotic freedom could emerge in the hypothetical string dual of QCD.

### [27] [Fermion Condensate Inflation, Dynamical Waterfall Mechanism and Primordial Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21535)
*Stephon Alexander,Pisin Chen,Jinglong Liu,Antonino Marciano,Misao Sasaki,Xuan-Lin Su*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种费米子凝聚暴胀（fermion condensate inflation）模型，暴胀由时空挠率（spacetime torsion）诱导的四费米子相互作用产生，无需引入标准模型之外的新标量场。暴胀结束后，手征化学势（axial chemical potential）触发瀑布相变（waterfall phase）并引发瞬时预加热（instant preheating）；瀑布相中形成的非拓扑孤子（Q-ball）可成为原初黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）的种子。该模型与Chern-Simons引力内在关联，预示着宇称破缺（parity-violating）宇宙，可通过PBH暗物质丰度和宇称破缺信号进行观测检验。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将费米子场分解为两个不同部门（sector），各自形成束缚态。在积分掉费米子后，束缚场充当暴胀子和辅助场，类似于混合暴胀（hybrid inflation）中的瀑布机制（waterfall mechanism）。引入手征化学势以自然终止暴胀并触发瞬时预加热。在瀑布相中，费米子凝聚的有效势支持非拓扑孤子（Q-ball）的形成。

Result: 费米子凝聚暴胀模型无需额外标量场即可驱动暴胀；瀑布相中的Q-ball可作为原初黑洞的种子；模型与Chern-Simons引力内在关联，预言宇称破缺的宇宙。PBH暗物质丰度和宇称破缺信号被认为是该模型的两个潜在观测检验途径。

Conclusion: 费米子凝聚暴胀模型在统一暴胀、预加热、原初黑洞形成及宇称破缺方面展现出理论自洽性，并提供了可观测的检验窗口（PBH暗物质与宇称破缺信号）。该工作为探索暴胀与引力、粒子物理之间的深层联系提供了新视角。

Abstract: Fermion condensate inflation, where inflation emerges from four-fermion interactions induced by spacetime torsion, removes the need for additional scalar fields beyond the Standard Model. In this framework, the fermion field can be decomposed into two distinguished sectors, each giving rise to bound states. After integrating out fermions, the bound fields play the roles of the inflaton and the auxiliary fields, resembling hybrid inflation with a waterfall mechanism. The inclusion of an axial chemical potential naturally introduces a mechanism to end inflation and trigger instant preheating. During the waterfall phase, the effective potential of the fermion condensate supports the formation of non-topological solitons such as Q-balls, which act as seeds of primordial black holes. This model is intrinsically connected to Chern-Simons gravity, which implies a parity-violating universe. Consequently, both the primordial black hole (PBH) dark-matter abundance and parity-violation signatures could provide observational tests of the model.

### [28] [IR behaviour of one-loop complex $\mathbb{R}\times S^3$ saddles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21736)
*Shubhashis Mallik,Gaurav Narain*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在四维爱因斯坦-希尔伯特引力（Einstein-Hilbert gravity）中，研究了 $\mathbb{R}\times S^3$ 复度规（complex metrics）的引力路径积分（gravitational path-integral），分析了不同边界条件下复鞍点（complex saddles）的红外性质，并计算了单圈重整化的 Hartle-Hawking 波函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有涨落的 $\mathbb{R}\times S^3$ 复度规上的引力路径积分，旨在探究不同边界选择下复鞍点的红外（IR）性质，以及宇宙从欧几里得（Euclidean）相到洛伦兹（Lorentzian）相的过渡机制。

Method: 采用 ADM 分解（ADM-decomposition），在初始边界施加“无边界”（no-boundary）条件，在最终边界分别考虑狄利克雷（Dirichlet）条件和固定外曲率（fixed extrinsic curvature）条件。使用 Hurwitz-Zeta 正则化（Hurwitz-Zeta regularization）计算单圈修正的 lapse 作用量，并通过 Picard-Lefschetz 方法和 WKB 方法（WKB method）计算单圈重整化 Hartle-Hawking 波函数，辅以 $i\varepsilon$ 规则（通过将宇宙学常数 $\Lambda$ 轻微复化实现）。

Result: 两种边界情形下，宇宙均经历从欧几里得相到洛伦兹相的转变；欧几里得相的主导鞍点为虚时间的欧几里得度规，洛伦兹相则有两个复度规作为主导鞍点叠加。度规涨落导致单圈波函数中出现随宇宙膨胀而长期增长的红外发散（secularly growing infrared divergences）。纯洛伦兹 dS 情形给出实鞍点。所有边界选择下，鞍点均保持 KSW 允许（KSW-allowed）。

Conclusion: 单圈重整化的 dS 波函数与 Hartle-Hawking 无边宇宙具有相同的领先阶红外发散。Picard-Lefschetz 方法单独不足以克服单圈计算的技术困难，需引入 $i\varepsilon$ 规则补充。

Abstract: Gravitational path-integral over $\mathbb{R}\times S^3$ complex metrics with fluctuations is studied in 4D for Einstein-Hilbert gravity in Lorentzian signature, with the aim to investigate the IR properties of complex saddles for various boundary choices. General covariance doesn't allow arbitrary boundary choices for the background and fluctuations. In the ADM-decomposition, while imposing ``no-boundary'' condition at the initial boundary, two scenarios are considered for the final boundary: Dirichlet and fixed extrinsic curvature. Universe undergoes transition from a Euclidean to Lorentzian phase in either scenario, where the dominant saddle in Euclidean phase correspond to a Euclidean metric (imaginary time), while the Lorentzian phase has two complex metrics as dominant saddles which superimpose. One-loop corrected lapse action is computed using Hurwitz-Zeta regularization. UV-divergences canceled by suitable counter terms lead to a renormalized lapse action. One-loop renormalized Hartle-Hawking wave-function is computed using the Picard-Lefschetz and WKB methods, where the contributions coming from the metric-fluctuations show secularly growing infrared divergences as the Universe expands. This is compared with the situation in pure Lorentzian dS, corresponding to a Universe transitioning from an initial state of vanishing conjugate momenta to final state of fixed extrinsic curvature, thereby giving real saddles. Picard-Lefschetz methods alone are not sufficient to overcome the technical hurdles in the one-loop computation, which needs to be supplemented by an $iε$-prescription, achieved via slight complexification of the cosmological constant $Λ$. The UV renormalized one-loop dS wavefunction has the same leading IR divergence as for the Hartle-Hawking no-boundary Universe. Interestingly for all boundary choices considered, the saddles remain KSW-allowed.

### [29] [Unitary Time Evolution and Vacuum for a Quantum Stable Ghost](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21823)
*Cédric Deffayet,Atabak Fathe Jalali,Aaron Held,Shinji Mukohyama,Alexander Vikman*

TL;DR: 本文对经典稳定的谐振子-鬼场（ghost）耦合系统进行量子化，证明了一个具有正离散谱的运动积分导致哈密顿量具有双向无界纯点谱、演化幺正、真空良好定义且正则变量平方期望值有界，并通过数值验证，认为该离散谱可推广至扩展相互作用中的稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典稳定的谐振子与负动能鬼场（ghost）耦合系统在量子化后可能面临稳定性问题，本文旨在证明该量子系统在特定运动积分（integral of motion）的离散谱约束下仍保持良定义且幺正演化。

Method: 对谐振子与鬼场的多项式耦合系统进行正则量子化；解析证明一个具有正离散谱的运动积分的存在性及其对哈密顿量谱、演化幺正性、真空与期望值有界性的影响；通过数值求解薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）验证解析结论。

Result: 哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）具有双向无界的纯点谱（pure point spectrum）；演化显式幺正（unitary）；真空（vacuum）良定义；正则变量的平方期望值有界；数值解与解析证明一致。

Conclusion: 该运动积分的离散谱（discrete spectrum）是系统稳定性的关键机制，并有望推广至更广泛的扩展相互作用情形。

Abstract: We quantize a classically stable system of a harmonic oscillator polynomially coupled to a ghost with negative kinetic energy. We prove that due to an integral of motion with a positive discrete spectrum: i) the Hamiltonian has a pure point spectrum unbounded in both directions, ii) the evolution is manifestly unitary, iii) the vacuum is well-defined, iv) expectation values for squares of canonical variables are bounded. Numerical solutions of the Schrödinger equation confirm these results. We argue that the discrete spectrum of the integral of motion enforces stability for extended interactions.

</details>


### [30] [Quantum mechanics with a ghost: Counterexamples to spectral denseness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21826)
*Cédric Deffayet,Atabak Fathe Jalali,Aaron Held,Shinji Mukohyama,Alexander Vikman*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文量化了具有相反符号动能项和非平凡相互作用的可积点粒子系统，利用可分离性理论证明经典稳定性条件也意味着离散分离的特征值谱，并建立了存在至多一个聚点或无聚点的充分条件，推翻了“鬼魅量子系统必然具有连续或稠密能谱”的普遍观念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有普遍观念认为，包含相反符号动能项（即“鬼魅”（ghostly））的量子系统必然具有连续或稠密的能谱。本文旨在通过量化具有相反符号动能项和非平凡相互作用的可积点粒子系统，检验并修正这一观念。

Method: 采用可分离性理论（separability theory）的方法，对具有相反符号动能项和相互作用的可积点粒子系统进行量子化处理。

Result: 经典稳定性条件也意味着离散分离的特征值谱（discrete separated eigenvalue spectra）；所得能谱在上下均无界，但不一定是稠密的；建立了恰好存在一个聚点（accumulation point）或完全没有聚点的充分条件。

Conclusion: 推翻了“鬼魅量子系统必须具有连续或稠密能谱”的广泛观念，表明此类系统的能谱可以具有更丰富的离散结构。

Abstract: We quantise integrable point-particle systems with opposite-sign kinetic terms and nontrivial interactions. Using methods from separability theory, we show that previously determined classical stability conditions also imply discrete separated eigenvalue spectra. The resulting energy spectrum is unbounded above and below but not necessarily dense. We establish sufficient conditions for (i) exactly one accumulation point, or (ii) none at all. This dispels the widespread notion that ghostly quantum systems must have a continuous or dense energy spectrum.

</details>


### [31] [High-energy photon hologram of a photon gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21835)
*P. O. Kazinski,A. A. Sokolov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文推导了光子气体单粒子密度矩阵的光子全息图（photon hologram），包括探测光子能量超过电子-正电子对产生阈值的情况；给出了高斯型以及相干和非相干高斯晶格形式下的全息图显式表达式，并发现相干与非相干晶格的共振锥条件不同；进一步推导了光子气体和单光子在任意量子态下的介电张量（dielectric susceptibility tensor），证明其在相干散射中表现为具有线性和圆双折射（linear and circular birefringences）的介质，在阈值以下透明、以上吸收；并指出在现有实验条件下可实现测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究光子气体的全息结构，特别是在探测光子能量高于电子-正电子对产生阈值（electron-positron pair creation threshold）时的情况，以及光子气体在相干散射中表现出的介质性质。

Method: 从光子气体的单粒子密度矩阵（one-particle density matrix）出发推导其光子全息图；分别针对单高斯型、相干与非相干高斯晶格（coherent and incoherent lattices of Gaussians）形式给出显式表达式；在探测光子质壳（on the probe photon mass-shell）上推导光子气体及单光子的介电张量。

Result: 得到了高斯型及相干/非相干晶格形式下全息图的显式表达式；发现相干与非相干晶格的共振散射锥（resonant cones of coherent scattering）条件不同；推导了介电张量的显式表达式；发现光子气体和单光子在相干散射中表现为具有线性和圆双折射的介质，在电子-正电子产生阈值以下透明、以上吸收。

Conclusion: 对于探测光子能量约1 GeV及以上、靶光子能量约1 eV及以上、且光子气体密度使经典强度参数（classical intensity parameter）量级为1的情况，利用现有实验设施可测量光子气体的全息图。

Abstract: The photon hologram of a one-particle density matrix of a photon gas is derived including the case where the energy of a probe photon is above the electron-positron pair creation threshold. The explicit expressions for the holograms of a photon gas with one-particle density matrix in the form of a single Gaussian and of coherent and incoherent lattices of Gaussians are obtained. The conditions for resonant cones of coherent scattering by coherent and incoherent lattices are found. These conditions turn out to be different. The explicit expression for the dielectric susceptibility tensor of a photon gas and of a single photon prepared in arbitrary quantum states are derived on the probe photon mass-shell. It is established that a photon gas and a single photon behave in coherent photon scattering as a medium with linear and circular birefringences that is transparent below the electron-positron creation threshold and is absorbing otherwise. It is shown that, for the probe photon energies of order $1$ GeV and higher, the energies of target photons of order $1$ eV and higher, and the photon gas density such that the classical intensity parameter is of order unity, the hologram of the photon gas can be measured with existing experimental facilities.

</details>

### [32] [Orbital angular momentum radiation and polarization of relativistic electrons in magnetic fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21856)
*Ziqiang Huang,Qi Meng,Xuan Liu,Wei Ma,Zhen Yang,Liang Lu,Alexander J. Silenko,Pengming Zhang,Liping Zou*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了相对论性电子在均匀磁场中同步辐射（synchrotron radiation）所导致的轨道角动量（OAM）极化现象。结果表明，在低光子能量区域跃迁率不对称，倾向于减小OAM，类似于Sokolov-Ternov效应中的自旋翻转不对称性。OAM极化时间比自旋极化时间短数个量级，对于大OAM，OAM极化率\(\mathcal{P}_{\text{OAM}}\)可接近100%。同步辐射因此可用于控制高能加速器中的涡旋电子束（vortex electron beams）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 同步辐射的自旋极化（spin polarization）已广为人知，但辐射过程中轨道角动量（OAM）的极化尚未被充分理解。本研究旨在探索涡旋电子（vortex electrons）在均匀磁场中的OAM极化辐射机制，填补该领域的空白。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，研究携带固有OAM的涡旋电子在均匀磁场中的辐射与极化行为；通过解析推导获得特征弛豫时间（relaxation time）和稳态OAM分布，并与Sokolov-Ternov效应进行类比分析。

Result: 在低光子能量区域跃迁率不对称，有利于OAM减小，类似自旋翻转不对称性。自旋极化率\(\mathcal{P}_{\text{spin}}\)可达92.38%，而OAM极化率\(\mathcal{P}_{\text{OAM}}\)在大OAM下可接近100%。在典型储存环参数下，OAM极化时间比自旋极化时间短数个量级。

Conclusion: 同步辐射可作为一种有效的OAM极化机制，用于控制高能加速器中的涡旋电子束，为相关应用提供新的技术手段。

Abstract: While spin polarization from synchrotron radiation is well established, the polarization of orbital angular momentum (OAM) in such radiative processes remains elusive. We study radiation and polarization of relativistic electrons in a uniform magnetic field, focusing on OAM polarization radiation for vortex electrons which carry intrinsic OAM. The results illustrate that transition rates are asymmetric in the low-photon-energy regime, favoring OAM decrease, analogous to the spin-flip asymmetry in the Sokolov-Ternov effect. Under these conditions, synchrotron radiation can polarize the OAM. The characteristic relaxation time and stationary-state OAM distribution are obtained analytically. The polarization of spin about \(\mathcal{P}_{\text{spin}}\) reaches \(92.38\%\), while that of \(\mathcal{P}_{\text{OAM}}\) can even approach almost unity for a large OAM; however, their polarization behaviors are different. For typical storage ring parameters, the OAM polarization time is orders of magnitude shorter than the spin polarization time. Thus, synchrotron radiation offers a mechanism for controlling vortex electron beams which carry OAM for high-energy accelerator applications.

</details>

### [33] [Liquid argon purification and purity monitoring: apparatus and first results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21307)

Method: 采用13升纯净液态氩测试站，配备单次液相纯化柱（single-pass liquid-phase purification column）、双栅格纯度监测器（double-gridded purity monitor）以及慢控制与数据采集系统（slow control and data acquisition system），通过测量电子寿命来评估液氩纯度。

Conclusion: 该测试平台已达到足够低的杂质浓度，可作为韦尔斯利学院LArTPC读出技术基础研究的设施，支持Q-Pix及其他冷电子学系统的研发工作。

Abstract: We report results from a 13-liter purified liquid argon test stand at Wellesley College. The system includes a single-pass liquid-phase purification column, a double-gridded purity monitor to assess the electron lifetime, and a slow control and data acquisition system. Initial measurements demonstrate an O$_2$-equivalent impurity concentration of 0.25 ppb, corresponding to an electron lifetime of 1.2 ms at a drift field of 500 V/cm. This test stand supports ongoing detector R&D on charge and light readout technologies for future large-scale liquid argon time projection chambers, such as Q-Pix and other cold electronics systems, as part of a facility at Wellesley College for fundamental studies of LArTPC readouts.

### [34] [Phenomenological Detector Design and Optimization in Vertically-Integrated Differentiable Full Simulations with Agentic-AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21804)
*Wonyong Chung,Qibin Liu,Liangyu Wu,Julia Gonski*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文首次将AI智能体（AI agents）通过双层优化框架（bilevel optimization framework）应用于高能物理（HEP）探测器的设计与优化，实现了探测器几何、前端数字化（digitization）以及高能重建算法参数的可微全仿真（differentiable full simulations）垂直整合。以双读出分段晶体电磁量能器（dual-readout segmented crystal EM calorimeter）为案例（基线分辨率为 $3\%/\sqrt{E}$），验证了基于大语言模型（LLM）的推理模型无需额外实验背景知识即可自主执行复杂工作流、优化垂直集成参数，并显著降低人力与计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理探测器设计涉及几何结构、前端电子学与重建算法等多层级参数的耦合，传统方法依赖人工逐层调优，效率低下且难以全局统筹。本文旨在探索AI智能体能否在垂直集成（vertically integrated）的可微仿真框架中自动识别关键参数、非线性遍历完整参数空间，从而提升设计效率并降低计算开销。

Method: 构建双层优化框架，将探测器几何、前端数字化参数与高能重建算法参数在可微全仿真中垂直集成；引入基于LLM的AI智能体，在不提供额外实验背景的前提下，使其自主执行复杂工作流并迭代优化参数子集，包括晶体颗粒度（granularity）与长度、ADC位数与采样率、重心聚类半径（center-of-gravity hit-clustering radius）等代表性参数。

Result: LLM推理模型能够有效执行复杂工作流，主动建议通用但相关的改进方向；成功同步优化了所选垂直集成参数子集。AI智能体的集成显著降低了人力和计算资源消耗，并为基于第一性原理（first-principles）的设计选择提供了高效的计算验证途径。但本文未能展现出智能体自主做出物理动机判断（physics-motivated judgment）或洞察飞跃的能力。

Conclusion: 本研究定义了当前高能物理实验设计方法的前沿边界：AI智能体可在垂直集成框架中高效完成参数优化与工作流执行，但尚未实现物理驱动的自主判断飞跃。该工作表明，将智能体整合到前沿研究的复杂工作流中，不仅能大幅降低劳动与计算成本，还可为第一性原理设计选择开辟高效的计算验证路径。

Abstract: We present the first implementation of AI agents into the design and optimization of detectors in high-energy physics experiments via a bilevel optimization framework that vertically integrates detector geometry, front-end digitization, and high-level reconstruction algorithm parameters in differentiable full simulations. Using the example of a dual-readout, segmented crystal EM calorimeter with a baseline resolution of $3\%/\sqrt{E}$, we investigate the capabilities and value propositions of AI agents in the identification and reduction of key detector parameters and in the nonlinear traversal of a given detector design's full parameter space. We find that LLM-based reasoning models today, without being given additional experiment-specific context, are able to effectively execute complex workflows and proactively suggest generic but relevant avenues for further study or improvement. Here, we demonstrate an AI agent's ability to use the workflow to simultaneously optimize a representative subset of vertically integrated detector parameters: crystal granularity and length, number of ADC bits and sampling rate, and center-of-gravity hit-clustering radius. We find that effective integration of agents into the complex workflows of frontier areas of research not only significantly reduces labor and compute, but opens up efficient avenues for computational validation of first-principles design choices. While the ability to make autonomous leaps of physics-motivated judgment or insight is not demonstrated in this work, this study defines the current frontier of experimental design methods in high-energy physics.

</details>

### [35] [Quasi-resonant normal form and quadratic lifespan for 3D gravity-capillary water waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20968)
*Roberto Feola,Riccardo Montalto,Federico Murgante*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了三维重力-毛细水波方程在周期边界条件下小振幅解的长时动力学行为，证明了对于几乎所有表面张力参数值，初始大小为ε的解在ε^{-2}时间尺度上保持小且存在。为解决高维空间中拟线性方程导致的导数损失问题，作者发展了一种结合尖锐频率划分与准共振正规形变换的新分析策略，利用准共振频率集的几何性质和水波系统的哈密顿结构，揭示了危险相互作用项的块对角结构，从而阻止了导数损失机制并避免有害小分母的累积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维水波方程由于拟线性（quasilinear）本质与高维空间中严重的二次和三次小除数相互作用（small-divisor interactions），经典正规形方法（normal form methods）因近共振（near-resonance）的累积而无法阻止导数损失，因此亟需发展新策略来克服这一障碍。

Method: 提出一种尖锐频率划分（sharp frequency partition）与准共振正规形变换（quasi-resonant normal form transformation）相结合的分析策略，该变换仅作用于选定的相互作用尺度。利用微局部分析（microlocal analysis）揭示危险相互作用项的块对角结构（block-diagonal structure），该结构源于准共振频率集的几何性质与水波系统的哈密顿结构（Hamiltonian structure）。

Result: 对于几乎所有表面张力参数值，初始大小为ε的解在ε^{-2}时间尺度上存在并保持小尺度。准共振正规形变换与块对角结构共同作用，使得相关算子保持Sobolev范数（Sobolev norms）而不产生能量增长，从而阻止导数损失机制并避免有害小分母的累积。

Conclusion: 本文发展的新分析策略成功克服了三维重力-毛细水波方程（gravity-capillary water waves equations）中拟线性与高维小除数相互作用带来的导数损失问题，为理解水波系统在长时尺度上的动力学行为提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: We study the long-time dynamics of small-amplitude solutions to the three-dimensional gravity-capillary water waves equations for an inviscid and irrotational fluid with periodic boundary conditions. We prove that, for almost all values of the surface tension parameter, solutions with initial size $\varepsilon$ exist and remain small over time intervals of order $\varepsilon^{-2}$. A major difficulty arises from the loss of derivatives caused by the quasilinear nature of the equations combined with severe quadratic and cubic small-divisor interactions in high space dimensions. Classical normal form methods applied to 3D water waves system typically fail to prevent derivative loss due to the accumulation of near-resonances. To overcome this obstruction, we develop a new analytical strategy that combines a sharp frequency partition with a quasi-resonant normal form transformation acting only on selected interaction scales. Our microlocal analysis reveals that the potentially dangerous interactions terms exhibit a block-diagonal structure, which stems from both the geometric properties of the quasi-resonant frequency sets and the Hamiltonian structure of the water waves system. As a consequence, these operators preserve Sobolev norms and do not produce energy growth. This structural insight, together with the quasi-resonant normal-form transformation, allows us to prevent derivative-loss mechanisms while avoiding the accumulation of harmful small denominators.

</details>


### [36] [Three-dimensional time-periodic problem on the Boltzmann equation with external force](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21339)
*Renjun Duan,Jinkai Ni*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文首次证明了三维全空间下，给定时间周期外力足够小时玻尔兹曼方程（Boltzmann equation）时间周期解的存在性与稳定性，填补了该问题仅在高维（维数≥5）成立的空白，并作为推论给出外力不依赖时间时定常解的存在性与稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维全空间下带时间周期外力的玻尔兹曼方程的时间周期问题自文献[13]首次研究以来一直悬而未决，该文献仅证明了空间维数不低于五维的情形。本文旨在填补这一空白，在更低的物理维度（三维）上给出肯定回答。

Method: 证明基于Serrin方法，通过研究带时间周期外力的柯西问题（Cauchy problem）的整体时间稳定性（global-in-time stability）来建立时间周期解的存在性。外力在函数空间$\mathcal{C}(\mathbb{R};\dot{B}^{-3/2}_{2,\infty}\cap\dot{H}^N)$（$N\geq 4$）中充分小。

Result: 在三维全空间中，当时间周期外力在指定函数空间中足够小时，玻尔兹曼方程存在时间周期解，且该解是稳定的。作为直接推论，当外力与时间无关时，三维玻尔兹曼方程的定常解（stationary solutions）的存在性与稳定性也得以建立。

Conclusion: 本文给出了三维全空间下带小时间周期外力的玻尔兹曼方程时间周期问题的肯定答案，并将结果推广到外力不依赖于时间的定常情形，推进了对该经典方程在物理维度下动力学行为的理解。

Abstract: The time-periodic problem on the Boltzmann equation with a given time-periodic external force in the three-dimensional whole space has remained open since it was first studied in [13] for only spatial dimensions not less than five. The goal of this paper is to give an affirmative answer to this problem provided that the external force is sufficiently small in the function space $\mathcal{C}(\mathbb{R};\dot{B}^{-3/2}_{2,\infty}\cap\dot{H}^N)$ with $N\geq 4$. The proof is based on Serrin's method through studying the global-in-time stability of the Cauchy problem with time-periodic external forces. As a direct consequence, the result also yields the existence and stability of stationary solutions to the physically realistic three-dimensional Boltzmann equation when the external force is time-independent.

</details>

### [37] [Orthosymplectic quantum groups revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21785)
*Kyungtak Hong,Alexander Tsymbaliuk*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文针对任意奇偶序列，提出了扩展正交辛量子超群（extended orthosymplectic quantum supergroups）的RLL实现，该实现与广义双代数（generalized doubles）的内部结构相容，并通过2-上循环扭变（2-cocycle twists）联系了不同符号约定，此外还建立了约化R矩阵（reduced R-matrix）在RLL实现中的分解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在为扩展正交辛量子超群提供一种统一的RLL实现方案，使其能够适用于任意奇偶序列，并与前期工作中获得的R矩阵（R-matrices）结果相衔接。

Method: 基于前期工作（arxiv:2408.16720）中求得的R矩阵，构建RLL实现，并通过2-上循环扭变建立不同符号约定之间的联系。同时，利用广义双代数的内部结构确保同构的相容性。

Result: 成功给出了任意奇偶序列下扩展正交辛量子超群的RLL实现，证明了该同构与广义双代数结构相容，揭示了不同符号约定之间的等价关系，并实现了约化R矩阵在RLL框架下的分解。

Conclusion: 该RLL实现为扩展正交辛量子超群提供了统一且结构相容的代数框架，为进一步研究相关量子超群及其表示理论奠定了基础。

Abstract: We present the RLL-realization of extended orthosymplectic quantum supergroups for any parity sequence, with R-matrices evaluated in the earlier work arxiv:2408.16720. Our isomorphism is compatible with the internal structure of generalized doubles. We also relate different sign conventions through 2-cocycle twists. Furthermore, we establish a factorization of the reduced R-matrix within the RLL-realization.

</details>
