### [38] [Interpretable Analytic Formulae for GWTC-4 Binary Black Hole Population Properties via Symbolic Regression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20941)
*Chayan Chatterjee*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究将符号回归（symbolic regression）应用于GWTC-4目录的后验推断产物，发现了描述双黑洞（binary black hole, BBH）群体四个关键关系的紧凑闭式解析表达式，包括红移依赖的并合率、质量比与有效自旋的关联、有效自旋分布的红移演化以及主质量峰的条件质量比分布。该框架成功压缩刚性与高柔性模型，并通过解析梯度诊断揭示了自旋-质量关联主要由后验宽度展宽而非均值偏移驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）分析揭示了双黑洞（BBH）群体中复杂的结构，包括主质量谱的显著特征和非平凡的自旋-质量关联（spin-mass correlations），但用于捕捉这些特征的现象学模型（phenomenological models）缺乏解析透明性，难以将稳健的物理定律与建模伪影区分开来。

Method: 采用符号回归（symbolic regression）对GWTC-4目录的后验推断产品进行分析，寻找描述四个关键群体关系的紧凑闭式解析表达式：并合率随红移的演化、有效自旋分布对质量比的依赖、有效自旋分布的红移演化，以及对应10太阳质量和35太阳质量主质量峰的条件质量比分布。

Result: 该框架成功将刚性和高柔性模型压缩为可微分现象学定律，动态恢复了低红移并合率斜率而无需预设幂律形式。符号回归提供的精确解析导数表明，质量比-有效自旋和红移-有效自旋关联主要由后验宽度的展宽（broadening of posterior widths）而非均值偏移驱动。此外，识别出对应10太阳质量和35太阳质量主质量峰的条件质量比分布具有性质不同的函数形式。

Conclusion: 所获得的闭式表达式实现了精确的解析梯度诊断和紧凑的替代性总结，特别适用于本身无法以低维解析形式获得的柔性数值后验。这些表达式还可促进并合率预测、形成通道比较和随机背景估计等下游计算的快速执行。

Abstract: Recent LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) analyses have revealed complex structure in the binary black hole (BBH) population, including distinct features in the primary mass spectrum and nontrivial spin-mass correlations. However, the phenomenological models used to capture these features often lack analytic transparency, making it difficult to isolate robust physical laws from modeling artifacts. To address this, symbolic regression is applied to the posterior inference products of the GWTC-4 catalog, discovering compact, closed-form analytic expressions for four key population relationships: (i) the merger-rate evolution with redshift; (ii) the mass-ratio dependence of the effective-spin distribution; (iii) the redshift evolution of the effective-spin distribution; and (iv) the conditional mass-ratio distributions associated with the 10 solar mass and 35 solar mass primary mass peaks. This framework successfully compresses both rigid and highly flexible models into differentiable phenomenological laws, dynamically recovering a consistent low-redshift merger-rate slope without assuming an a priori power-law form. The exact analytic derivatives provided by symbolic regression show that the mass ratio--effective spin and redshift--effective spin correlations are robustly driven by broadening of the posterior widths rather than shifts in the mean. Furthermore, qualitatively distinct functional forms for the mass-ratio distributions conditioned on the 10 solar mass and 35 solar mass primary mass peaks are identified. These closed-form expressions enable exact analytic gradient diagnostics and compact surrogate summaries, particularly for flexible numerical posteriors that are not otherwise available in low-dimensional analytic form. They also facilitate rapid downstream calculations for rate forecasting, formation channel comparison, and stochastic background estimation.

</details>


### [39] [Relativistic effects in k-essence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20989)
*Didam Duniya,Isaac Opio,Bishop Mongwane,Hassan Abdalla*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文研究了冷暗物质和k-本质（k-essence）主导的晚期宇宙中，相对论效应对线性和角向星系功率谱（galaxy power spectra）的影响。在三种k-essence模型（dilaton、tachyon、DBI）中，傅里叶空间（Fourier space）的相对论修正对k-essence微观物理不敏感，但在角功率谱（angular power spectrum）中相对论效应显著放大，对聚类型k-essence具有更好的区分能力，其中tachyon模型表现出最清晰的偏离特征。忽略相对论修正可能导致对k-essence偏离宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）的系统性误估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相对论效应（relativistic effects）对暗能量的细微变化非常敏感，且在大尺度和高红移（high redshift）区域会显著增长，正好处于即将开展的巡天项目的能力范围内。作者希望探究这些效应能否有效区分不同k-essence模型与标准宇宙学模型（concordance model）之间的差异。

Method: 采用冷暗物质和k-essence主导的晚期宇宙框架，选取三种核心模型（dilaton、tachyon、DBI标量场），通过强制设定相同的当前宇宙学参数（present-day cosmological parameters），在线性功率谱和角功率谱中考察相对论效应，对比k-essence模型与标准模型的预言差异。

Result: 相对论修正（relativistic corrections）在大尺度上占主导并随红移增长，但在傅里叶空间中对k-essence微观物理不敏感，模型间存在强简并。而角功率谱中相对论效应显著放大，对聚类型k-essence（clustering k-essence）敏感度更高，tachyon模型在多极矩（multipoles）和红移上展现出最清晰的偏离特征，尤其在Doppler势和速度-引力势（velocity and gravitational potentials）贡献部分。

Conclusion: 忽略相对论修正会导致对k-essence偏离宇宙学常数的系统性误估；相对论角功率谱是探测超大尺度物理更一致且稳健的探针。下一代针对视界尺度（horizon-scale）模式的巡天项目必须采用完整的相对论建模，才能准确捕捉非标准暗能量的信号。

Abstract: Relativistic effects are sensitive to subtle changes in dark energy. These effects grow on very large scales and at high redshifts, which will be the reach of upcoming surveys. We investigate these effects in both the linear and the angular galaxy power spectra in a late-time universe dominated by cold dark matter and k-essence, focusing on three core models (dilaton, tachyon, and DBI scalar fields) and contrasting their predictions with those of the concordance model. By enforcing identical present-day cosmological parameters, we isolate the imprints of k-essence dynamics and perturbations on very large scales. We found that relativistic corrections dominate on very large scales and grow with redshift, but are largely insensitive to k-essence microphysics in Fourier space, leading to strong degeneracies among the models. However, in the angular power spectrum, where line-of-sight integrals are naturally included, relativistic effects are significantly amplified, yielding better sensitivity to clustering k-essence. In particular, the tachyon exhibits clear deviations across multipoles and redshifts, with distinct imprints in the Doppler and the combined (velocity and gravitational) potentials contributions. Furthermore, our results show that neglecting relativistic corrections can lead to systematic misestimation of deviations of k-essence from the cosmological constant. Our results show the relativistic angular galaxy power spectrum as a more consistent and robust probe of ultra-large-scale physics. These findings underscore the need for full relativistic modelling in next-generation surveys that are targeting horizon-scale modes, where the imprint of non-standard dark energy is most pronounced.

</details>


### [40] [Cosmological Gravitational Waves from Ultralight Vector Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21080)
*Tomás Esteban Ferreira Chase,Diana López Nacir*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文计算了超轻矢量（自旋-1）暗物质场在演化过程中产生的宇宙引力波丰度，推导了在Bianchi I几何背景下标量、矢量与张量扰动之间的混合效应，并通过修改版CLASS得到了引力波的当代频谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超轻矢量暗物质场的均匀背景会破坏空间各向同性，导致标量、矢量和张量扰动之间产生混合，因此需要研究这种混合是否会成为随机引力波背景（stochastic GW background）的来源。

Method: 采用Bianchi I几何描述各向异性背景，推导该背景下的扰动方程；展示标量扰动如何通过混合机制充当张量模式的源；将引力波产生与宇宙学演化程序集成到修改版CLASS（Cosmic Linear Anisotropy Solving System）中实现数值计算。

Result: 标量扰动与张量模式之间的混合确实能够产生随机引力波背景；通过修改版CLASS的数值模拟，得到了该引力波在当代的频谱（present-day spectrum）。

Conclusion: 超轻矢量暗物质场在宇宙演化过程中可产生可观测的引力波信号，其机制源于各向异性背景下的扰动混合效应。

Abstract: We compute the abundance of cosmological gravitational waves produced during the evolution of an ultralight vector (spin-1) dark matter field. A homogeneous background vector field breaks spatial isotropy, requiring a Bianchi I geometry and inducing a mixing between the scalar, vector, and tensor perturbation sectors. We derive the perturbation equations in this background and show that, as a consequence of this mixing, scalar perturbations act as a source of tensor modes, generating a stochastic GW background. The production and cosmological evolution of these gravitational waves are implemented in a modified version of CLASS, from which we obtain the present-day spectrum.

</details>


### [41] [Impact of the Infrared Cutoff on Structure Formation in Tsallis Holographic Dark Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21490)
*Biswajit Das*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文检验了Tsallis全息暗能量（THDE）模型在宇宙结构形成中的可行性，发现结构增长历史对红外截断（IR cutoff）的选择高度敏感：基于未来事件视界的模型能与观测数据吻合，甚至在某些参数下优于ΛCDM模型；而基于粒子视界的模型则无法再现观测到的结构增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验Tsallis全息暗能量（THDE）模型在宇宙结构形成中的可行性，特别是红外截断（IR cutoff）选择对结构增长的影响，以判断该模型是否符合观测数据。

Method: 考虑两种常用红外截断——粒子视界（particle horizon）与未来事件视界（future event horizon），分析线性物质扰动（linear matter perturbations）的演化，计算增长因子（growth factor）、增长速率（growth rate）以及可观测的fσ₈(z)，并与红移空间畸变（redshift-space distortion）测量数据进行比较。

Result: 基于未来事件视界的THDE模型与观测数据一致，在合适的Tsallis参数δ取值下，其拟合结果可与ΛCDM模型相当甚至略优；基于粒子视界的模型则普遍无法再现观测到的结构增长。

Conclusion: THDE模型的可行性关键取决于红外截断的选择；结构形成是对广义全息暗能量（generalized holographic dark energy）场景的严格检验。

Abstract: We investigate the viability of Tsallis holographic dark energy (THDE) models, focusing on the role of the infrared (IR) cutoff in the growth of cosmic structures. Considering two commonly used choices of the cutoff, the particle horizon and the future event horizon, we analyze the evolution of linear matter perturbations and compute the growth factor, growth rate, and the observable $fσ_8(z)$. These predictions are compared with observational data from redshift-space distortion measurements. We find that the growth history is highly sensitive to the choice of IR cutoff. Models based on the future event horizon are consistent with observational data and can provide a fit comparable to, or slightly better than, the $Λ$CDM model for suitable values of the Tsallis parameter $δ$. In contrast, models constructed using the particle horizon generally fail to reproduce the observed growth of structure. These results demonstrate that the viability of THDE models depends crucially on the choice of IR cutoff and highlight the importance of structure formation as a stringent test of generalized holographic dark energy scenarios.

</details>


### [42] [Impact of Primordial Black Hole population on 21 cm observables at high redshift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21666)
*Atrideb Chatterjee,Barun Maity,Koushiki*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文扩展了光子守恒再电离框架SCRIPT，纳入原初黑洞（PBH）作为早期活动星系核（AGN）种子，研究其对21厘米信号（21-cm signal）的影响。结果表明，PBH的X射线加热会显著削弱全球21厘米信号的深度并压低宇宙黎明期间的功率谱振幅，且PBH质量函数的选择对信号预测有重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统高红移21厘米信号建模未考虑活动星系核（AGN）的影响，但JWST在红移z~10处发现了多个AGN，因此亟需将这些早期AGN纳入预测。本文假设这些AGN由原初黑洞（PBH）播种，系统研究其对21厘米信号的影响。

Method: 采用半数值（semi-numerical）模型方法，扩展了显式光子守恒（explicitly photon-conserving）再电离框架SCRIPT，加入宇宙黎明（cosmic dawn）物理和PBH贡献；在红移范围z~30–5内，自洽计算21厘米线的全局信号（global signal）和功率谱（power spectrum），并分析不同PBH质量函数（mass function）的影响。

Result: PBH的X射线加热使全球21厘米信号的深度显著变浅；宇宙黎明期间预期的功率谱振幅被压低；不同PBH质量函数对21厘米信号的形状产生显著不同影响，可导致差异很大的预测结果。

Conclusion: 早期AGN（由PBH种子产生）对21厘米信号有不可忽略的调制作用，将其纳入建模是必要的；PBH质量函数的选择是影响信号预测的关键因素。

Abstract: The 21-cm signal, one of the most promising probes of the high-redshift Universe, has traditionally been modelled without accounting for the effects of active galactic nuclei (AGN) in the pre-JWST era, primarily due to the lack of observational evidence for AGNs at z > 6. However, following the discovery of several AGNs at redshifts as high as z ~ 10 by JWST, it has become imperative to incorporate the impact of these early AGNs when predicting the 21-cm signal. Supposing that these AGNs are seeded by primordial black holes (PBHs), we study their impact with a semi-numerical model setup. Specifically, we extended the explicitly photon-conserving reionization framework, SCRIPT, including essential cosmic dawn physics and PBH contributions. This enables us to compute both the global signal and the power spectrum of the 21-cm line over the redshift range z ~ 30 - 5 within a self-consistent framework. Building on this setup, we then investigate the impact of different PBH mass functions (obeying current observational constraints) on the resulting signal. The X-ray heating from PBHs can substantially make the depth of the global 21-cm signal shallower and suppress the expected power amplitude during cosmic dawn. We also find that the choice of mass function plays a crucial role in shaping the 21-cm signal, and can, in fact, lead to significantly different predictions.

</details>


### [43] [Saturation Mechanisms in the Interacting Dark Sector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21671)
*Andronikos Paliathanasis,Kevin J. Duffy*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类由稀疏度尺度（sparseness scale）参数调制的相互作用暗区（interacting dark sector）唯象宇宙学模型，以描述晚期宇宙的加速膨胀。通过引入受生态学和生物学饱和机制启发的半饱和常数来约束暗物质与暗能量之间的能量交换，并考察了三种非线性相互作用模型。利用哈勃归一化方法进行相空间分析，结合超新星、宇宙计时器、重子声学振荡（BAO）DESI DR2数据以及红移空间畸变等观测数据进行贝叶斯分析。结果表明，对于其中两个模型，稀疏度参数为零的情形在超过95%置信区间上被排除，为暗区相互作用中非零稀疏度尺度提供了观测支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有暗区相互作用模型通常缺乏对相互作用强度的天然饱和机制，可能允许非物理行为（如幽灵穿越（phantom crossing））。本文借鉴生态学与生物学中的饱和机制，提出以稀疏度尺度（sparseness scale）调制暗物质（dark matter）与暗能量（dark energy）之间的相互作用，从而更自然地描述晚期宇宙加速膨胀。

Method: (1) 受生态学和生物学中成熟的饱和机制启发，将稀疏度尺度（sparseness scale）作为半饱和常数引入暗区相互作用，以约束能量交换并控制动力学行为。(2) 提出三种非线性相互作用模型，其中两种在稀疏度参数为零时还原为线性相互作用情形。(3) 采用哈勃归一化方法对宇宙学场方程进行相空间分析，确定不动点及其稳定性，重建场方程的渐近行为。(4) 利用超新星（Supernovae）星表、宇宙计时器（cosmic chronometers）、DESI DR2重子声学振荡（BAO）测量数据，以及通过 $f$ 和 $f\sigma_8$ 观测量的红移空间畸变测量数据，对模型进行贝叶斯分析。

Result: 贝叶斯分析表明，在三个模型中，有两个模型的稀疏度参数为零的情形在超过95%置信区间上被排除，这为暗区相互作用中存在非零稀疏度尺度提供了观测支持。

Conclusion: 引入稀疏度尺度能够有效控制暗区相互作用的动力学行为并防止幽灵穿越。观测数据倾向于支持非零的稀疏度参数，表明暗区相互作用中确实存在一种饱和机制，这一机制在地球生物学与宇宙学之间建立了有趣的跨学科联系。

Abstract: We introduce a family of phenomenological cosmological models featuring an interacting dark sector modulated by a sparseness scale parameter, in order to describe the late-time accelerated expansion of the universe. The sparseness scale, inspired by well-established saturation mechanisms in ecology and biology, is introduced in the interaction as a half-saturation constant that bounds the energy exchange between dark matter and dark energy, controls the dynamical behaviour of the physical variables and can prevent the phantom crossing. We consider three nonlinear interacting models, where two of them recover the linear interacting scenarios when the sparsity parameter vanishes. We examine the phase-space of the cosmological field equations by using the Hubble normalization approach. We determine the stationary points and their stability properties in order to reconstruct the asymptotics behaviour of the field equations. Such an analysis allows us to demonstrate the effects of the sparseness scale on the background dynamics. We test the interacting models with observational data. Specifically, we employ Supernovae catalogues, cosmic chronometers, Baryon Acoustic Oscillation measurements from DESI DR2, and redshift-space distortion measurements of the growth of large-scale structure through the $f$ and $fσ_8$ observables. The Bayesian analysis suggests that, for two of the three models, a vanishing sparsity parameter is disfavoured at more than the 95\% confidence interval, providing observational support for a nonzero sparseness scale in the dark sector interaction.

</details>

# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [44] [A rigorous quasipolynomial-time classical algorithm for SYK thermal expectations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21089)
*Alexander Zlokapa*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev（SYK）模型中吉布斯态（Gibbs states）的局域可观测量估计问题，在足够高的恒定温度下，提出并严格证明了一种拟多项式时间（quasipolynomial-time）的经典算法，该算法引入了一种新的Wick配对团簇展开（Wick-pair cluster expansion）方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子模拟中，估计吉布斯态的局域可观测量是一个核心问题。尽管在渐进低温下该问题是BQP完全的（BQP-complete），但在恒定温度下是否存在量子优势（quantum advantage）仍是一个开放问题。SYK模型因其吉布斯态具有多项式量子电路复杂度（polynomial quantum circuit complexity）且不被高斯态（Gaussian states）描述，成为研究这一问题的自然候选，但严格分析极为困难。

Method: 作者引入了一种新的Wick配对团簇展开方法，用于克服现有技术（如随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）、团簇展开（cluster expansions）、量子路径积分（quantum path integral）及复制技巧（replica trick）的严格形式化）在SYK模型分析中遇到的困难，从而构建了可严格证明的经典算法。

Result: 在足够高的恒定温度下，给出了一个严格证明的拟多项式时间经典算法，能够估计SYK模型的局域热期望值（local thermal expectations）。

Conclusion: 该结果表明，在足够高的恒定温度下，SYK模型的局域可观测量估计不存在量子优势；所提出的Wick配对团簇展开方法有望广泛应用于无序量子多体系统（disordered quantum many-body systems）的严格分析。

Abstract: Estimating local observables in Gibbs states is a central problem in quantum simulation. While this task is BQP-complete at asymptotically low temperatures, the possibility of quantum advantage at constant temperature remains open. The Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) model is a natural candidate: at any constant temperature, its Gibbs states have polynomial quantum circuit complexity and are not described by Gaussian states. Rigorous analyses of the SYK model are difficult due to the failure of known techniques using random matrix theory, cluster expansions, and rigorous formulations of the quantum path integral and replica trick. Despite this, we give a rigorous proof of a quasipolynomial-time classical algorithm that estimates SYK local thermal expectations at sufficiently high constant temperature. Our result introduces a new Wick-pair cluster expansion that we expect to be broadly useful for disordered quantum many-body systems.

</details>


### [45] [Variance Geometry of Exact Pauli-Detecting Codes: Continuous Landscapes Beyond Stabilizers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21800)
*Arunaday Gupta,Baisong Sun,Xi He,Bei Zeng*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过高阶数值范围（higher-rank numerical ranges）的几何视角，证明精确检测Pauli错误的量子纠错码通常构成连续连通族（connected continuous families），而非离散的解区域。稳定子码（stabilizer codes）仅占据这些连续景观中可忽略的离散点集，揭示了一类广泛未被探索的严格非可加性精确码（genuinely nonadditive exact codes）。这些码族的联合Pauli方差轮廓（joint Pauli variance profile）可由一个标量参数 λ* 完整刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前精确量子纠错码（exact quantum codes）的研究多为离散的代数构造（如稳定子码、置换不变码等），但高阶数值范围（rank ≥ 2）的几何结构尚未被充分理解。本文旨在探索这些码是否存在连续的参数化族，并揭示稳定子码与非可加性码之间的几何关系。

Method: 基于Knill-Laflamme条件导出的标量参数 λ*（即最大混合态上Pauli期望值特征向量的欧几里得范数），作者分析了高阶算子压缩（higher-rank operator compressions）的几何结构。通过Stiefel流形优化（Stiefel-manifold optimization）和对称性适配参数化（symmetry-adapted parameterizations），对小系统采用本征值交错（eigenvalue interlacing）和对称性扇区分解（symmetry-sector decompositions）进行解析处理，对大系统进行数值处理。

Result: 精确Pauli纠错码在参数空间中形成连通连续族，而非离散区域。稳定子码仅占据这些连续景观中可数的测度零（measure-zero）子集。在所有分析的无限制和对称性兼容情形下，可达到的 λ*-谱（attainable λ*-spectrum）在非空时形成单一闭区间（single closed interval），尽管一般性证明仍未给出。

Conclusion: 本文将稳定子码、对称性码和非可加性码族统一纳入高阶方差框架（higher-rank variance framework），提出了精确量子纠错码景观的连续几何视角，揭示存在大量未被探索的非可加性精确码。

Abstract: Exact quantum codes detecting a prescribed set of Pauli errors are approached through algebraic constructions--stabilizer, codeword-stabilized, permutation-invariant, topological, and related families. Geometrically, exact Pauli detection is governed by joint higher-rank numerical ranges of these Pauli operators, whose structure for rank $\geq 2$ is largely uncharted. From this viewpoint, we show that such codes often form connected continuous families rather than collections of disjoint solution regions. These families are characterized by a single scalar derived from the Knill-Laflamme conditions: denoted $λ^*$, it is the Euclidean norm of the signature vector of Pauli expectation values on the maximally mixed code state, and provides a one-parameter summary of the code's joint Pauli variance profile. Within these continuous landscapes, stabilizer codes occupy only discrete, measure-zero subsets of the attainable $λ^*$-spectrum, exposing a largely unexplored continuum of genuinely nonadditive exact codes. We establish this picture by analyzing the geometry of higher-rank operator compressions, and extend it to symmetry-restricted settings where cyclic and permutation symmetries are imposed on both the error model and the code projector. Small-system cases reveal interval, singleton, and empty regimes through eigenvalue interlacing and symmetry-sector decompositions; larger systems are treated numerically via Stiefel-manifold optimization and symmetry-adapted parameterizations. In every unrestricted and symmetry-compatible case analyzed, the attainable $λ^*$-spectrum forms a single closed interval whenever nonempty--although a general proof remains open. These results place stabilizer, symmetric, and nonadditive code families within a unified higher-rank variance framework, suggesting a continuous geometric perspective on the landscape of exact quantum codes.

### [46] [Algorithmic Locality via Provable Convergence in Quantum Tensor Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21919)
*Siddhant Midha,Yifan F. Zhang,Daniel Malz,Dmitry A. Abanin,Sarang Gopalakrishnan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文为强单射张量网络上的置信传播算法建立了首个端到端理论，证明其可在多项式时间内高效计算物理量，并揭示了“算法局域性”现象：局部扰动的影响随距离快速衰减，使得局部更新与可观测量的局域近似成为可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将置信传播（belief propagation）框架系统应用于张量网络（tensor networks）计算，为广泛使用的数值实践提供严格的理论保证，弥合算法实践经验与可证明性能之间的差距。

Method: 针对满足强单射性（strong injectivity）的一类投影纠缠对态（projected entangled pair states, PEPS），建立了张量网络置信传播的端到端理论；结合聚类修正（cluster-corrected）的BP算法与聚类展开（cluster expansion）技术进行分析。

Result: 当单射性参数超过某一常数阈值时，BP不动点可高效求得；聚类修正BP算法能在多项式时间（poly(N)）内以1/poly(N)的误差计算N量子比特系统的物理量；发现了“算法局域性”（algorithmic locality）现象，即局部扰动对BP不动点的影响随距离快速衰减，局部更新仅需局部重计算；局域期望值可通过局域数据以可控精度近似。

Conclusion: 该研究为张量网络置信传播在一大类多体态（many-body states）上的有效性提供了首个严格保证，弥合了广泛数值实践与可证明算法性能之间的理论鸿沟。

Abstract: Belief propagation has recently emerged as a powerful framework for evaluating tensor networks in higher dimensions, combining computational efficiency with provable analytical guarantees. In this work, we develop the first end-to-end theory of tensor network belief propagation for a class of projected entangled pair states satisfying \emph{strong injectivity}. We show that when the injectivity parameter exceeds a constant threshold, BP fixed points can be found efficiently, and a cluster-corrected BP algorithm computes physical quantities to $1/\mathrm{poly}(N)$ error in $\mathrm{poly}(N)$ time for an $N$ qubit system. We identify a striking phenomenon we term \emph{algorithmic locality}: local perturbations of the tensor network affect the BP fixed point with an influence decaying rapidly with distance. As a result, updates to the fixed point after a local perturbation can be carried out using only local recomputation. Moreover, through the cluster expansion, this locality extends to observables, implying that local expectation values can be approximated from local data with controlled accuracy. Our results provide the first rigorous guarantee for the effectiveness of tensor-network belief propagation on a wide class of many-body states, bridging a gap between widely used numerical practice and provable algorithmic performance.

### [47] [Ghost Degrees of Freedom Without Quantum Runaway: Exact Moment Bounds from an Operator Conservation Law](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21348)
*Christopher Ewasiuk,Stefano Profumo*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明了一个与鬼自由度（ghost degree of freedom）耦合的谐振子体系存在精确的量子守恒律，该守恒律给出了均方位相空间半径（mean squared phase-space radius）的严格上界，从而表明鬼量子不稳定性（ghost quantum instability）并非错误符号动能项的必然结果，而是取决于相互作用结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 鬼自由度通常出现在有效场论（effective field theory）中，因其动能项符号为负，传统上被认为会导致量子不稳定性（quantum instability）。然而，这种不稳定性是否必然发生，仍缺乏严格的量子层面理解。

Method: 通过正则对易关系（canonical commutation relations）和莱布尼茨法则（Leibniz rule）推导精确的量子守恒律；无需约束势（confining potential）、谱假设（spectral assumptions）或微扰展开（perturbative expansion）；并采用海森堡绘景（Heisenberg picture）、薛定谔绘景（Schrödinger picture）和福克空间对角化（Fock-space diagonalization）三种独立数值框架进行验证。

Result: 所研究的相互作用是有界且在大分离下消失的，这保证了体系在二阶矩意义下的量子稳定性；数值结果确认波包被限制在解析上界以下、能谱为实数，且泊松能级统计（Poisson level statistics）与可积结构（integrable structure）一致。

Conclusion: 鬼量子不稳定性并非错误符号动能项的必然后果，而是关键地取决于相互作用结构；对于该论文所研究的相互作用类别，谱离散性和基态存在性问题仍需进一步研究。

Abstract: We prove an exact quantum conservation law for a harmonic oscillator coupled to a ghost degree of freedom: a second classical conserved quantity lifts to a quantum operator that commutes with the Hamiltonian with no hbar corrections, yielding a rigorous, state-independent upper bound on the mean squared phase-space radius for all time and every quantum state with finite initial second moments. The proof uses only canonical commutation relations and the Leibniz rule; it requires no confining potential, no spectral assumptions, and no perturbative expansion. The interaction studied here is bounded and vanishes at large separations, the generic situation in effective field theory, yet this suffices to guarantee quantum stability in the sense of bounded second moments. Three independent numerical frameworks (Heisenberg picture, Schrodinger picture, and Fock-space diagonalization) confirm wavepacket confinement below the analytic bound, a real energy spectrum, and Poisson level statistics numerically consistent with an integrable structure. The absence of a confining potential means the proof is silent on spectral discreteness and the existence of a ground state; those questions, addressed for polynomial confining interactions in concurrent work, remain open for the interaction class studied here and represent the sharpest targets for future work. Ghost quantum instability is therefore not an inevitable consequence of a wrong-sign kinetic term but depends critically on the interaction structure.

Abstract: We explore the application of the Variational Quantum Eigensolver (VQE) to investigate the ground state properties, particularly the entanglement entropy, of the Transverse Field Ising Model (TFIM) in one, two, and three dimensions, considering systems of up to 27 spins. By benchmarking VQE results against exact diagonalization and analyzing the entanglement properties across different system sizes and geometries, we assess the algorithm's effectiveness in capturing critical phenomena. Using results of TFIM, we also investigate how VQE's expressivity and optimization influence the simulation of highly entangled quantum states. We employ different ansätze: the hardware-efficient EfficientSU2 from Qiskit, the physics-inspired Hamiltonian Variational ansätz (HVA) and HVA with symmetry breaking, and benchmark their performance using energy variance, entanglement entropy, spin correlations, and magnetization. ### [49] [Multidimensional semiclassical single- and double-quantum spectroscopy of anharmonic molecular polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21158)
*Michael Reitz,Harsh Bhakta,Wei Xiong,Joel Yuen-Zhou*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 基于大N极限（large-𝒩 limit）下的半经典演化方法，提出一种高效计算非谐分子极化激元（anharmonic molecular polaritons）的相位分辨多维光谱（phase-resolved multidimensional spectra）的通用框架，并通过相位循环（phase cycling）技术实现单、双量子极化激元光谱的透明构建，成功解释了极化激元漂白效应（polariton bleach effect）等实验现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非谐分子极化激元的多维光谱计算在理论建模上存在困难，特别是如何高效地解析相位分辨信息。此外，实验中观察到的极化激元漂白效应等关键现象长期缺乏理论解释，亟需一种兼具计算简洁性与物理透明度的通用建模方法。

Method: 采用大N极限下的半经典演化（semiclassical evolution），将分子哈密顿量（molecular Hamiltonian）与腔场（cavity field）耦合处理，并从输入场的振幅和相位两方面系统展开响应，利用相位循环作为斜脉冲相位匹配（phase matching）的类比，在 Liouville 空间中隔离出贡献的非线性路径（nonlinear pathways）。

Result: 成功构建了二维单量子（single-quantum）和双量子（double-quantum）极化激元光谱，并通过与实验测量的单量子光谱直接对比验证方法的有效性，为短等待时间下的极化激元漂白效应提供了理论解释；进一步展示了双量子相干光谱（double-quantum coherence spectroscopy）如何直接探测双激发流形（double-excitation manifold）中各类非谐性的印记。

Conclusion: 该方法建立了一个实用且强大的建模与解释框架，适用于强耦合光-物质平台（strongly coupled light-matter platforms）的非线性光谱实验，并为腔增强分子平台（cavity-enhanced molecular platforms）的设计提供理论指导。

Abstract: We present a general and efficient approach to compute phase-resolved multidimensional spectra of anharmonic molecular polaritons, based on a semiclassical evolution of the molecular Hamiltonian and cavity field in the large-$\mathcal{N}$ limit of many molecules coupled to a confined photonic mode. By systematically expanding the response in both amplitudes and phases of the input fields, our method enables a transparent and computationally simple construction of phase-cycled two-dimensional single- and double-quantum polariton spectra from the underlying nonlinear signal components. Here, phase cycling acts as an analogue of phase matching with oblique pulses, allowing for the isolation of the contributing nonlinear pathways in Liouville space. We specialize to vibrational polaritons and benchmark the method through direct comparison with experimentally measured single-quantum spectra, providing an explanation for the longstanding puzzle of the polariton bleach effect observed at short waiting times. Further, we show how the imprint of various types of anharmonicities on the double-excitation manifold can be directly probed and analyzed through double-quantum coherence spectroscopy. Taken together, our results establish a practical and powerful framework for the modeling and interpretation of nonlinear spectroscopic experiments on strongly coupled light-matter platforms and for guiding the design of cavity-enhanced molecular platforms.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用倾斜林德布拉德方法研究量子跳跃的全计数统计（full counting statistics）；结合团簇平均场和累积量展开技术，分别捕捉跳跃相关性的短程和长程结构；同时分析探测事件的等待时间分布（waiting-time distributions）。

Result: 量子跳跃相关性显示出底层相的清晰特征，并在相变过程中展现出不同的动力学特征。

Conclusion: 轨迹分辨可观测量（trajectory-resolved observables）可作为开放量子多体系统中集体行为的探针；长程相互作用在塑造非平衡动力学中具有重要作用。

Abstract: We characterize nonequilibrium phases in long-range dissipative spin systems through the statistical properties of quantum jump trajectories. While the average dynamics governed by the Lindblad master equation provides access to steady-state expectation values of order parameters, the quantum trajectory framework reveals features encoded in the spatial and temporal correlations of detection events. Focusing on a model exhibiting a paramagnetic-to-ferromagnetic phase transition, we investigate the full counting statistics of quantum jumps using a tilted Lindbladian approach. We combine this with cluster mean-field and cumulant expansion techniques, which allow us to capture, respectively, the short- and long-range structure of jump correlations. In addition, we study the waiting-time distributions of detection events. We show that quantum jump correlations display clear signatures of the underlying phases and reveal distinct dynamical features across the transition. Our results highlight the potential of trajectory-resolved observables as probes of collective behavior in open quantum many-body systems and provide new insights into the role of long-range interactions in shaping nonequilibrium dynamics.

### [51] [Generalized stochastic spin-wave theory for open quantum spin systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21574)
*Zejian Li,Anna Delmonte,Rosario Fazio*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 提出一个半经典（semiclassical）框架，通过推广自旋波近似（generalized spin-wave approximations）来求解驱动-耗散自旋系统中的开放量子动力学（open quantum dynamics），并在二维晶格上的变程驱动-耗散Ising模型中展示了其适用范围与丰富的临界行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的自旋波理论在处理短程相互作用和局域量子跳跃时受限，难以有效模拟大规模相互作用自旋系统的开放量子动力学。

Method: 提出半经典框架，采用推广的自旋波近似来描述从主方程（master equation）解开（unravelled）的量子轨迹（quantum trajectories），同时适用于态扩散（state-diffusion）和量子跳跃（quantum-jump）两类轨迹动力学。

Result: 在耗散沿驱动轴方向时，发现连续相变破坏$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称性，且相互作用范围从全连接到最近邻的调谐会深刻改变临界性的普适类（universality class）；在耗散沿相互作用轴方向时，观察到一级相变（first-order transition）。

Conclusion: 该框架为自旋系统中非平衡动力学和多体相的高效半经典描述提供了强大的工具箱。

Abstract: We propose a semiclassical framework for solving open quantum dynamics in driven-dissipative spin systems. Our method consists of generalized spin-wave approximations tailored to describing quantum trajectories unravelled from the master equation, and generically applies to regimes beyond the reach of conventional spin-wave theories, including short-range interactions and local quantum jumps, enabling the efficient simulation of large-scale interacting spins. We illustrate the versatility of our framework by studying a variable-range driven-dissipative Ising model on a 2D lattice. When the dissipation acts along the drive axis, we find a continuous phase transition breaking the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry, and demonstrate that the interaction range, when tuned from fully-connected to nearest-neighbour, profoundly alters the universality class of the criticality. With the dissipation along the interaction axis, we show the emergence of a first-order transition. Demonstrated with both state-diffusion and quantum-jump types of trajectory dynamics, our framework provides a powerful toolbox for the efficient semiclassical description of non-equilibrium dynamics and many-body phases in spin systems.

### [52] [Entanglement of two optical emitters mediated by a terahertz channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21723)
*Yanis Le Fur,Diego Martín-Cano,Carlos Sánchez Muñoz*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出并实验演示了一种通过太赫兹（THz）光子介导产生极性量子发射体之间稳态纠缠的方案。利用强可见光驱动产生Rabi劈裂的缀饰本征态，其能级差可光学调谐至THz波段；结合集体耗散与驱动机制，在实验可行参数下实现了高并发度（C>0.9）的稳态纠缠，且全部操作与量子态层析均通过光学手段完成，构建了可见光-THz混合量子接口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 太赫兹（THz）波段量子技术亟需可寻址量子比特与THz量子信道之间的相干接口（coherent interface），但目前该能力仍严重欠缺。本文旨在填补这一空白，实现THz光子介导的量子纠缠生成。

Method: 利用强可见光驱动极性量子发射体，产生Rabi劈裂的缀饰本征态（Rabi-split dressed eigenstates），其能隙可光学调谐至THz范围。发射体的极性激活本征态内的THz跃迁，使其耦合到THz光子模式，诱导集体耗散动力学（collective dissipative dynamics）。通过近THz跃迁频率失谐的边带光学驱动（sideband optical drive）实现有效THz发射体的相干驱动与控制。

Result: 在集体耗散与驱动的共同作用下，生成了高并发度（concurrence, C>0.9）的稳态纠缠（steady-state entanglement），且该结果在实验可行参数下可达到。所有相干操控与量子态层析（quantum state tomography）完全通过光学方式实现，无需直接THz控制与探测。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种混合可见光-THz量子接口（hybrid visible-THz quantum interface），其中THz信道介导量子比特间的纠缠（qubit-qubit entanglement），同时保持全光学可访问性。这为实现THz量子技术的关键操作需求提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Quantum technologies in the terahertz (THz) require a coherent interface between addressable qubits and THz quantum channels -- a capacity that so far, remains largely underdeveloped. Here, we propose and demonstrate the generation of steady-state entanglement between polar quantum emitters, mediated by THz photons. We exploit strong visible-light driving of the emitters to create Rabi-split dressed eigenstates whose energy separation can be optically tuned into the THz regime. The polar nature of the emitters activates THz transitions within these eigenstates, allowing them to couple to a THz photonic mode that induces collective dissipative dynamics. A coherent driving and control of these effective THz emitters is achieved by using a sideband optical drive with detuning close to the THz transition frequency. The resulting interplay of collective dissipation and driving activates a mechanism to generate steady-state entanglement with high values of the concurrence ($C>0.9$), attainable under experimentally feasible parameters. Crucially, both coherent manipulation and quantum state tomography are implemented entirely through optical means, avoiding direct THz control and detection. This establishes a hybrid visible-THz quantum interface in which a THz channel mediates qubit-qubit entanglement (a key operational requirement for THz quantum technologies) while remaining optically accessible.

</details>


### [53] [Robust continuous symmetry breaking and multiversality in the chiral Dicke model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21820)
*Nikolay Yegovtsev,Sayan Choudhury,W. Vincent Liu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文推广了Dicke模型，引入手性Dicke模型。该模型具有内在的U(1)对称性，并展现出U(1)破缺的超辐射相。研究发现系统在同一相变中表现出“多重标度性（multiversality）”，即不同普适类（universality classes）支配同一对相之间的转变，例如动力学临界指数从zν=1变为zν=1/2。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Dicke模型是理解集体光-物质相互作用的范式，但标准模型缺乏连续对称性。作者希望通过引入手性耦合（chiral interactions）来推广该模型，探索由连续对称性带来的新物理现象。

Method: 作者构造了一个手性Dicke模型，其中原子系综通过手性相互作用耦合到双模腔。通过分析基态相图和量子涨落谱，作者研究了量子相变（quantum phase transitions）及其临界行为。

Result: 该模型展现出U(1)破缺的超辐射相，其参数空间范围广泛。量子涨落谱在对称相和破缺相中均高度可调。系统表现出多重标度性：沿参数空间中的特殊线，正常-超辐射相变的动力学临界指数从zν=1变为zν=1/2。

Conclusion: 手性Dicke模型为在光-物质耦合系统中实现新型量子相和多普适类临界现象提供了一个强有力的平台。

Abstract: The Dicke model (DM) serves as a paradigm for understanding collective light-matter interactions. We introduce the chiral Dicke model, a generalization where an atomic ensemble couples to a two-mode cavity via chiral interactions. Unlike the standard DM, the chiral DM is endowed with an inherent continuous $U(1)$ symmetry associated with angular momentum conservation. The ground-state phase diagram and the associated quantum phase transitions are charted out, revealing a $U(1)$-broken superradiant phase that spans a broad parameter space. We demonstrate that the spectrum of quantum fluctuations is highly tunable in both the symmetric and broken phases. Strikingly, our calculations reveal that the system exhibits `multiversality', where distinct universality classes govern the transition between the same two phases. In particular, along a special line in parameter space, the dynamical critical exponent for the normal-superradiant phase transition changes from $zν=1$ to $zν=1/2$. Our work establishes the chiral Dicke model as a powerful platform to realize novel quantum phases and multiversal critical phenomena in light-matter coupled systems.

</details>


### [54] [Enhancing Coherence of Spin Centers in p-n Diodes via Optimization Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21874)
*Jonatan A. Posligua,David E. Stewart,Denis R. Candido*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过结合泊松方程数值解与非耗尽区电荷噪声计算，开发了一种缩放梯度下降优化算法，最小化自旋中心的光学线宽，从而找出最大化自旋中心相干性的二极管设计参数组合。研究以SiC p-i-n二极管中的空位缺陷为对象，在物理约束下优化了偏压、掺杂密度与分布、器件长度等参数，并提出了泄漏电流对相干性影响的新理论形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管反向偏置p-n结二极管已被证实能有效缩小固态自旋缺陷的光学线宽并增强自旋相干性，但影响自旋中心相干性的多参数（如掺杂密度与分布、温度、偏压、自旋中心位置）尚未被系统优化。本文旨在回答“哪一组设计参数能最大化自旋中心相干性”这一关键问题。

Method: 开发了一种缩放梯度下降（scaled gradient descent）优化算法，将二极管的泊松方程（Poisson equation）数值解与非耗尽区计算得到的电荷噪声（charge noise）相结合，以最小化自旋中心的光学线宽。优化针对SiC p-i-n二极管中的双空位缺陷（divacancies），涵盖单参数和多参数情形，并受限于实际物理约束（如低偏压、避免介电击穿、掺杂密度物理阈值）。同时，针对反向偏置下的泄漏电流（leakage current），建立了新的理论形式来评估其对相干性的影响。

Result: 通过优化算法确定了在物理约束下使光学线宽最窄的二极管设计参数组合。研究表明，泄漏电流引起的噪声可以通过将自旋缺陷植入远离二极管表面位置来有效抑制。

Conclusion: 该工作为实验上设计能容纳具有最窄光学线宽和最长相干时间的自旋中心的二极管提供了具体指导。

Abstract: Solid-state spin defects hold great promise as building blocks for various quantum technologies. Embedding spin centers in $p$-$n$ diodes under reverse bias has proved to be a powerful strategy to narrow the optical linewidth and increase spin coherence, while also enabling control of the photoluminescence wavelength via Stark shift. Given the multitude of parameters influencing spin centers in diodes (e.g., doping densities and profiles, temperature, bias voltage, spin center position), a question that has not yet been answered is: which set of these design parameters maximizes spin center coherence? In this work, we address this question by developing a scaled gradient descent optimization algorithm that minimizes the optical linewidth of spin centers by combining the numerical solution of a diode's Poisson equation with calculated charge noise from the non-depleted regions. Our optimization is performed for both single- and multiple-parameter cases for divacancies in SiC $p$-$i$-$n$ diodes, including reverse-bias voltage, doping density and profile, and diode total length. Importantly, the optimization is subject to realistic physical constraints, such as small operating bias voltages, avoidance of the dielectric breakdown regime and physical thresholds for doping density. Additionally, due to the leakage current at reverse bias voltages, we develop a new formalism to investigate its influence on coherence. We show that the corresponding noise can be mitigated by implanting spin defects away from the diode's surfaces. Our work provides guidance on experimentally relevant diodes for hosting spin centers with the narrowest optical linewidths and longest coherence times.

</details>


### [55] [Dual-use quantum hardware for quantum resource generation and energy storage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21913)
*Vaibhav Sharma,Yiming Wang,Shouvik Sur*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明量子资源（如纠缠）的高效制备与量子电池的集体充电优势可以共存，并提出了一个基于超导电路的集成硬件协议，使同一实验装置可在量子电池充电与量子传感两种功能间切换，表明量子资源与存储能量是可协同生产的两个不同量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子资源（如纠缠）的高效生成是量子技术平台的核心目标，而量子电池（quantum battery）作为一种利用集体量子效应实现快速储能的纳米器件，其充电优势同样备受关注。此前这两个研究方向相互独立，本文旨在探究二者之间的内在联系。 

Method: 作者首先从理论上论证：快速生成资源富集量子态（resourceful quantum states）的协议可以同时以集体优势为量子电池充电，反之亦然。基于这一联系，提出一个集成硬件协议（integrated hardware protocol），在超导电路（superconducting circuits）上实现，每个实验运行（experimental run）可互换地完成量子电池充电或通过生成具有计量学价值的状态（metrologically useful states）进行量子传感。

Result: 建立了量子资源与存储能量之间可以协同生产的理论联系，并提出了一个在超导电路上实现的双功能硬件协议，无需额外硬件成本即可在充电与传感功能间动态切换。

Conclusion: 量子资源与存储能量是两种不同但可协同生产的量，这为构建能够在传感与储能功能间动态切换的模块化量子架构（modular quantum architecture）打开了新途径，从而以零额外硬件成本获得附加功能。

Abstract: Quantum resources such as entanglement form the backbone of quantum technologies and their efficient generation is a central objective of modern quantum platforms. Independently, quantum batteries have emerged as nanoscale devices that utilize collective quantum effects to store energy with a charging advantage over classical strategies. Here, we show that these two pursuits can co-exist: protocols for fast generation of resourceful quantum states can simultaneously charge a quantum battery with a collective advantage, and conversely, a quantum battery protocol with a charging advantage can produce resource-rich states. Using this connection, we propose an integrated hardware protocol on superconducting circuits in which each experimental run can interchangeably accomplish either quantum battery charging, or quantum sensing through generation of metrologically useful states. Our results establish that quantum resources and stored energy are distinct yet co-producable quantities, opening the door to modular quantum architectures that dynamically switch between sensing and energy-storage functions, thereby producing additional functionalities without extra hardware cost.

</details>

### [56] [Element-deletion-enhanced digital image correlation for automated crack detection and tracking in lattice materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20974)
*Alessandra Lingua,Arturo Chao Correas,François Hild,David S. Kammer*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种专为点阵材料（architected materials）设计的全局数字图像相关（DIC）框架，该框架直接在点阵网格上求解相关问题，并利用数据驱动的残差准则自动识别和移除失效单元，从而精确追踪裂纹萌生与扩展过程。在3D打印的规则与非完美三角点阵上的I型加载验证表明，该方法能够准确捕捉损伤萌生与裂纹传播，并提供可用于数值模型的临界失效应变估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前点阵材料的应用受限于对其离散结构中裂纹萌生与扩展机制的不充分理解。传统针对连续固体的光学方法（如数字图像相关，digital image correlation, DIC）无法解析点阵中细长梁的局部高度变形，因此亟需一种能够同时兼顾点阵离散性和失效过程中材料不连续性演化的测量策略。

Method: 提出了一种全局DIC框架，直接在点阵网格（lattice mesh）上求解相关（correlation）问题，并在分析过程中自动移除失效单元。损伤检测基于数据驱动的残差准则（data-driven residual criterion），从而实现对局部变形和裂纹尖端运动的鲁棒追踪，并在不断演化的完整点阵拓扑上提供物理一致的位移场测量。

Result: 在3D打印的规则与非完美三角点阵（triangular lattices）上的I型加载（mode-I loading）验证表明，该方法准确捕捉了损伤萌生与裂纹传播过程。此外，识别失效单元可提供临界失效应变（critical failure strain）的估计，该估计可直接用于数值模型或作为DIC分析中的替代单元删除阈值（element-deletion threshold）。

Conclusion: 所提出的全局DIC框架能够有效表征点阵材料中的裂纹萌生与扩展，解决了传统光学方法在离散结构中的局限性；同时，该方法提供的临界失效应变估计对数值建模具有直接应用价值。

Abstract: Architected materials can exhibit remarkable combinations of stiffness, strength, and toughness, yet their application is currently limited by an incomplete understanding of how cracks initiate and propagate through their discrete architecture. Elucidating the mechanisms that underpin these processes is challenging because lattice failure is governed by highly localized deformations of slender beams, which fall outside the resolution and assumptions of optical methods developed for continuum solids, such as digital image correlation (DIC). Thus, characterizing crack propagation within lattice materials requires measurement strategies capable of resolving lattice-scale deformations while accounting for both the intrinsic discreteness of lattice architectures and the progressive formation of material discontinuities during failure. This work introduces a global DIC framework tailored to architected materials, in which the correlation problem is solved directly on the lattice mesh and damaged elements are automatically removed during the analyses. Damage detection, which relies on a data-driven residual criterion, enables the robust tracking of localized deformation and crack-tip motion under different testing conditions. The method provides physically consistent displacement field measurements on the evolving intact lattice topology and resolves the crack path over time. Validations on 3D-printed regular and imperfect triangular lattices under mode-I loading demonstrate that the approach accurately captures both damage initiation and crack propagation. Furthermore, we demonstrate that identifying damaged elements provides an estimate of the critical failure strain, which can be used directly in numerical models or adopted as an alternative element-deletion threshold in DIC analyses.

</details>


### [57] [Orientation Dynamics of Gyrotactic Microswimmers in Turbulent Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21033)
*Suraj Kumar Nayak,Vishwanath Shukla,Akshay Bhatnagar*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过直接数值模拟（DNS）研究了悬浮在均匀各向同性湍流中的趋旋性（gyrotactic）微型游泳者的动力学行为，分析了三个无量纲参数（长径比、游泳速度和重定向时间）对取向分布、自相关、均方位移及垂直迁移效率的影响，并提出了一个简化二维模型以定性复现三维模拟的关键趋势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解趋旋性微生物（gyrotactic microorganisms）在湍流环境中的运动和迁移机制，这对于生态学（如浮游生物垂直迁移）和生物工程应用具有重要意义。

Method: 采用直接数值模拟（direct numerical simulations, DNS）求解悬浮在均匀各向同性湍流（homogeneous and isotropic turbulence）中的微型游泳者动力学。游泳者由三个无量纲参数表征：长径比（aspect ratio, γ）、无量纲游泳速度（dimensionless swimming speed, φ）和无量纲重定向时间（dimensionless reorientation time, ψ）。此外，构建了一个简化的二维模型用于定性对比。

Result: 强趋旋性（小ψ）促进游泳者垂直对齐，弱趋旋性导致近各向同性取向。低游泳数下取向分布几乎与形状无关，但高活性下分布尾部显示形状依赖性；大ψ时杆状粒子沿垂直方向对齐更强。小ψ下杆状游泳者沿应变率张量拉伸方向对齐，大ψ下偏好与涡量矢量对齐。取向自相关呈指数衰减，衰减率标度为1/(2ψ)。均方位移（mean-squared displacement, MSD）显示从短时弹道运动到长时扩散行为的转变。简化二维模型定性复现了三维模拟的主要趋势。

Conclusion: 趋旋性强度和粒子长径比共同调节微型游泳者在湍流中的取向动力学和垂直迁移效率；所提出的简化二维模型可作为高效近似工具用于进一步研究。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of gyrotactic microswimmers suspended in homogeneous and isotropic turbulence by using direct numerical simulations (DNS). The swimmers are characterized by three non-dimensional parameters: their aspect ratio ($γ$), a dimensionless swimming speed ($φ$), and a dimensionless reorientation time ($ψ$). Strong gyrotaxis (smaller $ψ$) promotes vertical alignment of the swimmers, while weak gyrotaxis leads to nearly isotropic orientations. At low swimming numbers, the orientation distribution is largely shape-independent with spheres and spheroids showing marginally greater vertical alignment than rods, whereas at higher activity the peaks of the distributions exhibit largely shape-independent behavior and the tails show a clear dependence on particle shape. However, at large $ψ$ rods exhibit a stronger alignment along the vertical. We observe that at small $ψ$ the rod-shaped swimmers respond to shear by aligning with the stretching direction of the strain-rate tensor, while at large $ψ$ the alignment with the vorticity vector is preferred. The orientation autocorrelation is found to decay exponentially, with a decay rate that scales as $1/(2ψ)$. Analysis of the mean-squared displacement (MSD) reveals a transition from a ballistic motion at short times to a diffusive regime at longer times. To assess the efficiency of vertical migration, we compute the probability distributions of vertical displacement over a fixed time interval and the time taken to migrate a specific vertical distance. Furthermore, we use a simplified two-dimensional model for spherical swimmers that qualitatively reproduces the key trends observed in the full three-dimensional (3D) simulations.

</details>


### [58] [Linking molecular timescales to linear viscoelastic response in dilute and semidilute unentangled wormlike micelle solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21194)
*Avishek Kumar,Rico F Tabor,P. Sunthar,J. Ravi Prakash*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文通过多粒子介观布朗动力学（Brownian dynamics）框架，模拟了未缠结蠕虫状胶束（wormlike micelle）溶液的应力松弛过程，识别了影响其动力学和线粘弹性响应的多个特征时间尺度，并建立了微观动力学与宏观流变学之间的直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蠕虫状胶束溶液通过可逆断裂（reversible scission）和链内松弛（intrachain relaxation）的动态耦合来松弛应力，涉及一组层次化的分子时间尺度，但这些时间尺度与线性粘弹性响应之间的关系尚未得到完整的解释。

Method: 开发了一个多粒子介观布朗动力学（Brownian dynamics）框架，使用带有粘性末端的珠-弹簧链（bead-spring chains）表示持久性蠕虫，通过可逆断裂和融合（fusion）组装形成蠕虫状胶束；利用RPY张量（Rotne-Prager-Yamakawa tensor）计入流体力学相互作用（hydrodynamic interactions）。

Result: 识别并量化了多个特征时间尺度，包括键寿命、自重组和非自重组时间、不同长度L的胶束断裂时间、各应力贡献的松弛时间及最长松弛时间；发现环状胶束（ring micelles）会适度延长重组和断裂过程，流体力学相互作用通过降低粘性末端迁移率影响部分时间尺度；非自重组时间和断裂时间经适当缩放后坍缩到主曲线（master curves）上；储能模量和损耗模量在中频区域表现出均聚物溶液所没有的特征。

Conclusion: 建立了一个将胶束微观动力学与宏观流变学直接联系起来的框架，明确了胶束时间尺度与动态模量中特征频率处信号之间的对应关系，准确预测了稀溶液和半稀溶液（semidilute）浓度区域中未缠结蠕虫状胶束的动态性质。

Abstract: Unentangled wormlike micelle solutions relax stress through a dynamic interplay of reversible scission and intrachain relaxation involving a hierarchy of molecular timescales whose relationship to linear viscoelastic response remains incompletely resolved. A multiparticle mesoscopic Brownian dynamics framework has been developed in which persistent worms, represented by bead-spring chains with sticky ends, assemble to form wormlike micelles via reversible scission and fusion. Both linear and ring-like micelles are formed across the dilute and semidilute concentration regimes. Accurate predictions of dynamic properties are obtained through inclusion of hydrodynamic interactions using a RPY tensor. We identify and quantify characteristic timescales governing micellar dynamics, including bond lifetimes, self- and non-self-recombination times, breakage times of wormlike micelles of length $L$, relaxation times of various contributions to stress, and the longest relaxation time. The dependence of these timescales on sticker strength, concentration, micellar topology and hydrodynamic interactions is established. The presence of ring micelles is found to moderately prolong recombination and breakage processes, while hydrodynamic interactions are shown to affect some of the timescales by reducing sticker mobility. When appropriately scaled, the dependence on mean length of the non-self-recombination and micelle breakage times collapse onto master curves. Storage and loss moduli exhibit distinctive features in the intermediate-frequency regime that are absent in homopolymer solutions. A clear connection is made between micellar timescales and these signatures in the dynamic moduli at various characteristic frequencies, providing a direct link between microscopic dynamics and macroscopic rheology in unentangled wormlike micellar solutions, in dilute and semidilute concentration regimes.

</details>


### [59] [Continuum granular flow model with restitution-derived viscoelastic damping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21448)
*Bodhinanda Chandra,Sachith Dunatunga,Ken Kamrin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统一的粘弹性-粘塑性连续介质框架，用于跨流态模拟率相关颗粒流，核心贡献是通过波衰减分析将恢复系数与连续粘度显式关联，从而桥接颗粒尺度碰撞物理与宏观阻尼，并在保持 μ(I) 流变学的前提下实现粘弹性-粘塑性耦合。该框架基于物质点法实现，并通过稳态、瞬态、振动和冲击驱动流算例验证了其捕获波传播、扩散和率相关行为的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 颗粒流在不同流态（从准静态到快速碰撞流）中表现出显著的率依赖行为，现有模型往往难以在统一的连续介质框架内同时刻画微观惯性、粘弹性耗散与塑性流动等多种机制，缺乏对颗粒尺度碰撞物理与宏观阻尼之间的直接理论关联。

Method: 通过分析颗粒集合体中的波衰减过程，推导出恢复系数（coefficient of restitution）与连续粘度（continuum viscosity）之间的显式关系，从而将颗粒尺度碰撞物理与宏观阻尼直接关联。同时保留由经典 μ(I) 流变学（μ(I) rheology）控制的惯性依赖塑性流动，并精心划分模型及应力更新例程中的弹性与粘性响应，使粘性耗散支配波动与碰撞过程但不改变塑性流动法则。该框架在物质点法（material point method）中实现。

Result: 通过一系列数值算例（包括稳态流、瞬态流、振动流和冲击驱动流）验证了该模型在统一连续介质框架下捕获波传播、扩散以及率依赖颗粒行为的能力。

Conclusion: 该统一粘弹性-粘塑性连续介质框架成功桥接了颗粒尺度碰撞物理与宏观连续尺度描述，为跨流态率依赖颗粒流模拟提供了有效手段，且不改变原有的塑性流动规则。

Abstract: This work presents a unified viscoelastic-viscoplastic continuum framework for modeling rate-dependent granular flows across regimes. The formulation incorporates two distinct rate-dependent mechanisms, namely micro-inertia and viscoelastic dissipation, within a single continuum description. A central contribution is an explicit link between the coefficient of restitution and a continuum viscosity, derived from an analysis of wave attenuation in granular assemblies, thereby establishing a direct connection between particle-scale collision physics and macroscopic damping. This relation is introduced while retaining inertia-dependent plastic flow governed by the classical $μ(I)$ rheology. The constitutive model is constructed by meticulously partitioning elastic and viscous responses within the model and corresponding stress-update routine, such that viscous dissipation governs wave propagation and collisional processes without altering the plastic flow rule. The framework is implemented within the material point method to simulate transient processes involving large deformations, material separation, and subsequent reconsolidation. A range of numerical examples, including steady, transient, vibrational, and impact-driven flows, demonstrates that the model captures wave propagation, diffusion, and rate-dependent granular behavior within a unified continuum setting.

</details>


### [60] [Self-phoretic colloids in chiral active fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21701)
*Michalis Chatzittofi,Yuto Hosaka,Andrej Vilfan,Ramin Golestanian*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文将趋化活性物质（phoretic active matter）理论推广至具有奇黏度（odd viscosity）的流体环境，推导了具有任意活性和迁移率表面分布的球形游动体的平动与转动自推进速度表达式，并讨论了轴对称与非轴对称涂层化学活性胶体（chemically active colloids）中对称性与手性（chirality）的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性活性流体（chiral active fluids）中的自主输运和驱动输运表现出经典流体力学（classical fluid mechanics）框架无法容纳的特征，其根源在于奇黏度（odd viscosity）的作用。现有理论亟需拓展以描述此类系统中的活性运动。

Method: 采用理论推广方法，将趋化活性物质理论推广至含奇黏度的流体环境；针对任意活性和迁移率表面分布的球形游动体，推导了平动与转动自推进速度的一般表达式。

Result: 得到了球形游动体在奇黏度流体中自推进速度的解析表达式；通过轴对称与非轴对称涂层化学活性胶体的具体例子，揭示了对称性与手性之间的相互作用。

Conclusion: 该研究结果可用于分析时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）和宇称对称性（parity symmetry）破缺的流体介质中趋化粒子的涌现集体动力学（emergent collective dynamics）。

Abstract: Autonomous and driven transport in chiral active fluids have been shown to exhibit features that cannot be accommodated within the classical formulation of fluid mechanics, due to the role of odd viscosity. We generalize the theory of phoretic active matter to fluid environments with odd viscosity and derive expressions for translational and rotational self-propulsion velocities in the case of a spherical swimmer with arbitrary activity and mobility surface profiles. We discuss specific examples of chemically active colloids with axisymmetric and non-axisymmetric coatings and the resulting interplay between symmetry and chirality. Our results can be applied to study the emergent collective dynamics of phoretic particles in fluid media with broken time-reversal and parity symmetries.

</details>

### [61] [Giant spontaneous Kerr effect reveals the defect origin of macroscopic time-reversal symmetry breaking in altermagnetic MnTe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21021)
*Weitung Yang,Choongjae Won,Cory Cress,Marshall Zachary Franklin,Xiaochen Fang,Shelby Fields,Nicholas Combs,Shaofeng Han,Weihang Lu,I. I. Mazin,Steven P. Bennett,Sang-Wook Cheong,Jing Xia*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过对比αMnTe单晶与化学计量比绝缘薄膜的磁光克尔效应，发现单晶中高达±1500微弧度的自发克尔旋转来源于载流子自掺杂（carrier self-doping）而非理想交变磁序（altermagnetic order），为交变磁体自旋电子学提供了实用光学读出手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnet）作为继铁磁体和反铁磁体之后的第三类共线磁性材料，在超快、无杂散场自旋电子学中具有潜力。然而，MnTe中观测到的宏观对称性破缺信号（自发霍尔效应与微弱剩余磁矩）究竟源于理想交变磁序（ideal altermagnetic order）还是缺陷激活，仍是一个悬而未决的问题。

Method: 对αMnTe单晶和化学计量比绝缘薄膜进行磁光克尔效应（magneto-optic Kerr effect）测量，对比两者在电信波长1550 nm处自发克尔旋转（spontaneous Kerr rotation）的信号差异。

Result: αMnTe单晶在奈尔温度（Néel temperature）TN = 307 K处出现高达±1500微弧度的巨大自发克尔旋转，而化学计量比绝缘薄膜中未检测到任何可分辨信号。

Conclusion: 体材料与薄膜的对比表明，宏观磁光响应的来源是载流子自掺杂（carrier self-doping）而非理想交变磁序，进而确立了基于电信波长克尔成像（Kerr imaging）的交变磁体自旋电子学实用读出方案。

Abstract: Altermagnetism, a recently identified third class of collinear magnetism with spin-split bands and vanishing net magnetization, has emerged in hexagonal \alphaMnTe{} and is regarded as a promising platform for ultrafast, stray-field-free spintronics and for optical readout of spin order at telecommunication wavelengths. Whether the macroscopic symmetry-breaking signatures reported in MnTe, a spontaneous Hall effect and a tiny ``gossamer'' remanent moment, reflect the ideal altermagnetic order or are activated by defects remains an open question. Here we report giant spontaneous Kerr rotations of up to $\pm 1500\microrad$ in \alphaMnTe{} single crystals at the telecommunication wavelength of $1550\,\mathrm{nm}$, onsetting precisely at the Néel temperature $\TN = 307\,\mathrm{K}$. In contrast, a stoichiometric insulating \alphaMnTe{} thin film shows no detectable signal. The bulk--film contrast identifies carrier self-doping, rather than the ideal altermagnetic order, as the source of macroscopic magneto-optical response, establishing telecom-wavelength Kerr imaging as a practical readout for altermagnetic spintronics.

</details>


### [62] [Symplectic symmetry of quadratic-band-touching Hamiltonians in two dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21524)
*Igor F. Herbut,Samson C. H. Ling*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文发现二维无质量狄拉克哈密顿量的低能内禀对称性为酉辛群 USp(2N)，并分析了该对称性下相互作用项的结构、自发破缺模式，以及其与正交群 O(2N) 的交集在晶格（如蜂窝晶格）中的表现为 U(N)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知 (2+1) 维无质量洛伦兹不变狄拉克哈密顿量的内禀低能对称性为 O(2N)。本文旨在指出，二维空间中存在一个类似的内禀对称性——酉辛群（unitary symplectic group）USp(2N)——对应于单粒子二次能带接触（quadratic-band-touching）哈密顿量，并探讨其相互作用物理与对称性结构。

Method: 从单粒子二次能带接触哈密顿量出发，识别其内禀对称性为 USp(2N)；将所有费米子双线性（fermionic bilinears）归类为该群的三个不可约表示（irreducible representations）；构建了同时尊重 USp(2N) 对称性与空间旋转对称性的相互作用理论，并考察红外相关（infrared-relevant）相互作用下的对称性保持与自发破缺；通过分析辛群与正交群在晶格（如蜂窝晶格）动量展开无限阶下的重叠，确定该交集为 U(N)。

Result: 二维二次能带接触哈密顿量的内禀对称性为 USp(2N)；所有费米子双线性属于 USp(2N) 的三个小不可约表示；允许两个独立相互作用项；在红外相关情形下，USp(2N) 对称性要么保持，要么自发破缺为 USp(N) × USp(N)；辛群与正交群的重叠在蜂窝晶格等体系中表现为 O(2N) ∩ USp(2N) = U(N)。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了二次能带接触哈密顿量的 USp(2N) 对称性，为理解相关相互作用系统的量子相变与对称性破缺提供了群论基础；同时明确了辛对称性与正交对称性在晶格中的交叠结构，有助于指导未来对二维拓扑物质中对称性分类的研究。

Abstract: The internal low-energy symmetry of the massless Lorentz-invariant Dirac Hamiltonian in $2+1$ dimensions is known to be $O(2N)$, where $N$ is the number of two-component Dirac fermions. Here we point out that there exists an analogous internal symmetry of the single-particle quadratic-band-touching Hamiltonian in two spatial dimensions, and it is the unitary symplectic group, $USp(2N)$. All fermionic bilinears belong to one of the three small irreducible representations of this group. The interacting theory that respects the $USp(2N)$ symmetry and the spatial rotations is constructed and found to allow two independent interaction terms. When these interactions are infrared-relevant the symplectic symmetry either remains preserved or becomes spontaneously broken to $USp(N) \times USp(N)$. The symmetry in the lattices such as honeycomb to infinite order in the dispersion's expansion in powers of local momentum is given by the overlap of the symplectic and the orthogonal groups. We show that this overlap is $O(2N) \bigcap USp(2N) = U(N)$.

</details>


### [63] [Studying 3D O(N) Surface CFT on the Fuzzy Sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21091)
*Jiechao Feng,Taige Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用模糊球（fuzzy sphere）上的双层海森堡模型，首次在连续O(N)对称性下确定了2+1维O(2)和O(3) Wilson-Fisher固定点中1+1维边界的边界共形场论（BCFT）数据，包括正常边界条件和普通边界条件对应的算子谱、原初算子和边界中心荷，并提供了超越伊辛普适类的模糊球BCFT谱学证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边界共形场论（boundary conformal field theory, BCFT）为存在边界的临界现象提供了普适框架，但连续O(N)对称性下高维边界BCFT数据的数值确定仍相对缺乏。本文旨在利用模糊球方法系统提取O(2)和O(3) Wilson-Fisher固定点的边界算子谱及边界临界数据。

Method: 基于模糊球上的双层海森堡模型，利用模糊球-状态-算子对应关系（fuzzy-sphere state-operator correspondence），计算边界算子谱（boundary operator spectra），识别低能边界原初算子（boundary primary operators），提取算子乘积展开（operator-product-expansion, OPE）数据，并估计两种边界条件下的边界中心荷（boundary central charges）。

Result: 正常边界条件下，从单点和两点函数提取的普适振幅a_σ和b_t与已有的蒙特卡洛基准定量一致。对于N=2和N=3，均发现正的特异对数指数α（extraordinary-log exponent α），为特异对数边界临界性（extraordinary-log boundary criticality）提供了独立的微观证据。

Conclusion: 本文成功将模糊球BCFT谱学方法从伊辛（Ising）普适类推广至连续O(N)对称性系统，为研究具有连续对称性的边界临界现象提供了新的数值工具和基准数据。

Abstract: Boundary conformal field theory (BCFT) provides a universal framework for critical phenomena in the presence of boundaries. We determine BCFT data for the normal and ordinary boundary universality classes of the $1+1$-dimensional boundaries of the $2+1$-dimensional $O(2)$ and $O(3)$ Wilson-Fisher fixed points, realized microscopically by a bilayer Heisenberg model on the fuzzy sphere. Using the fuzzy-sphere state-operator correspondence, we obtain boundary operator spectra, identify low-lying boundary primary operators, extract operator-product-expansion (OPE) data, and estimate the boundary central charges for both boundary conditions. For the normal boundary condition, the universal amplitudes $a_σ$ and $b_t$ extracted from one- and two-point functions agree quantitatively with Monte Carlo benchmarks where available. For both $N=2$ and $N=3$, we find a positive extraordinary-log exponent $α$, providing independent microscopic evidence for extraordinary-log boundary criticality. Our results extend fuzzy-sphere BCFT spectroscopy beyond the Ising universality class to continuous $O(N)$ symmetry.

</details>


### [64] [BCS-BEC crossover of polaritonic condensates in mass-imbalanced semimetal/semiconductor microcavities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21244)
*Thi-Hau Nguyen,Minh-Tien Tran,Van-Nham Phan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究质量不平衡和库仑相互作用对半导体/半金属微腔中极化激元凝聚体的复杂相结构及其BCS-BEC交叉的影响。在无约束Hartree-Fock近似框架下分析两带电子-空穴模型，展示了从半导体区到半金属区不同配对机制和凝聚体特性的连续变化，并揭示了发光谱可作为这些交叉现象的明确光谱特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨质量不平衡（mass imbalance）和库仑相互作用（Coulomb interaction）如何影响微腔极化激元凝聚体（polaritonic condensates）的复杂相结构及其BCS-BEC交叉（Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer至Bose-Einstein condensation crossover），以构建统一的物理理解框架。

Method: 采用无约束Hartree-Fock近似（unrestricted Hartree-Fock approximation），建立包含光子模式的两带电子-空穴模型（two-band electron-hole model），将库仑吸引和光-物质耦合（light-matter coupling）置于同等地位处理，进而分析单粒子谱函数（single-particle spectral functions）和发光性质（luminescence properties）。

Result: 半导体区：正带隙稳定紧密束缚的激子，低密度下主要形成BEC型类激子极化激元凝聚体；增加激发密度和减小质量不平衡则连续过渡至BCS型配对，具有中间和类光子极化激元特征。半金属区：有利于巡游电子-空穴配对，BCS型凝聚体占主导，仅当库仑相互作用足够强且质量不平衡较大时才出现BEC型类激子相干性。发光谱的演化清晰反映了这些交叉现象。

Conclusion: 发光谱的演变可成为区分极化激元凝聚体相变和交叉现象的清晰光谱标记，为理解和调控微腔系统中的极化激元凝聚体提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: The impacts of the mass imbalance and Coulomb interaction on the complex phase structures of the polaritonic condensates and their Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer (BCS)--Bose-Einstein condensation (BEC) crossover in semiconductor and semimetal microcavities are investigated. In the framework of the unrestricted Hartree-Fock approximation, a two-band electron-hole model involving photon mode is analyzed by treating Coulomb attraction and light-matter coupling on equal footing. The single-particle spectral functions and the luminescence properties are then examined. In the semiconducting regime, a positive band gap stabilizes tightly bound excitons and yields predominantly BEC-type excitoniclike polaritonic condensates at low density, while increasing excitation density and reducing mass imbalance drives a continuous crossover toward BCS-type pairing with intermediate and photoniclike polaritonic character. In contrast, the semimetallic regime favors itinerant electron-hole pairing, with BCS-type condensates dominating and BEC excitoniclike coherence emerging only at sufficiently strong Coulomb interaction and large mass imbalance situations. The evolution of luminescence spectra provides clear spectroscopic signatures of these crossover phenomena, offering a unified framework for understanding and controlling polaritonic condensates in microcavity systems.

</details>


### [65] [Condensate states in Fermi and Bose-Hubbard ladders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21296)
*F. X. Liu,E. S. Ma,Z. Song*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维扩展Hubbard梯子模型（extended Hubbard ladders）中费米子和硬核玻色子在配对态下的统计等价性，指出当只考虑局域对（pair）态时，硬核玻色子对和费米子对服从相同的统计规律。通过构建精确的凝聚对（condensate-pair）本征态，并利用谱生成代数（spectrum generating algebra）与数值模拟，揭示了费米子与硬核玻色子的相似性及Hilbert空间碎片化（Hilbert-space fragmentation）的可能机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管硬核玻色子（hardcore bosons）和费米子（fermions）都不能占据同一个单格点态，它们仍服从不同的统计规律，导致截然不同的多粒子量子态（如凝聚态vs费米液态）。然而当只考虑配对态时，两者可能呈现相同形式，这一潜在等价性构成了本文的研究动机。

Method: 研究了可在合成原子梯子（synthetic atomic ladders）中实验实现的费米和玻色扩展Hubbard梯子模型。在SU(2)对称性下构建了费米梯子的一组精确凝聚对本征态，并通过谱生成代数获得；相应的硬核玻色子对应态则通过将费米子算符替换为硬核玻色子算符得到。此外，通过动态响应的数值模拟研究了次近邻跳跃（next-nearest-neighbor hopping）对凝聚态的影响。

Result: 费米梯子的精确凝聚对本征态可在SU(2)对称性下构造并由谱生成代数导出。硬核玻色子对的本征态不依赖于对称性，而是依赖于受限谱生成代数（restricted spectrum generating algebra）。次近邻跳跃对凝聚态的影响通过数值模拟得到分析。结论可推广至双层系统（two-layer system）。结果揭示了费米子与硬核玻色子的相似性，以及Hilbert空间碎片化的可能机制。

Conclusion: 研究表明当仅考虑配对态时，费米子与硬核玻色子表现出统计上的等价性，这为理解两类粒子的深层联系提供了新的视角。同时，该研究揭示了Hilbert空间碎片化的一种可能机制，对多体量子系统的理论分类具有潜在意义。

Abstract: Although neither hardcore bosons nor fermions can occupy the same single-site state, they still obey different statistics, resulting in distinct many-particle quantum states, such as condensate states versus Fermi-liquid states. However, when only pair states are considered, the two can take the same form, since a local hardcore Bose pair and a Fermi pair obey the same statistics. In this work we demonstrate this by studying both Fermi and Bose extended Hubbard ladders, which can be realized experimentally in synthetic atomic ladders. A set of exact condensate-pair eigenstates for the Fermi ladder is constructed under SU(2) symmetry and can then be obtained by the spectrum generating algebra. The corresponding hardcore boson counterpart can be simply obtained by replacing fermionic operators with hardcore bosonic ones. Nevertheless, the boson-pair eigenstates are associated not with symmetry but with the restricted spectrum generating algebra. We also investigate the effect of next-nearest-neighbor hopping on the condensate states through numerical simulations of the dynamic response. The conclusions can be extended to a two-layer system. Our result reveals not only the resemblance of fermions to hardcore bosons, but also a possible mechanism of Hilbert-space fragmentation.

</details>


### [66] [$η$-pairing in a two-band model of spinless fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21318)
*Igor N. Karnaukhov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过 Bethe ansatz 精确求解一维无自旋费米子双带模型，发现双粒子杂化（two-particle hybridization）可降低巡游费米子间的排斥相互作用，并在强耦合下转变为吸引相互作用，实现无自旋费米子的 η 配对（η-pairing），进而诱导 p 波超导态，可能为高压富氢材料中的高温超导现象提供解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索通过双粒子杂化机制实现无自旋费米子 η 配对的可行性，并为高压富氢材料中实验观察到的高温超导现象提供理论解释。

Method: 构建包含巡游费米子（itinerant fermions）与局域费米子（localized fermions）通过双粒子杂化相互作用的双带模型（two-band model），在一维（1D）情况下利用 Bethe ansatz 获得精确解（exact solution）。

Result: 双粒子杂化降低了巡游费米子间的排斥相互作用；在强相互作用条件下，有效相互作用变为吸引，实现了无自旋费米子的 η 配对。

Conclusion: 通过双粒子杂化实现的 η 配对可导致 p 波超导态（p-superconducting states），该机制可能解释高压富氢材料中观察到的高温超导现象。

Abstract: We study the two-band model of spinless fermions in which itinerant fermions interact with localized fermions through the two-particle hybridization. In 1D version, the model has exact solution using the Bethe ansatz. It has been shown that accounting for two-particle hybridization reduces the repulsive interaction between itinerant fermions. In the case of strong interaction, the effective interaction between itinerant fermions is attractive, and $η$-pairing of spinless fermions is realized. The proposed pairing mechanism via two-particle hybridization can lead to $p$-superconducting states with $η$-pairing. $η$-pairing of spinless fermions could explain the phenomenon of high-temperature superconductivity experimentally observed in hydrogen-rich materials at high pressures.

</details>


### [67] [Pressure-Tuned Competing Electronic States in Layered Tellurides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21336)
*Mahmoud Abdel-Hafiez,Govindaraj Lingannan,D. A. Chareev,A. N. Vasiliev,Anas Abutaha,Kadir Can Dogan,Mehmet Yagmurcukardes,Mehmet Egilmez,Hasan Sahin,Sami El-Khatib*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过静水压下的磁输运实验，系统研究了块体半导体2H-MoTe₂从局域化跳跃输运到量子干涉输运的连续演化过程，并借助第一性原理计算揭示了压力驱动带隙闭合的物理机制，建立了一个统一描述压力调控输运行为的理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 层状过渡金属二硫属化物（TMDs）中并存多种可调谐的竞争电子态，但无序、电子结构与量子输运之间的相互作用机制尚待深入理解。本文旨在通过静水压（hydrostatic pressure）这一干净的外界扰动，在一个单一材料体系中系统追踪从局域化（localized）到量子相干（quantum-coherent）输运的演化过程。

Method: 对块体半导体2H-MoTe₂进行静水压下的磁输运测量（最高磁场60 T，最高压力15.6 GPa）；利用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析压力对电子能带结构的影响；采用一种物理动机驱动的唯象描述（phenomenological description）统一拟合不同压力下的磁电阻（magnetoresistance）行为。

Result: 常压下，输运从高温金属行为转为激活导电，最终进入强局域化变程跳跃（variable-range hopping）区，并在45 K附近出现显著的磁输运异常以及高达60 T的非饱和巨磁电阻。加压至15.6 GPa时，绝缘态被迅速抑制，出现以量子干涉主导的低电阻率态，并在低温下发生从弱反局域化（WAL）到弱局域化（WL）的交叉。第一性原理计算显示压力导致带隙连续塌缩，最终形成半金属（semimetallic）电子结构。

Conclusion: 研究建立了一个统一的压力调控输运图像，覆盖从跳跃到量子相干的全域输运行为，并发现局域化与量子干涉区间内的特征电子长度尺度（characteristic electronic length scale）保持可比性，表明两种看似不同的输运机制之间存在内在关联。

Abstract: Layered transition-metal dichalcogenides (TMDs) host competing electronic states that can be tuned by external perturbations, providing a platform to explore the interplay between disorder, electronic structure, and quantum transport. Here we investigate magnetotransport in bulk semiconducting 2H-MoTe2 under hydrostatic pressure. At ambient pressure, transport evolves from high-temperature metallic behavior into activated conduction and ultimately a strongly localized variable-range hopping regime, accompanied by a pronounced magnetotransport anomaly near 45 K and large, nonsaturating magnetoresistance extending up to an unprecedented field of 60 T in semiconducting 2H-MoTe2. Under compression to 15.6 GPa, the insulating state is rapidly suppressed and a low-resistivity regime emerges in which quantum interference dominates, exhibiting a crossover from weak antilocalization (WAL) to weak localization (WL) at low temperatures. A physically motivated phenomenological description captures the magnetoresistance across these regimes and yields a characteristic electronic length scale that remains comparable across the localized and quantum-interference regimes. First-principles calculations reveal a continuous pressure-driven collapse of the bandgap into a semimetallic electronic structure. These results establish a unified picture of pressure-tuned transport spanning hopping and quantum-coherent regimes.

</details>


### [68] [Decomposing Fractional Quantum Hall Wave Functions via Operator Contraction Multiplication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21434)
*Dong-Hao Guan,Licheng Wang,Yuan Zhou,Ai-Lei He,Yi-Fei Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于算符收缩乘法（operator contraction multiplication）的代数方案，用于分解分数量子霍尔（fractional quantum Hall, FQH）波函数。通过引入费米子和玻色子算符并建立三条基本收缩规则，实现了Laughlin态的精确分解，并首次完成了Halperin态的完整分解。该框架突破了Jack多项式（Jack polynomials）的长期局限，为单组分和多组分FQH态提供了统一的分解方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有FQH波函数分解方法（如Jack多项式框架）在处理多组分系统时存在局限性，长期无法实现对Halperin态等复杂多组分FQH态的完整分解。本文旨在发展一种通用的代数方案，统一处理单组分和多组分FQH波函数的分解问题。

Method: 基于算符收缩乘法，引入费米子和玻色子算符，建立三条基本收缩规则（contraction rules）以实现Laughlin态的精确分解。对于多组分系统，通过结式（resultants）和初等对称多项式（elementary symmetric polynomials）分解耦合的Jastrow因子，从而实现Halperin态的分解。对于Halperin (2,2,1)态，显式推导其基本展开式，识别根位型（root configurations），并揭示色内与色间压缩算符（intra- and inter-color squeezing operators）。

Result: 首次实现了Halperin态的完整分解。利用该方法计算了多达16个粒子、分解维度超过10^11的轨道纠缠谱（orbital entanglement spectra），获得的边缘激发序列（edge excitation sequences）与手征Luttinger液体理论（chiral Luttinger liquid theory）精确匹配。

Conclusion: 该代数方案突破了Jack多项式的长期局限，为单组分和多组分FQH态提供了统一的分解框架，并为探索更复杂FQH态的波函数开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We develop a general algebraic scheme to decompose fractional quantum Hall (FQH) wave functions based on the operator contraction multiplication. By introducing fermionic and bosonic operators and establishing three fundamental contraction rules, we achieve an exact decomposition of Laughlin states. This approach naturally extends to multi-component systems by factorizing coupled Jastrow factors via resultants and elementary symmetric polynomials, enabling the first complete decomposition of Halperin states. For Halperin ($2,2,1$) state, we explicitly derive its basic expansion, identify root configurations, and reveal intra- and inter-color squeezing operators, thereby uncovering the underlying generalized Pauli principle. Using this method, we compute orbital entanglement spectra for up to $16$ particles with decomposition dimensions exceeding $10^{11}$, obtaining edge excitation sequences that precisely match chiral Luttinger liquid theory. Our framework breaks through the longstanding limitations of Jack polynomials, provides a unified decomposition for both single- and multi-component FQH states, and opens a new avenue for exploring wave functions for more complex FQH states.

</details>


### [69] [Dynamical mean-field theory for dense spin systems at finite temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21563)
*Przemysław Bieniek,Timo Gräßer,Götz S. Uhrig*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将spinDMFT方法从无限温度扩展到有限温度的重要扩展，使其能够计算虚时关联（imaginary-time correlations）和热力学量，并通过与有限尺寸系统比较，在随机耦合系统和铁磁系统中验证了方法的有效性，同时发现了铁磁序的出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自旋动力学无限温度方法（spinDMFT）仅限于无限温度情形，无法处理有限温度下的自旋关联和热力学量计算，因此需要开发一种扩展方法以填补这一空白。

Method: 基于费米子动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory, DMFT）的思想，采用单点近似（single-site approximation）和自洽条件（self-consistency condition），将spinDMFT方法系统性地扩展到有限温度，从而能够计算虚时关联和热力学量。

Result: 方法基准测试显示：在随机耦合系统中与有限尺寸结果吻合很好，在铁磁系统中一致性良好，但在反铁磁系统中出现较大偏差；此外，方法中还观测到了铁磁序（ferromagnetic order）的出现。

Conclusion: 该方法在随机耦合和铁磁体系中表现可靠，但在反铁磁体系中存在显著局限性；未来可探讨该方法的扩展方向及应用前景。

Abstract: In recent years, a method for computing spin dynamics at infinite temperature (spinDMFT) was developed. It utilizes the ideas of dynamical mean-field theory for fermions: single-site approximation and a self-consistency condition to approximate time-dependent spin correlations. In this work, we develop a crucial extension of the method to systems at finite temperature, able to compute imaginary-time correlations and thermodynamical quantities. We benchmark the method by comparison to results in finite-size systems, obtaining very good agreement with correlations in a random-coupling system, good agreement for a ferromagnetic system and large discrepancies in the case of an antiferromagnet. We note the appearance of ferromagnetic order in the method. We discuss possible extensions and potential applications of the approach.

</details>

### [70] [Monolithically Integrated VO$_2$ Mott Oscillators for Energy-Efficient Spiking Neurons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21487)
*Fabio Bersano,Cyrille Masserey,Vanessa Conti,Andrea Iaconeta,Niccolo' Martinolli,Ehsan Ansari,Anna Varini,Igor Stolichnov,Adrian Mihai Ionescu*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文报道了基于二氧化钒（VO₂）的1T-1MR（单晶体管-单忆阻器）尖峰神经元的单片后道工艺（BEOL）集成方案，在CMOS兼容平台上实现了紧凑、低功耗的基于莫特相变（Mott phase-transition）的神经形态硬件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受脑启发的非布尔计算（non-Boolean computing）具有内在容错性和并行性，但实际部署受限于缺乏兼容大规模集成的紧凑、节能尖峰硬件；现有VO₂基神经形态器件依赖分立组件，集成密度和系统适用性受限。

Method: 采用单片后端工艺（back-end-of-the-line, BEOL）集成，将VO₂纳米片器件通过脉冲激光沉积（pulsed-laser deposition）在低于430°C的条件下制备于介电隔离的绝缘体上硅（silicon-on-insulator, SOI）p型无结场效应晶体管（junctionless field-effect transistor, JLFET）上，形成紧凑的1T-1MR结构。

Result: 60 nm厚、有源面积6 μm²的VO₂器件实现了40至410 kHz的栅极可调振荡，室温下每尖峰能耗低至18 pJ，忆阻器功耗为8 μW，并具备向低于3 μW缩放的可能性；发现了振荡频率对电流和温度的非单调依赖关系，以及偏置依赖的随机尖峰动力学；演示了压控振荡器功能和两个纳米振荡器通过JLFET的有源可调电阻耦合。

Conclusion: 本工作为构建密集、节能且与CMOS技术兼容的单片集成莫特基神经形态硬件（Mott-based neuromorphic hardware）建立了可行路径。

Abstract: Brain-inspired non-Boolean computing offers intrinsic error tolerance and parallelism, but its practical deployment is limited by the lack of compact, energy-efficient spiking hardware compatible with large-scale integration. Mott phase-transition materials provide a promising route, as their abrupt insulator-to-metal transitions enable neuron-like thresholding and oscillatory dynamics in compact devices. Among these, vanadium dioxide (VO$_2$) stands out for its near-room-temperature transition, fast switching, and scalability. However, existing VO$_2$-based neuristors rely on discrete components, limiting integration density and system applicability. Here, we report monolithic back-end-of-the-line (BEOL) integration of one-transistor-one-VO2-memristor (1T-1MR) spiking neurons on CMOS-compatible platforms. VO$_2$ nanosheet devices are fabricated by pulsed-laser deposition below 430 °C on dielectrically isolated silicon-on-insulator (SOI) p-type junctionless field-effect transistors (JLFETs) in a compact 1T-1MR configuration. The architecture exhibits gate-tunable oscillations from 40 to 410 kHz in 60 nm-thick VO$_2$ devices with an active area of 6 $μ$m$^2$, achieving energy consumption as low as 18 pJ per spike at room temperature, with memristor power dissipation of 8 $μ$W and potential scaling toward sub-3 $μ$W operation. We further uncover a non-monotonic dependence of oscillation frequency on current and temperature, along with bias-dependent stochastic firing dynamics, highlighting the rich behavior of integrated VO$_2$ memristor systems. Finally, we demonstrate voltage-controlled oscillator functionality and actively tunable resistive coupling of two nano-oscillators mediated by a JLFET. These results establish a pathway toward dense, energy-efficient, and monolithically integrated Mott-based neuromorphic hardware compatible with CMOS technology.

### [71] [Broad-band High-Energy Resolution Hard X-ray Spectroscopy using Transition Edge Sensors at SPring-8](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21846)
*Shinya Yamada,Yuto Ichinohe,Hideyuki Tatsuno,Ryota Hayakawa,Hirotaka Suda,Takaya Ohashi,Yoshitaka Ishisaki,Tomoya Uruga,Oki Sekizawa,Kiyofumi Nitta,Yoshio Takahashi,Takaaki Itai,Hiroki Suga,Makoto Nagasawa,Masato Tanaka,Minako Kurisu,Tadashi Hashimoto,Douglas Bennett,Ed Denison,William,Doriese,Malcolm Durkin,Joseph Fowler,Galen O'Neil,Kelsey Morgan,Dan Schmidt,Daniel Swetz,Joel Ullom,Leila Vale,Shinji Okada,Takuma Okumura,Toshiyuki Azuma,Toru Tamagawa,Tadaaki Isobe,Satoshi Kohjiro,Hirofumi Noda,Keigo Tanaka,Akimichi Taguchi,Yuki Imai,Kosuke Sato,Tasuku Hayashi,Teruhiko Kashiwabara,Kohei Sakata*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文成功在SPring-8同步辐射X射线光源上运行了过渡边缘传感器（transition-edge sensor, TES）光谱仪并评估其性能。该240像素系统（220像素同时工作）在6 keV处达到约4 eV的能量分辨率（1 c/s/pixel），在高计数率下（约2×10³ c/s/all pixels）分辨率约为5 eV。利用TES的宽波段光谱能力，实现了标准样品的多元素同时分析，并进行了荧光模式下的X射线吸收近边结构（XANES）分析。TES的高能量分辨率成功分辨了As Kα与Pb Lα₂的邻近谱线，并从气溶胶中检测到微量Fe信号。这些结果为硬X射线同步辐射装置中基于TES的高分辨率光谱学应用迈出了重要的第一步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在同步辐射光源中，常规探测器（如硅漂移探测器）的能量分辨率有限，难以分辨能量相近的荧光谱线（如As Kα与Pb Lα₂）以及检测微量或稀薄样品中的弱信号。因此，需要一种具有更高能量分辨率且兼具宽波段光谱能力的探测器，以实现更精确的多元素同时分析和X射线吸收近边结构（X-ray absorption near-edge structure, XANES）分析。

Method: 采用基于过渡边缘传感器（transition-edge sensor, TES）的240像素光谱仪系统（来自美国国家标准与技术研究院NIST），在SPring-8同步辐射光源上运行并评估其性能。在荧光模式下进行X射线吸收近边结构（XANES）分析，利用TES的高能量分辨率和宽波段光谱能力，对标准样品和气溶胶样品进行多元素同时检测与谱线分辨。

Result: 220像素同时运行时，在6 keV处能量分辨率约为4 eV（计数率约1 c/s/pixel）。在高计数率（约2×10³ c/s/all pixels）下，能量分辨率约为5 eV。成功分辨了标准样品中能量相近的As Kα与Pb Lα₂谱线，并获得了Pb Lα₂的XANES谱。从气溶胶样品中检测到微量Fe的X射线信号，并与空白靶的谱图明显区分。

Conclusion: 基于过渡边缘传感器（TES）的高分辨率光谱仪能够在硬X射线同步辐射装置中实现邻近谱线的清晰分辨和微量元素的灵敏检测，为后续TES光谱学在同步辐射领域的实际应用（如多元素分析和XANES分析）奠定了重要的第一步。

Abstract: We have succeeded in operating a transition-edge sensor (TES) spectrometer and evaluating its performance at the SPring-8 synchrotron X-ray light source. The TES spectrometer consists of a 240 pixel National Institute of Standards and Technology (NIST) TES system, and 220 pixels are operated simultaneously with an energy resolution of $4$~eV at 6~keV at a rate of about 1~c/s/pixel. The tolerance for high count rates is evaluated in terms of energy resolution and live time fraction, leading to an empirical compromise of about 2 x 10^3 c/s/all pixels with an energy resolution of 5 eV at 6 keV. By utilizing the TES's wide-band spectroscopic capability, simultaneous multi-element analysis is demonstrated for a standard sample. We conducted X-ray absorption near-edge structure (XANES) analysis in fluorescence mode using the TES spectrometer. The excellent energy resolution of the TES enabled us to detect weak fluorescence lines from dilute samples and trace elements that have previously been difficult to resolve due to the nearly overlapping emission lines of other dominant elements. The neighboring lines of As K alpha and Pb L alpha2 of the standard sample were clearly resolved and the XANES of Pb L alpha2 was obtained. Moreover, the X-ray spectrum from the small amount of Fe in aerosols was distinguished from the spectrum of a blank target, which helps us to understand the targets and the environment. These results are the first important step for the application of high resolution TES-based spectroscopy at hard X-ray synchrotron facilities.
