### [72] [Nanoscale Fluorescence Thermometry: Probes, Recent Advances and Emerging Directions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21186)
*Md Shakhawath Hossain,Nhat Minh Nguyen,Thi Ngoc Anh Mai,Trung Vuong Doan,Chaohao Chen,Qian Peter Su,Jiayan Liao,Yongliang Chen,Quynh Le-Van,Vu Khac Dat,Toan Dinh,Xiaoxue Xu,Toan Trong Tran*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过综述荧光纳米测温术，系统梳理其从荧光观测变量（包括光谱位置、强度、线宽及激发态动力学）中推断温度的基本机制，并评估不同材料平台与最新进展。

Result: 荧光纳米测温术已在纳米电子学、微流控及生物系统等领域实现了亚微米至纳米级精度的远程、空间分辨温度测量。

Abstract: The transition of materials and devices to nanometer, atomic, and quantum scales makes thermal characterization increasingly challenging, driving the need for advanced nanoscale thermometry. Fluorescence nanothermometry has emerged as a powerful approach, enabling remote, spatially resolved temperature measurements with sub-micrometer-to-nanometer precision across applications in nanoelectronics, microfluidics, and biological systems. In these systems, temperature is inferred from variations in fluorescence observables, including spectral position, intensity, linewidth, and excited-state dynamics. This review provides a comprehensive and critical overview of fluorescence nanothermometry, covering fundamental mechanisms, material platforms, recent advances, and emerging applications. It further presents a critical evaluation of key challenges and discusses emerging strategies and future research directions toward achieving robust, real-time thermometry. It is anticipated that this review will stimulate further advances in material platforms and system design, accelerating the development of accurate, scalable, and application-ready nanoscale thermometers.

### [73] [Analytic Inverse Design of Temporal Metamaterials via Space-Time Duality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21383)
*Giuseppe Castaldi,Marino Coppolaro,Massimo Moccia,Carlo Rizza,Nader Engheta,Vincenzo Galdi*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文针对时间超材料（temporal metamaterials）缺乏系统性设计方法的问题，基于时空对偶性（space-time duality）和一维空间逆散射理论（inverse scattering theory），发展了一套解析逆设计框架。通过将反射（后向波）和透射（前向波）响应设定为有理函数形式，直接得到封闭形式的物理可实现折射率调制（refractive-index modulations），避免了迭代优化，并实现了数学算子合成与滤波器设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间超材料虽能通过在时间上调制折射率来控制波传播，但尚缺乏系统化的设计方法论，现有方法难以直接获得具有指定功能响应的时间介质。

Method: 基于时空对偶性与一维空间逆散射理论，将反射（backward-wave）和透射（forward-wave）响应设定为有理函数（rational-function）形式，推导出封闭形式的物理可实现折射率调制，从而建立解析逆设计框架。

Result: 成功合成了数学算子（导数与积分）以及切比雪夫型（Chebyshev-type）和巴特沃斯型（Butterworth-type）滤波器，并通过时域有限差分（finite-difference time-domain, FDTD）模拟验证了结果的有效性。

Conclusion: 该工作为定制化功能响应与频谱响应的时间介质建立了一条通用路径，可应用于基于波的信号处理、可编程滤波以及受光子时间晶体（photonic time crystals）启发的放大方案。

Abstract: Temporal metamaterials, created by modulating the refractive index in time, offer powerful means of controlling wave propagation but still lack a systematic design methodology. Here, we develop an analytic inverse-design framework rooted in space-time duality and the established theory of one-dimensional spatial inverse scattering. By prescribing reflection (backward-wave) and transmission (forward-wave) responses in rational-function form, we obtain closed-form refractive-index modulations that are guaranteed to be physically admissible. This approach avoids iterative optimization and provides direct analytic control of the modulation. We illustrate the method with syntheses of mathematical operators, such as derivatives and integrals, as well as Chebyshev- and Butterworth-type filters, and validate the results through finite-difference time-domain simulations. Our findings establish a general route to temporal media with tailored functional and spectral responses, enabling applications in wave-based information processing, programmable filtering, and amplification schemes inspired by photonic time crystals.

</details>


### [74] [Modulation of Spin Angular Momentum of Emission in Symmetric 1D Plasmonic Crystals by Cathodoluminescence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21550)
*Yuxin Yang,Izzah Machfuudzoh,Qiwen Tan,Takumi Sannomiya*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文展示，尽管一维等离激元晶体（1D PlCs）在结构上是对称的，但通过扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）中的电子束相干激发过渡辐射与1D PlC模式的发射，其干涉可产生能量和动量分辨的圆偏振光（CPL），并揭示了CPL在纳米尺度的色散和空间依赖性；此外，与结构边界处表面等离极化激元散射的干涉还能通过激发位置调控CPL的产生效率。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）中的电子束相干激发一维等离激元晶体（1D PlCs）的过渡辐射（transition radiation）与模式发射（emission），通过二者的干涉产生能量和动量（发射角）分辨的圆偏振光（CPL）。同时，利用结构边界处表面等离极化激元（surface plasmon polariton, SPP）的散射干涉，通过改变激发位置沿平台（terrace）的坐标来调节CPL的产生效率。

Result: 在结构对称的一维等离激元晶体（1D PlCs）上成功实现了可控的圆偏振光（CPL）生成，获得了纳米尺度上CPL的色散（dispersion）和空间依赖性信息；通过调节激发位置，实现了CPL生成效率的调制。

Conclusion: 结构对称的一维等离激元晶体（1D PlCs）可作为可控圆偏振光（CPL）生成的平台，其纳米尺度的色散和空间依赖性为CPL的操控及等离激元器件（含相位信息）的设计提供了直接指导。

Abstract: The spin angular momentum (SAM) of light has become a cornerstone of numerous photonic applications, including optical communication and chiral photonics. Because SAM is inherently associated with circularly polarized light (CPL), the ability to modulate CPL in a controlled and efficient manner is essential not only for advancing fundamental studies of light-matter interactions but also for enabling next-generation photonic technologies. However, such modulation is commonly realized by structurally chiral systems, which inherently limits the feasibility of dynamic tuning. Here, we demonstrate that one-dimensional plasmonic crystals (1D PlCs), despite their structural symmetry, can serve as a platform for controllable CPL generation. By employing an electron beam in scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM), we coherently excite transition radiation and emission from 1D PlC modes. Their interference produces energy- and momentum- (emission angle-) resolved CPL, which clearly reveals its dispersion and spatial dependence at the nanoscale, providing direct guidance for its manipulation and offering insights into the design of plasmonic devices including the phase information. Furthermore, interference with surface plasmon polariton scattering at the structural boundary enables the efficiency modulation of CPL generation via the excitation position along the terrace.

### [75] [Sharpening New Physics Searches in Neutrino Oscillations with DUNE-PRISM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20951)
*Josu Hernández-García,Jacobo López-Pavón,Salvador Urrea*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了PRISM技术如何通过多离轴角测量来减轻中微子通量和核截面系统误差，显著恢复DUNE近探测器对非幺正性（non-unitarity）和惰性中微子（sterile neutrinos）的探测灵敏度，其中电子和μ子扇区改善显著，τ扇区因通量低于产生阈值而改善有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 下一代长基线中微子振荡实验（如DUNE）的物理潜力受限于中微子通量预测和中微子-原子核截面（neutrino-nucleus cross sections）的系统误差（systematic uncertainties），尤其在新物理搜寻中，信号表现为能谱的小畸变，对谱误差高度敏感。

Method: 采用PRISM（Precision Reaction Independent Spectrum Measurement）技术，通过多个离轴角（off-axis angles）的测量提供数据驱动的系统误差抑制手段，并自行生成了比DUNE合作组统计量更高的不同离轴角下的中微子与反中微子通量数据。

Result: PRISM能显著降低大系统误差的影响，将电子扇区和μ子扇区对非幺正性和惰性中微子的灵敏度恢复至接近小谱误差的水平；但τ扇区由于离轴通量主要低于τ产生阈值（τ production threshold），改善幅度有限。

Conclusion: PRISM技术能够有效缓解中微子振荡实验中的系统误差限制，增强新物理搜寻能力；研究提供的离轴通量数据作为辅助材料公开发布。

Abstract: Upcoming long-baseline neutrino oscillation experiments such as DUNE aim to achieve unprecedented precision, but their physics reach is ultimately constrained by systematic uncertainties in neutrino flux predictions and neutrino-nucleus cross sections. These limitations are especially critical for new-physics searches in neutrino oscillations at the near detector, including non-unitarity and sterile neutrinos, where the signal manifests as small distortions in the energy spectrum and is therefore highly sensitive to spectral uncertainties. The PRISM (Precision Reaction Independent Spectrum Measurement) technique offers a robust strategy to mitigate these effects by exploiting measurements at multiple off-axis angles, effectively providing a data-driven handle to reduce systematics. In this work, we demonstrate that PRISM can significantly reduce the impact of large systematic uncertainties, restoring sensitivity to non-unitarity and sterile neutrino scenarios in the electron and muon sectors to a level comparable to that obtained with small spectral uncertainties. We also include the results for the $τ$ sector with PRISM; however, in this case, since the majority of the flux measured at off-axis angles lies below the $τ$ production threshold, we find the improvement to be marginal. As part of this work, we have obtained neutrino and antineutrino fluxes for different off-axis angles with higher statistics than those provided by the DUNE collaboration. We make available these fluxes as auxiliary material to this manuscript.

</details>


### [76] [Improving the robustness of the $δ_{CP}$ determination with $ν$SCOPE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20956)
*João Paulo Pinheiro,Salvador Urrea*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究量化了DUNE和T2HK实验中，轻子CP破坏（leptonic CP violation）灵敏度对截面比理论假设的依赖程度；采用模型无关（model-agnostic）方法后发现灵敏度显著下降，而引入νSCOPE实验的精准截面测量后，损失的灵敏度基本得到恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轻子CP破坏（leptonic CP violation）的测量是未来长基线中微子实验（如DUNE和T2HK）的首要目标，但其关键参数δ_CP的提取依赖于近-远探测器外推以及对截面比σ_{ν_e}/σ_{ν_μ}和σ_{\barν_e}/σ_{\barν_μ}的理论假设（如轻子普适性（lepton universality）和核模型（nuclear modeling）），而这些假设的系统性影响尚未被充分量化。

Method: 采用模型无关（model-agnostic）、数据驱动（data-driven）的方法，对DUNE和T2HK实验中ν_e和\barν_e截面的系统性不确定性（systematic uncertainties）进行估计，以此评估灵敏度对理论假设的依赖程度；随后进一步评估加入νSCOPE实验（结合中微子标记（neutrino tagging）和窄带离轴技术（Narrow-Band Off-Axis technique））的截面测量对灵敏度的恢复效果。

Result: 采用模型无关方法后，DUNE和T2HK的CP破坏灵敏度显著下降：在最大CP破坏（maximal CP violation）处，DUNE的灵敏度降低近3σ，T2HK降低4σ。加入νSCOPE实验的测量后（可实现σ_{ν_μ}和σ_{\barν_μ}的百分级测量，并将σ_{ν_e}/σ_{ν_μ}比约束在约2%水平），损失的灵敏度基本得到恢复。

Conclusion: 高精度的外部截面测量可能对实现δ_CP的充分鲁棒测定（fully robust determination）以及打破其与核模型误建模（nuclear mis-modeling）或影响中微子探测的新物理（new physics）之间的简并（degeneracy）至关重要。

Abstract: The determination of leptonic CP violation is a primary goal of future long-baseline neutrino experiments such as DUNE and T2HK. The extraction of $δ_{\mathrm{CP}}$ relies on the near-to-far extrapolation and on the assumed knowledge of the cross-section ratios $σ_{ν_e}/σ_{ν_μ}$ and $σ_{\barν_e}/σ_{\barν_μ}$, which are typically inferred under theoretical assumptions such as lepton universality and depend on nuclear modeling. In this work, we quantify how much of the sensitivity of DUNE and T2HK arises from these assumptions by performing a model-agnostic, data-driven estimation of systematic uncertainties in $ν_e$ and $\barν_e$ cross sections. We find that adopting such an agnostic approach can substantially degrade the CP-violation sensitivity, reducing it by nearly $3σ$ at maximal CP violation for DUNE, and $4σ$ for T2HK. We then assess the impact of the proposed $ν$SCOPE experiment, which, through a combination of neutrino tagging and the Narrow-Band Off-Axis technique, can provide percent-level measurements of $σ_{ν_μ}$ and $σ_{\barν_μ}$ and constrain the ratio $σ_{ν_e}/σ_{ν_μ}$ at the $\sim 2\%$ level. We show that including prospective $ν$SCOPE measurements largely restores the lost sensitivity, highlighting that precise external cross-section measurements may be essential for a fully robust determination of $δ_{\mathrm{CP}}$ and for breaking its degeneracy with nuclear mis-modeling or possible new physics affecting neutrino detection.

</details>


### [77] [Kitchen Sink Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20965)
*Ranit Das,Marie Hein,Gregor Kasieczka,Michael Krämer,Lukas Lang,Radha Mastandrea,Louis Moureaux,Alexander Mück,David Shih*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究针对共振异常检测（resonant anomaly detection）方法中现有基准信号模型单一、观测量选择存在模型依赖与灵敏度折衷两大局限，提出了新的模拟信号基准（simulated signal benchmark）数据集，并探索了一种结合能量流多项式（Energy Flow Polynomials, EFPs）与子喷注变量（subjettiness）的“厨房水槽”（kitchen sink）可观测量集。实验表明，该可观测量集在理想异常检测器（anomaly detector）与CWoLa搜索任务中均表现出最广泛的信号灵敏度；此外，一种基于属性装袋（attribute bagging）的变体方法能在显著降低训练成本的同时保持可比的异常检测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有共振异常检测研究存在两大局限：一是仅依赖极少数模拟信号基准模型（simulated signal benchmark models），缺乏多样性；二是观测量选择面临两难——使用精心设计的高阶喷注子结构观测量（jet substructure observables）性能优异但易产生模型依赖（model dependence），而使用全对撞事件相空间（full collider event phase space）虽更具不可知性（agnostic）却灵敏度不足。本文旨在同时克服这两个局限。

Method: 作者制定了一系列新的模拟信号基准，并以与LHCO R&D基准完全兼容的格式公开提供；同时构建了一种由能量流多项式（Energy Flow Polynomials, EFPs）与子喷注变量（subjettiness）组成的高水平且高度不可知（highly agnostic）的可观测量集（称为“厨房水槽”集）。将该可观测量集应用于理想异常检测器（idealized anomaly detector）与CWoLa狩猎任务（CWoLa hunting task），并与三个基线可观测量集（Baseline LHC Olympics集、子喷注变量集、能量流多项式集）进行对比。此外，还测试了一种属性装袋（attribute bagging）变体，每个集成成员（ensemble member）在喷注子结构观测量的随机子集上训练。

Result: “厨房水槽”可观测量集对广泛类型的信号展现出最高的灵敏度。属性装袋变体方法能够达到与完整可观测量集可比的异常检测性能，同时显著降低了训练成本（training cost）。

Conclusion: 本文提出的新信号基准和“厨房水槽”可观测量集有效弥补了现有共振异常检测研究中基准单一与观测量选择折衷的不足；属性装袋策略为在不牺牲检测性能的前提下降低计算开销提供了可行方案。

Abstract: An enormous amount of R&D effort has resulted in many new resonant anomaly detection methods being proposed in recent years. However, the vast majority of previous R&D studies have suffered from two limitations: they have focused on a very small set of simulated signal benchmark models; and they have either used small sets of carefully crafted high-level jet substructure observables, which can be highly performant but are prone to model dependence, or the full collider event phase space, which is more agnostic but suffers from reduced sensitivity. In this work, we address both limitations: we formulate a number of new simulated signal benchmarks, which we make publicly available in a format fully compatible with the LHCO R&D benchmark; and we explore a high-level, yet highly agnostic, observable set consisting of Energy Flow Polynomials in addition to the usual subjettiness variables. We evaluate this "kitchen sink" observable set for both an idealized anomaly detector and the CWoLa hunting task, along with three baseline observable sets (the Baseline LHC Olympics set, subjettiness observables, and Energy Flow Polynomials). We find that our kitchen sink approach is the most sensitive to a broad range of signal types. Furthermore, we show that an attribute bagging variant, in which each ensemble member is trained on a random subset of substructure observables, yields comparable anomaly detection performance while significantly reducing training cost.

</details>


### [78] [Masked-Token Prediction for Anomaly Detection at the Large Hadron Collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21035)
*Ambre Visive,Roberto Ruiz de Austri,Polina Moskvitina,Clara Nellist,Sascha Caron*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次将来自大语言模型的掩码词元预测（masked-token prediction）技术应用于高能物理（High Energy Physics）中的异常检测（anomaly detection）。通过仅在背景事件上训练的轻量编码器（encoder）学习标准模型（Standard Model, SM）物理结构，在推理阶段标记偏离该学习的序列为异常。在四顶夸克产生（four-top-quark production）和超对称胶子对产生（supersymmetric gluino pair production）两类搜索任务上评估，验证了该方法对微小偏差的敏感性，并发现基于深度学习的词元化（tokenization）策略（如VQ-VAE）显著优于查表法。该方法在标准模型背景上训练后可迁移至不同BSM搜索，实现可扩展、模型无关的低计算成本异常检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理中的异常检测需要在对信号（signal）完全未知的情况下，从压倒性背景（background）中识别出罕见信号。传统方法依赖对特定新物理信号的预先假设，缺乏模型无关（model-independent）的通用检测能力。本文旨在利用大语言模型中成熟的掩码词元预测技术，开发一种仅需背景样本训练的轻量级异常检测方法，从而降低对新物理信号的先验依赖，并提升检测的可扩展性。

Method: 采用轻量编码器（encoder）架构，仅使用标准模型背景事件进行训练，通过掩码词元预测（masked-token prediction）任务学习背景数据的结构。推理时，将偏离该学习结构的序列标记为异常。词元化（tokenization）通过两种策略实现：基于向量量化变分自编码器（vector-quantized variational autoencoder, VQ-VAE）的深度学习方法，以及传统的查表词元化（look-up table tokenization）。

Result: 在四顶夸克产生和超对称胶子对产生两类搜索任务上，该方法均表现出色，尤其在四顶夸克（与背景极为相似）信号上展现了良好的敏感性。深度学习的VQ-VAE词元化策略在性能上显著优于查表词元化。与现有异常检测基线的对比验证了方法的鲁棒性（robustness）。此外，模型在标准模型背景上训练后可迁移至不同的BSM搜索任务。

Conclusion: 研究表明，基于词元（token）的对撞机数据表示与变换器（transformer）架构相结合，在发现新物理（new-physics）方面具有巨大潜力。该方法一旦在SM背景上完成训练，即可迁移至多种不同的BSM搜索场景，实现可扩展、模型无关的异常检测，同时显著降低计算成本。

Abstract: Anomaly detection in High Energy Physics requires identifying rare signals against overwhelming backgrounds, without prior knowledge of the signal. We present the first application of masked-token prediction, a technique from Large Language Models, to this problem. A lightweight encoder architecture trained solely on background events captures the structure of Standard Model (SM) physics; at inference, sequences deviating from this learned structure are flagged as anomalous. We evaluate the approach on searches for four-top-quark production and supersymmetric gluino pair production, both featuring top-rich final states with substantial missing transverse energy, covering SM and beyond the Standard Model (BSM) scenarios. Strong performance on the four-top signature, which closely resembles background, demonstrates the method's sensitivity to subtle deviations. We further show that the tokenization strategy significantly impacts performance: deep-learned tokenization via vector-quantized variational autoencoders (VQ-VAE) outperforms look-up table tokenization. Comparison with established anomaly detection baselines confirms robustness. These results highlight the potential of token-based collider data representations combined with transformer architectures for new-physics discovery. Once trained on SM background, the model transfers across different BSM searches, enabling scalable, model-independent anomaly detection at reduced computational cost.

</details>


### [79] [Neutron Portal and Dark Matter-Baryon Coincidence: from UV Completion to Phenomenology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21168)
*Sudhakantha Girmohanta,Yuichiro Nakai,Yoshihiro Shigekami,Zhihao Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于中子门户算子（neutron portal operator）提出了一种暗物质-重子巧合问题的动力学解决方案，该方案通过一个强过冷的暗色禁闭相变（dark confinement phase transition）同时解释脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing arrays）观测到的纳赫兹随机引力波信号，并产生宇宙中的暗物质与重子不对称性。暗物质质量尺度与中子门户截断尺度通过紫外完备（ultraviolet completion）自然关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决暗物质-重子巧合问题（dark matter-baryon coincidence problem），即解释为何暗物质与普通重子的能量密度处于同一量级。同时，为脉冲星计时阵列观测到的纳赫兹随机引力波信号提供动力学起源。

Method: 引入中子门户算子连接可见区与暗区的不对称性（asymmetry）；构建紫外完备模型（包括树图和圈图两种方案）；利用近似不动点（approximate fixed point）控制暗区动力学，并在重门户态被积掉后引发暗色禁闭相变，动力学产生GeV量级的尺度。

Result: 不对称暗物质（asymmetric dark matter）的GeV质量尺度可通过紫外完备自然关联到中子门户的（多）TeV截断尺度；禁闭相变尺度与有效中子门户尺度之间存在明确联系。

Conclusion: 该框架为暗物质-重子巧合问题提供了动力学解释，同时与脉冲星计时阵列引力波信号兼容；论文还讨论了束流打靶实验（beam dump searches）和对撞机实验中探测中子门户的约束与前景。

Abstract: We present a dynamical solution to the dark matter-baryon coincidence problem based on the neutron portal operator connecting the visible and dark sector asymmetries. This framework is motivated by the possibility that a strongly supercooled dark confinement phase transition accounts for the nano-Hz stochastic gravitational wave signal observed by pulsar timing arrays, while also generating the dark matter and baryon asymmetry in the Universe. We show that the GeV-scale mass of asymmetric dark matter can be naturally correlated with the (multi-)TeV scale cut-off for the neutron portal through its ultraviolet completion. The dark sector is governed by an approximate fixed point and confines once the heavy portal states are integrated out, dynamically generating a scale of $\mathcal{O} ({\rm GeV})$. We analyze both tree and loop-level ultraviolet completions and demonstrate how the resulting confinement scale is linked to the effective neutron portal scale. We also discuss cosmological constraints and experimental prospects in beam dump searches and colliders for probing the neutron portal.

</details>


### [80] [Odd Physics Off the Diagonal: Constraining CP-violating SMEFT with Quantum Tomography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21857)
*Avalon Roberts,Patrick Dougan,Alexander Oh,Savanna Shaw*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用量子断层扫描（Quantum Tomography）技术重建双玻色子系统的自旋密度矩阵，以超越标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）中电荷宇称（CP）破坏效应的传统分析方法，实现对CP奇偶贡献的联合灵敏约束，包括纯二次新物理（NP）项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型（SM）中的CP破坏源不足以解释宇宙中的正反物质不对称性，需要引入新的CP破坏物理。然而SMEFT中的CP破坏信号在偏振不敏感的可观测量中与CP守恒算符高度简并，仅能在方位角衰变角中通过SM-NP干涉区分，传统方法信息利用不充分。

Method: 采用量子断层扫描技术，重建双玻色子体系的自旋密度矩阵（spin density matrix, SDM），从而提取超越“干涉复活”（interference resurrection）的完整新物理信号，包括纯二次NP项。

Result: 该方法对CP偶和CP奇贡献的特征提供了优越的同时敏感度，能够捕捉传统角度可观测量无法完全涵盖的效应。

Conclusion: 基于自旋密度矩阵重建的量子断层扫描方法，能够更充分地利用SMEFT中的CP破坏信息，为探测超出标准模型的新物理提供更强有力的约束工具。

Abstract: New sources of charge-parity (CP) violation beyond those described in the Standard Model (SM) are required to explain the observed matter--antimatter asymmetry of the Universe. The Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT) provides a framework to introduce additional electroweak sources of CP-odd physics in a model-independent manner. However, these CP-violating signatures are mostly degenerate to CP-even SMEFT operators in polarisation-blind observables, distinguishable only in the SM-New Physics (NP) interference using the azimuthal decay angle. Using Quantum Tomography techniques, we present a new approach to constraining these NP effects. Reconstructing the spin density matrix (SDM) of a diboson system, we go beyond `interference resurrection' to exploit the full signature of the Beyond-SM physics, including the pure quadratic NP terms. We show that this approach provides superior simultaneous sensitivity to characteristic features of CP-even and CP-odd contributions, including effects not fully captured by traditional angular observables.

</details>

Abstract: Ultra high energy cosmic rays have been see coming from the direction of the local cosmic void. ### [82] [Disentangling new physics with quantum entanglement in $t\bar{t}$ production at future lepton colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21332)
*Masato Arai,Kentarou Mawatari,Nobuchika Okada*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了未来轻子对撞机（如ILC和多TeV缪子对撞机）中顶夸克对（top-antitop pair）产生的量子纠缠（quantum entanglement）与贝尔不等式（Bell inequality）破坏现象，并在标准模型（SM）及三种新物理扩展模型（标量中介、$U(1)_{B-L}$规范模型、Randall-Sundrum额外维）下评估了纠缠标记（entanglement marker）、并发性（concurrence）和最大CHSH参数等量子信息可观测量，发现新物理可导致显著偏离标准模型的纠缠行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索未来轻子对撞机中顶夸克对产生过程中的量子纠缠与贝尔不等式破坏，并检验它们能否作为探测新中性相互作用和额外维动力学（extra-dimensional dynamics）的灵敏探针。

Method: 在标准模型中通过$s$道$\gamma$和$Z$玻色子交换描述顶夸克对产生，并在三种新物理扩展——标量中介（scalar mediator）、最小$U(1)_{B-L}$规范模型（引入$Z'$玻色子）和Randall-Sundrum（RS）情景（引入Kaluza-Klein引力子）——下计算量子信息可观测量，包括纠缠标记、并发性和最大Clauser-Horne-Shimony-Holt（CHSH）参数，分析其对质心能量、散射角和模型参数的依赖。

Result: 相对于标准模型预期，标量中介情景中纠缠通常被减弱；而在$U(1)_{B-L}$和Randall-Sundrum情景中，在现象学相关参数区域内，纠缠会出现显著偏差。

Conclusion: 量子信息可观测量有潜力成为未来轻子对撞机中探测新中性相互作用和额外维动力学的高灵敏探针。

Abstract: We investigate quantum entanglement and Bell-inequality violation in top-antitop pair production at future lepton colliders such as the International Linear Collider (ILC) and multi-TeV muon colliders. Within the Standard Model (SM), the process proceeds through $s$-channel $γ$ and $Z$ exchange and exhibits characteristic spin-correlation patterns that encode a non-trivial amount of entanglement. We then examine how these features are modified in several well-motivated extensions of the SM:(i) a neutral scalar mediator that couples to charged leptons and top quarks via Yukawa interactions and contributes as an additional $s$-channel exchange; (ii) the minimal gauged $U(1)_{B-L}$ model, which introduces a new neutral gauge boson $Z'$ coupling vectorially to SM fermions; and (iii) a Randall-Sundrum scenario, in which the exchange of massive Kaluza-Klein gravitons arising from a warped extra dimension induces additional spin-dependent interactions. For all cases, we evaluate quantum-information observables, including the entanglement marker, the concurrence, and the maximal Clauser-Horne-Shimony-Holt parameter, and study their dependence on the center-of-mass energy, scattering angle, and model parameters. We find that, relative to the SM expectation, the entanglement is typically reduced in the scalar-mediator scenario, while sizable deviations can arise in the $U(1)_{B-L}$ and Randall-Sundrum cases for phenomenologically relevant regions of parameter space. These results demonstrate the potential of quantum-information observables as sensitive probes of new neutral interactions and extra-dimensional dynamics in future lepton colliders.

</details>


### [83] [Heavy Quark Transport is Non-Gaussian Beyond Leading Log](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21895)
*Jean F. Du Plessis,Bruno Scheihing-Hitschfeld*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过计算弱耦合非阿贝尔等离子体中相对论性重夸克的领头阶动量转移核，发现超出领头对数阶的重夸克输运本质上是非高斯的：纵向动量转移分布具有不对称的指数尾部，这对平衡动力学至关重要。这一结构此前在强耦合全息等离子体中被发现，表明它并非弱/强耦合、共形性或超对称性所特有，因此物理夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）也应展现这一稳健特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解弱耦合下重夸克输运中超出领头对数（leading logarithm）阶的行为，探究其是否仍满足标准的高斯（Gaussian）扩散图像，并检验该行为在不同耦合强度体系下的普适性。

Method: 在弱耦合非阿贝尔等离子体（non-Abelian plasma）中，计算相对论性重夸克的领头阶动量转移核（leading-order momentum transfer kernel），并对热尺度（thermal scale）上的微扰动量转移与通过硬热圈重求和（hard-thermal-loop resummation）修正的软物理进行匹配。

Result: 发现纵向动量转移分布具有不对称的指数尾部（asymmetric exponential tails），该尾部对平衡动力学至关重要；且这一结构此前已在强耦合全息等离子体（holographic plasma）中被发现。

Conclusion: 该非高斯输运特征并非弱耦合或强耦合、共形性（conformality）或超对称性（supersymmetry）所特有，因此物理夸克-胶子等离子体也应展现这一稳健（robust）特征。

Abstract: We find that heavy quark transport beyond leading logarithm at weak coupling is intrinsically non-Gaussian: the longitudinal momentum transfer distribution has asymmetric exponential tails that are crucial for equilibration dynamics. We show this by computing the leading-order momentum transfer kernel for relativistic heavy quarks in weakly coupled non-Abelian plasmas, matching perturbative momentum transfer on the thermal scale to hard-thermal-loop-resummed soft physics. This is the same structure previously found in strongly coupled holographic plasmas, showing that it is not peculiar to weak or strong coupling, conformality, or supersymmetry. We therefore expect that this is a robust feature that physical quark-gluon plasma should also exhibit.

### [84] [The two-level systems in cryogenic solids, or how to avoid stressful memories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21109)
*Vassiliy Lubchenko*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文揭示了“双能级系统（two-level systems, TLSs）”在结构玻璃中的普遍存在与其在不同稳定玻璃材料中的差异表现，提出TLS的缺失意味着构型熵（configurational entropy）降低，并通过比较淬火玻璃、超稳定气相沉积薄膜、Swap Monte Carlo模拟玻璃及天然琥珀，指出焓稳定（enthalpic stabilization）可能通过增键（increased bonding）而非单纯老化（ageing）实现，同时评论了TLS合作性（cooperativity）方面的现有理论争议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 结构玻璃中普遍存在的低能激发（“双能级系统”，TLS）的起源与调控机制长期未解；特别是近期实验发现超稳定玻璃（ultrastable glasses）中TLS数量大幅减少，而同样焓稳定的天然琥珀中TLS却持续存在，这一矛盾亟需理论解释。

Method: 本文为理论分析与评述性研究，基于文献中淬火玻璃、气相沉积超稳定玻璃薄膜、Swap Monte Carlo模拟玻璃及天然琥珀的已有实验结果，通过构型熵和焓稳定性两个维度进行对比分析，并提出关于TLS合作性争议的评注及验证性实验建议。

Result: TLS的减少意味着材料的构型熵低于传统淬火玻璃；琥珀虽焓稳定，但TLS并未减少，推测其焓稳定来自增键而非老化；现有关于TLS合作性（cooperativity）的多种理论预测之间存在不一致。

Conclusion: TLS的缺失与构型熵降低相关，但焓稳定并不必然导致TLS减少——关键在于稳定化的微观机制（老化降熵 vs. 增键）；需进一步实验验证以上图景并厘清TLS合作性的争议。

Abstract: Structural glasses prepared by bulk quenching a liquid melt universally exhibit puzzling low-energy excitations commonly known as the ``two-level systems'' (TLSs). Recent studies indicate that ultrastable glassy films made by vapor deposition exhibit substantially fewer TLSs and, at the same time, are more stable enthalpically than conventional glasses made by quenching a melt. A similar phenomenon is observed in very stable glasses of model liquid mixtures prepared using swap Monte Carlo sampling. However, in a separate set of enthalpically stable solids, exemplified by amber matured over geological times, the two-level systems persist. In addressing this seeming conflict, we emphasize that a depletion of the TLSs, if any, means the configurational entropy of the material is lower than that of conventional glasses made by bulk-quenching a melt. Ageing does induce reduction in configurational entropy, but amber, we speculate, achieves enthalpic stabilization through increased bonding, not ageing. We separately comment on the discrepancy among existing predictions for the extent of cooperativity of the two-level systems. Several experiments are suggested to test the present picture.

### [85] [Fate of the Unbound States in Near-infinitely Deep Potential Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21281)
*Shujie Cheng,Tong Liu,Gao Xianlong*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文基于一维准周期近无限深势阱模型，研究势阱深度和非厄米性（non-Hermiticity）对非束缚态（unbound states）的影响。通过扩展Liu-Xia模型至更深结构，结合反参与率（IPR）计算与Avila全局理论（Avila's global theory），证实即使在更深势阱中，特定能量区间仍存在非束缚态。在引入增益-损耗效应的非厄米系统中，非束缚态以束缚态与非束缚态混合的形式存在，但混合区域与纯束缚态区域之间存在清晰能量边界，该边界可由Avila全局理论证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在准周期近无限深势阱这一极端势场条件下，势阱深度与非厄米性如何影响非束缚态的存在行为，为非束缚态在极端势场中的物理规律提供新见解。

Method: 采用一维准周期近无限深势阱模型，在Liu-Xia模型基础上扩展至更深势阱结构；通过计算反参与率（IPR）并基于Avila全局理论（Avila's global theory）进行理论分析；进一步将研究拓展至具有增益-损耗效应的非厄米系统。

Result: 在更深势阱中，特定能量区间内仍存在非束缚态；在非厄米系统中，非束缚态以束缚态（bound states）与非束缚态混合态的形式出现；混合区域与纯束缚态区域之间存在清晰且可证明的能量边界。

Conclusion: 势阱深度增大并未完全消除非束缚态的存在，非厄米性诱导了混合态形式的非束缚态行为，Avila全局理论可有效证明能量边界的成立，研究成果为极端势场中非束缚态的理解提供了新视角。

Abstract: Based on the one-dimensional model with quasi-periodicity and nearly infinite depth potential well, this paper studies how the depth of the potential well and non-Hermiticity affects the unbound states. By extending the Liu-Xia model to a deeper structure, we confirm through calculating IPR and based on Avila's global theory, that although the potential well is deeper, there are still unbound states within specific energy intervals. Extending the research to non-Hermitian systems with gain-loss effects, we find that the non-Hermiticity leads to the existence of unbound states in a mixed state form composed of bound states and unbounded states. However, there are clear energy boundaries between the mixed regions with unbound states and the pure bound state regions, which can be proved by Avila's global theory. Our research results provide new insights into the unbound states in extreme potential fields.

### [86] [Cracking Gravitational Wave Multiple Ringdown Modes in Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20914)
*Ziming Wang,Han Wang,Yuxin Yang,Yiming Dong,Hai-Tian Wang,Yi-Ming Hu,Lijing Shao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文开发了一套面向空间引力波探测器的铃宕（ringdown）分析流程，通过引入FIREFLY加速算法，首次证明其与时间延迟干涉（TDI）可观测量的兼容性，并在包含六个准正则模（quasi-normal modes）的模拟信号上实现了约200倍的加速效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来空间引力波探测器将接收来自大质量黑洞并合（massive BH binary coalescences）的铃宕信号并解析多个模态，导致计算负担急剧增加，亟需高效的铃宕分析方法来缓解这一问题。

Method: 将在地面探测器上已验证的加速算法FIREFLY应用于空间探测器场景，结合时间延迟干涉（TDI）可观测量构建了一套实用的铃宕分析流程。

Result: 在包含六个准正则模的模拟铃宕信号上，该方法实现了约200倍的计算加速，且保持了高保真度（high fidelity）。

Conclusion: 该新方法具有良好的统计解释性（sound statistical interpretation），可用于空间环境下的多模态铃宕分析，并且可扩展到频带内的其他引力波（GW）源。

Abstract: Ringdown signals from perturbed black holes (BHs) offer a clean window into BH spacetime, strong-field gravity, and fundamental physics. Presently the quasi-normal modes of stellar-mass BH ringdowns have been successfully extracted in the ground-based gravitational wave (GW) observations. Looking ahead, the future space-borne observatories will listen to the ringdowns from massive BH binary coalescences more loudly and resolve multiple modes to unprecedented precision, which calls for efficient approaches to mitigate the sharply increasing computational burden. We develop a practical ringdown analysis pipeline for space-borne detectors by implementing FIREFLY, a novel acceleration algorithm validated in ground-based detectors, and for the first time demonstrate its compatibility and effectiveness with the time-delay interferometry (TDI) observables. With high fidelity, we achieve a $\sim 200$-fold speedup for a simulated ringdown signal including six modes, providing a viable and scalable route for multi-mode ringdown analysis in the space context. This new approach has sound statistical interpretation and is extensible to other GW sources in band.

### [87] [Smoking Gun Signatures of Quasilocal Probability in Black Hole Ringdowns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20922)
*Oem Trivedi,Alfredo Gurrola,Robert J. Scherrer*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文将曲直时空中的准局域概率（quasilocal probability）思想应用于黑洞振铃（black hole ringdown），揭示了由视界诱导的概率流（probability flux）导致的非厄米动力学（non-Hermitian dynamics）产生的三种可观测特征，并论证了这些特征组合可作为准局域概率的稳健鉴别器，同时指出黑洞振铃是检验量子力学厄米性（Hermiticity）是否在量子引力中为基本属性还是涌现对称性的新领域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在先前提出的弯曲时空中准局域概率概念的基础上，发展其对黑洞振铃的观测意义，旨在通过可观测信号检验量子力学中厄米性的根本性及量子引力中可能涌现的对称性。

Method: 通过分析视界诱导的概率流所引致的有效非厄米动力学，推导出三种可观测特征：关联的多模偏差（correlated multi-mode deviations）、弱振幅依赖性（weak amplitude dependence）以及波形阻尼与能量核算之间的失配（mismatch between waveform damping and energy accounting）。这些效应源于单一的边界通量机制（boundary-flux mechanism），从而呈现出受约束的低维结构。

Result: 三种特征虽可分别被其他修改引力理论（modified gravity）模拟，但其组合模式构成准局域概率的稳健鉴别器；未来的引力波观测能以有意义的精度探测这些信号。

Conclusion: 黑洞振铃为检验量子力学厄米性究竟是基本属性还是量子引力中的涌现对称性提供了新的试验场。

Abstract: Building on recent work introducing the idea of Quasilocal Probability in curved spacetime, we develop its observational implications for black hole ringdown in detail. We show that horizon-induced probability flux leads to an effective non-Hermitian dynamics producing three distinctive signatures, which are correlated multi-mode deviations, weak amplitude dependence and a mismatch between waveform damping and energy accounting. These effects arise from a single boundary-flux mechanism and therefore exhibit a constrained, low-dimensional structure not expected in generic modified gravity scenarios. We demonstrate that while individual deviations may be mimicked, their combined pattern provides a robust discriminator of quasilocal probability. We further argue that upcoming gravitational wave observations can probe these signatures at meaningful precision. We also establish that black hole ringdown is a novel arena to test whether quantum mechanical Hermiticity is really a fundamental property or an emergent symmetry in quantum gravity.

### [88] [Radial adiabatic perturbations of stellar compact objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20960)
*Paulo Luz,Sante Carloni*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在广义相对论（general relativity）框架下，建立了自引力非耗散非完美流体径向绝热线性扰动理论的协变且规范不变形式；通过将热力学性质编码为状态方程和涉及物质与运动学变量的各向异性压强的假设，获得了适用于多种热力学理论的一组方程；并基于新爱因斯坦场方程解和因果性约束，提出了动态稳定恒星的最大致密性上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有广义相对论中的流体扰动理论在处理非完美流体（imperfect fluids）时缺乏协变且规范不变（covariant and gauge-invariant）的统一表述，难以直接应用于多种热力学理论的比较与稳定性分析。

Method: 将热力学性质编码为状态方程（equation of state）和涉及物质与运动学变量的各向异性压强（anisotropic pressure）假设，推导出适用于多种热力学理论的扰动方程；引入新的爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein field equations）解，并施加因果性（causality）约束。

Result: 以Eckart理论、Bemfica-Disconzi-Noronha-Kovtun理论和截断Israel-Stewart理论为例，评估并比较了它们对致密恒星径向绝热扰动的演化预测；基于新解和因果性约束，提出了动态稳定恒星的致密性（compactness）上限。

Conclusion: 所建立的协变规范不变框架能统一描述多种热力学理论下非完美流体的扰动行为，且新的致密性上限为存在非平凡径向和切向压强的动态稳定恒星提供了理论约束。

Abstract: We present a covariant and gauge-invariant formulation of the theory of radial adiabatic linear perturbations of self-gravitating, non-dissipative imperfect fluids within the theory of general relativity. By codifying the thermodynamical properties of the source into an equation of state and an ansatz on anisotropic pressure that involves both matter and kinematic variables, we obtain a set of equations that is directly applicable to a wide variety of thermodynamic theories for matter fields. As examples, we evaluate and compare the predictions of the Eckart theory, the Bemfica-Disconzi-Noronha-Kovtun theory, and the Truncated Israel-Stewart theory on the properties and evolution of radial adiabatic perturbations of stellar compact objects modeled by classical equilibrium solutions. Introducing a new solution of the Einstein field equations, and imposing causality, we propose an upper bound for the maximum compactness of dynamically stable stars with non-trivial radial and tangential pressures.

</details>


### [89] [Spontaneous Symmetry Breaking and the Vacuum Displacement Principle: From Galactic Scales to Cosmic Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21050)
*Rodrigo Maier*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 提出一种修正引力框架，将真空建模为经历自发对称破缺的希格斯型标量场。通过引入重子物质与真空基底的耦合，产生恢复性浮力修正测地线方程并弱等效原理。该机制在真空极限下恢复史瓦西度规，在物质存在下提供汤川修正的牛顿势，从而解释平坦星系旋转曲线和宇宙学常数的追踪机制，无需引入暗物质或暗能量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统引力理论在解释星系旋转曲线和宇宙学常数问题时通常需要引入暗物质（dark matter）和暗能量（dark energy）等暗扇区（dark sectors），但这些假设面临巧合问题（coincidence problem）和精细调节问题（fine-tuning problem）。本文旨在探索一种无需暗扇区的修正引力框架。

Method: 将真空建模为经历自发对称破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）的希格斯型标量场（Higgs-type scalar field）χ，并通过引入耦合项 $Q^ν= αT \nabla^νχ$ 形式化了一个“位移原理”（displacement principle），将重子物质（baryonic matter）视为真空基底中的杂质。该相互作用产生恢复性浮力（restorative buoyancy force），修正测地线方程（geodesic equation）并导致弱等效原理（Weak Equivalence Principle）的违反。

Result: 该机制在真空极限下自然恢复史瓦西度规（Schwarzschild metric），在存在物质时提供汤川修正的牛顿势（Yukawa-corrected Newtonian potential）。该修正能够动态解释平坦星系旋转曲线（flat galactic rotation curves），并为宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）提供追踪机制（tracking mechanism）。

Conclusion: 该框架有望在无需引入暗扇区的前提下，同时解决平坦星系旋转曲线问题和宇宙学常数的巧合问题与精细调节问题，为修正引力理论提供了一条新的路径。

Abstract: We present a modified gravity framework where the vacuum is modeled as a Higgs-type scalar field $χ$ undergoing spontaneous symmetry breaking. By introducing a coupling $Q^ν= αT \nabla^νχ$, we formalize a displacement principle where baryonic matter acts as an impurity in the vacuum substrate. This interaction leads to a restorative buoyancy force that modifies the geodesic equation and violates the Weak Equivalence Principle. We show that this mechanism naturally recovers the Schwarzschild metric in the vacuum limit while providing a Yukawa-corrected Newtonian potential in the presence of matter. This correction offers a dynamical explanation for flat galactic rotation curves and a tracking mechanism for the cosmological constant, potentially resolving the coincidence and fine-tuning problems without the need of dark sectors.

We further analyze the characteristics of the derived cosmological model. *Mohamed Aarif A,Soumya Chakrabarti*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Chiellini可积框架下研究了理想流体与空间均匀标量场混合系统的引力坍缩，推导了封闭解析解，发现系统呈现出渐近坍缩行为（proper volume单调递减但有限时间内不为零），并分析了能量条件、视界形成及内外解的匹配问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非相互作用理想流体与空间均匀标量场混合系统在引力坍缩中的动力学行为，利用Chiellini可积性获得解析解，以更深入地理解标量场在引力坍缩过程中的角色及奇点形成机制。

Method: 选取扩展Higgs型自相互作用势，将Klein-Gordon方程约化为广义阻尼Milne-Pinney型微分方程；利用Chiellini可积框架推导标量场及尺度因子的闭合形式解析解；通过Israel-Darmois连接条件将内部均匀解匹配至广义Vaidya外部解。

Result: 标量场保持正则（canonical）性质；理想流体可违反零能量条件（Null Energy Condition）；坍缩分支中proper volume单调递减但有限时间不趋于零；参数空间中存在无捕获面或多表观视界（apparent horizon）等多种可能性。

Conclusion: 该系统呈现出渐近坍缩（asymptotic collapse）行为，避免了有限时间奇点形成；能量条件与视界结构的多样性表明标量场-流体混合系统在引力坍缩中具有丰富的动力学特征，内外解的成功匹配确保了坍缩场景的连续性。

Abstract: We study the gravitational collapse of a non-interacting mix of perfect fluid and a spatially homogeneous scalar field within a Chiellini-integrable framework. We choose an extended Higgs-type self-interaction potential and reduce the Klein-Gordon equation into a generalized damped Milne-Pinney class of differential equation. We derive a closed-form analytical solution for the scalar field, the scale factor and explore the collapsing branch of the same. We find that it exhibits an asymptotic collapse in which the proper volume decreases monotonically but never reaches zero at finite time. We analyze the energy conditions for the constituent elements of the collapsing sphere. While the scalar field remains canonical in nature, we find that the perfect fluid can violated the Null Energy Condition. We also study the formation of apparent horizon condition and find multiple possibilities depending on the parameter space : either no trapped surface or the formation of multiple apparent horizons. We match the interior homogeneous solution to a generalized Vaidya exterior via the Israel-Darmois junction conditions, yielding the corresponding boundary mass function, ensuring a smooth collapse scenario.

### [93] [Non-Equilibrium Physics of Thermodynamicized Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21166)
*Wen-Xiang Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一个非平衡框架（non-equilibrium framework）用于热力学化黑洞，通过熵泛函原理、基于留数（residue）的欧几里得轮廓方法以及拓扑留数分类，统一描述熵产生对奇异作用量的贡献，并在Kerr-Newman型黑洞的f(R)引力中给出平衡与非平衡修正结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞热力学框架主要局限于平衡态，无法处理具有物质、电荷和旋转通量（flux）的动态驱动黑洞系统。本文旨在将熵泛函诠释（entropy-functional interpretation）与留数方法结合，建立能够包含不可逆熵产生（irreversible entropy production）的非平衡形式。

Method: 方法包括三个核心部分：(1) 熵泛函原理（entropy functional principle）用于选择物理的在壳背景（on-shell backgrounds）；(2) 基于简单极点奇异性（simple pole singularities）的欧几里得与等温线（contour）描述视界温度；(3) 多视界黑洞构型的拓扑留数分类（topological residue classification）。在此基础上构建准静态非平衡配分泛函（quasi-stationary non-equilibrium partition functional），其中不可逆熵产生作为奇异作用量（singular action）的额外贡献出现。

Result: 该框架在绝热极限（adiabatic limit）下恢复标准平衡关系，并推广到动态驱动系统。在常曲率f(R)引力的Kerr-Newman型黑洞中，平衡熵由f在背景曲率处的导数加权；非平衡修正来自通量诱导的有效热力学作用量形变。分析表明，外视界与内视界具有相反的拓扑定向（topological orientation），非极端Kerr-Newman族保持拓扑类W=0，除非发生视界分岔（bifurcation）或合并改变奇异性结构。

Conclusion: 本文建立的非平衡黑洞热力学框架可统一处理平衡与非平衡效应，并通过自由能曲线、Kerr-Newman温度曲线和熵产生定律的数值图示验证了理论行为。

Abstract: This work presents a non-equilibrium framework for thermodynamicized black holes, inspired by the entropy-functional interpretation of emergent gravity and by residue-based methods in black hole thermodynamics. The main idea is to unify three components: an entropy functional principle for selecting physical on-shell backgrounds, a Euclidean and contour-based description of the horizon temperature through simple pole singularities, and a topological residue classification of multi-horizon black hole configurations. On this basis, the paper introduces a quasi-stationary non-equilibrium partition functional in which irreversible entropy production appears as an additional contribution to the singular action. The formalism reproduces the standard equilibrium relations in the adiabatic limit, while also extending them to dynamically driven black-hole systems with matter, charge, and rotational fluxes. The framework is then applied to Kerr Newman type black holes in constant curvature f(R) gravity, where the equilibrium entropy remains weighted by the derivative of f at the background curvature, while non-equilibrium corrections arise from flux-induced deformations of the effective thermodynamic action. The analysis further shows that the outer and inner horizons carry opposite topological orientations, so the non-extremal Kerr Newman family stays in the topological class W = 0 unless a horizon bifurcation or merger changes the singularity structure. Finally, several function plots are provided to illustrate the behavior of equilibrium and non-equilibrium free energy, the Kerr Newman temperature curve, and the entropy production law.

### [94] [Calculation of a regularized Teukolsky Green function in Schwarzschild spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21219)
*David Q. Aruquipa,Marc Casals,Brien C. Nolan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在史瓦西时空的(Bardeen-Press-)Teukolsky方程中，精确计算了推迟格林函数（retarded Green function）Hadamard形式中的各个因子，推导了其直接部分的分离变量形式，并利用所得ℓ模计算了引力扰动中扣除直接部分后的推迟格林函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于史瓦西时空中Teukolsky方程推迟格林函数的计算仍不完善，Hadamard形式中的关键因子尚未被精确表达。作者旨在获得这些因子的精确表达式，并改进此前的研究结果。

Method: 在共形于史瓦西的乘积时空𝒮² × ℳ₂中工作，使得度规取直积形式，从而分离出推迟格林函数Hadamard形式的直接部分（singular part）。分别计算其中的角因子和ℳ₂因子，后者被表达为沿测地线满足输运方程的自旋依赖因子乘以van Vleck行列式的平方根，并在恒定半径轨道上给出精确结果。

Conclusion: 得到的扣除直接部分后的推迟格林函数在实际计算中能更好地表示近邻点附近的推迟格林函数行为。这项工作为史瓦西时空扰动理论的精确计算提供了更完善的解析工具。

Abstract: We obtain exact expressions for various factors involved in the Hadamard form of the retarded Green function for the (Bardeen-Press-)Teukolsky equation on Schwarzschild spacetime. We use these to improve on previous results for the calculation of this Green function. We work in a spacetime $\mathcal{M}_2\times\mathbb{S}^2$ conformal to Schwarzschild, in which the metric takes a direct product form. This allows us to derive a separable form for the direct (i.e., singular) part of the Hadamard form of the retarded Green function. The angular factor in this quantity is calculated explicitly. This shows an interesting interplay between geodesics of $\mathbb{S}^2$, spin-weighted spherical harmonics, and Euler angles. The $\mathcal{M}_2$ factor equates to a spin-dependent factor that satisfies a transport equation along geodesics, times the square root of the van Vleck determinant. Both terms are calculated in an exact form for constant radius orbits (which includes the cases of circular timelike geodesics and static worldlines of Schwarzschild spacetime). This separable form also allows us to obtain the multipolar $\ell$-modes of the direct part for electromagnetic and gravitational field perturbations. We then use these $\ell$-modes to calculate, in the gravitational case, the retarded Green function minus its direct part: this is a better representation in practise of the retarded Green function for points near coincidence.

### [95] [Bianchi-I Cosmology with Radiation in Asymptotically Safe Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21237)
*Chiang-Mei Chen,Ting-Kui Fan,Rituparna Mandal,Nobuyoshi Ohta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究在渐近安全引力（asymptotically safe gravity）框架下分析了各向异性Bianchi-I宇宙的晚期演化。对于辐射主导宇宙，经典演化出现对数项导致缓慢各向同性化，而量子效应在中间阶段抑制各向异性。存在磁场时，若经典宇宙学常数为零，宇宙演化至持久各向异性的Kasner型（Kasner-type）区域；若宇宙学常数非零，晚期由宇宙学常数主导，宇宙渐近趋近各向同性的德西特（de Sitter）相。Hodge对偶性证明结论同样适用于电场主导环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索渐近安全引力框架下各向异性宇宙的晚期演化行为，特别是量子引力效应对各向异性衰减和磁场演化的影响。

Method: 在渐近安全引力框架下分析Bianchi-I宇宙模型，分别考察辐射主导流体（状态方程 $p=\rho/3$）和磁场存在两种情况，并利用Hodge对偶性（Hodge duality）将结论推广至电场主导环境。

Result: 辐射主导宇宙中经典演化存在对数项导致缓慢各向同性化，量子效应在中间阶段产生次主导修正（subleading corrections）以软化各向异性。磁场存在且经典宇宙学常数为零时，宇宙演化至Kasner型区域，持久保持各向异性，但量子效应增强膨胀率并加速磁场衰减；经典宇宙学常数非零时，晚期由宇宙学常数主导，宇宙渐近趋近各向同性德西特相，各向异性和磁场均指数衰减。

Conclusion: 量子引力效应（渐近安全引力）对各向异性宇宙的晚期演化有显著影响，且磁场与电场在Hodge对偶意义下演化行为等价。

Abstract: We study the late-time evolution of an anisotropic Bianchi-I universe with radiation in the framework of asymptotically safe gravity. We first discuss the radiation-dominated universe for the perfect fluid with the equation of state $p=ρ/3$, and find that the classical evolution involves logarithmic terms, which lead to a slow approach toward isotropy. The quantum effects introduce subleading corrections that soften the anisotropy in the intermediate stage. Next we discuss the universe with magnetic fields. For a vanishing classical cosmological constant, we find that the universe in general evolves toward a Kasner-type regime with persistent anisotropy while the expansion rate is enhanced by quantum effects, leading to a faster decay of the magnetic field. In contrast, for a nonzero classical cosmological constant, the late-time dynamics are dominated by the cosmological constant, and the universe asymptotically approaches an isotropic de Sitter phase with exponential decay of both anisotropies and the magnetic field. Finally, we employ Hodge duality to demonstrate that these cosmological findings apply equally to environments dominated by electric fields.

Abstract: Superradiant instability of ultralight bosons can produce clouds around rotating black holes, whose continuous gravitational wave (GW) emission is a promising observational target. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究仅局限于特定的二次标量耦合项（quadratic scalar coupling terms）和球对称恒星（spherically symmetric stars），而实际标量-张量理论中的耦合可出现在任意阶数，且天体物理中的中子星普遍具有角动量。因此，有必要探索更一般耦合形式以及旋转效应下标量化相变的结构。

Method: 利用朗道理论（Landau theory）的工具，将标量化现象建模为相变过程；引入共形标度因子（conformal scaling factor）中的线性项与二次项，以考虑更一般的耦合形式；同时通过引入旋转效应，分析恒星角动量对相变结构的影响。

Result: 线性耦合的引入使得解空间变得复杂，但朗道模型能够系统地找到在数值搜索中常被忽略的标量化解分支。恒星旋转的主要影响是将发生相变的恒星质量向更高值移动，但在定性图像上与球对称情形相似。

Conclusion: 朗道标量化模型（Landau model of scalarization）为系统探索更一般耦合下的标量化解分支提供了一种新颖且有效的工具；旋转效应虽定量改变相变发生的位置，但未改变其定性结构。

Abstract: There has been a recent revival in understanding the spontaneous scalarization phenomenon in scalar-tensor gravity as a phase transition. Using the tools of the Landau theory, we now know that first-order transitions where scalarization occurs in a discontinuous manner is more prominent than what had been considered in the literature, and this might lead to novel observation channels. However, the examples so far have been restricted to specific quadratic scalar coupling terms and spherically symmetric stars. Here we explore the phase transition structure of scalarization for more general couplings, considering linear as well as quadratic terms in the conformal scaling factor of the theory. Moreover, we also investigate the effect of rotation on the scalarization phase transition. Both of these considerations are natural choices since the coupling in a scalar-tensor theory can appear at all orders, and astrophysical neutron stars commonly have angular momentum. The introduction of linear coupling leads to a complex solution space which is harder to explore. However, we demonstrate that the Landau model of scalarization enables us to systematically find the branches of scalarized solutions that are commonly overlooked in numerical searches, providing a novel tool. On the other hand, the main effect of stellar rotation is shifting the stellar masses at which the phase transition occurs to higher values, but the qualitative picture remains similar to what happens under spherical symmetry.

</details>


### [98] [A Study of Non-Singular Bounce in Myrzakulov-type $f(R,T)$ Gravity with Chaplygin Gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21415)
*Khandro K Chokyi,Abdel Nasser Tawfik,Surajit Chattopadhyay*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在 Myrzakulov 型 f(R,T)=R+αT+βT² 引力框架下，结合 Chaplygin 气体状态方程，通过对称尺度因子重建（Model I）和自治动力系统分析（Model II）两种方法，验证了非奇异弹跳宇宙（non-singular bounce）的可行性。结果表明，负的二次迹参数 β 可产生几何排斥力，有效违反零能量条件（Null Energy Condition, NEC），从而避免大爆炸奇点，并且该模型在早期和晚期宇宙均满足稳定性与因果性要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准宇宙学模型面临大爆炸奇点（Big Bang singularity）问题，需在广义相对论（General Relativity）框架外寻找替代方案。本研究旨在探索 f(R,T) 修正引力理论能否通过物质-几何耦合提供纯粹的几何机制实现弹跳宇宙，避免引入奇异物质场。

Method: 采用两种分析路径：Model I 基于对称尺度因子（symmetric scale factor）假设构建重建方案（reconstruction scheme）；Model II 运用自治动力系统分析（autonomous dynamical system analysis）。两者均结合 Chaplygin 气体状态方程，并对参数空间 (β, ρ₀) 进行数值扫描。

Result: 当 β < 0 时，物质-几何耦合在高密度区产生足够几何排斥力，有效违反零能量条件（NEC）。参数扫描显示存在一个临界密度阈值，低于该阈值宇宙将遵循广义相对论的奇异轨迹。有效状态方程渐近趋近 de Sitter 吸引子（w_eff → -1），声速平方在 0 ≤ c_s² ≤ 1 范围内。

Conclusion: f(R,T) 框架为大爆炸奇点提供了一种稳定、纯几何的经典替代方案，该模型同时满足早期宇宙弹跳需求与晚期宇宙加速膨胀的要求。

Abstract: This study investigates the non-singular bounce within the framework of Myrzakulov-type $f(R,T) = R + αT + βT^2$ gravity by adopting a Chaplygin gas equation of state. We employ two methodologies: a reconstruction scheme via a symmetric scale factor ansatz (Model I) and an autonomous dynamical system analysis (Model II). Our results indicate that the quadratic trace parameter $β$ acts as a primary physical driver; specifically, for $β< 0$, the matter-geometry coupling generates sufficient geometric repulsion to effectively violate the Null Energy Condition (NEC) at high densities without the requirement of exotic matter fields. A numerical scan of the $(β, ρ_0)$ parameter space indicates a critical density threshold required to initiate the bounce, below which the Universe follows a singular General Relativity trajectory. The models are shown to be physically viable, with the effective equation of state asymptotically approaching a de Sitter attractor ($w_{\text{eff}} \to -1$) and the squared speed of sound remaining within the stability and causality bounds ($0 \le c_s^2 \le 1$). This study shows that the $f(R,T)$ framework provides a stable, classically geometric alternative to the Big Bang singularity, consistent with both early-universe requirements and late-time accelerated expansion.

### [99] [Born-Infeld Electrogravity and Dyonic Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.05273)
*Guadalupe Ahumada Acuña,Cecilia Bejarano,Rafael Ferraro*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文定义了一种Born-Infeld电引力理论（Born-Infeld electrogravity），其拉格朗日量通过单一行列式结构耦合引力和电磁学。在Palatini形式下推导场方程，引力部分约化为无挠率、与度规相容的爱因斯坦方程；电磁部分则存在两种等价解释。通过球对称dyon解分析视界结构、极值条件和热力学，发现在小电荷极限下存在一个由Born-Infeld常数、牛顿常数和光速唯一确定的基本极端黑洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Palatini形式（Palatini formalism），对度规（metric）、联络（connection）和矢量势（vector potential）进行独立变分；通过球对称dyon解（spherically symmetric dyonic solutions）分析视界结构、极值条件与热力学性质。

Result: 引力部分退化为标准爱因斯坦方程；电磁部分可等价解释为标准Born-Infeld电动力学在有效背景几何中，或反常Born-Infeld电动力学在物理度规中。小电荷极限下存在一个由Born-Infeld常数、牛顿常数和光速唯一确定的极端黑洞（extremal black hole）。

Conclusion: Born-Infeld电引力在小电荷极限下自然预言了一个基本极端黑洞，其质量和视界面积仅由基本常数决定，暗示该理论可能为黑洞量子化提供新的理论线索。

Abstract: Born-Infeld electrogravity is defined through a Lagrangian that couples gravity and electromagnetism within a single determinantal structure. The field equations are derived in Palatini's formalism, where the metric, connection, and vector potential are varied independently in the action. As a result, the gravitational sector reduces to Einstein's equations with a torsion-free, metric-compatible connection. The electrodynamic sector, in turn, admits two equivalent interpretations or $pictures$: it can be seen either as a standard Born-Infeld electrodynamics in an effective background geometry, or as an $anomalous$ Born-Infeld electrodynamics in the physical metric. We illustrate the dynamics by analyzing the horizon structure, the extremality conditions, and the thermodynamics of spherically symmetric dyonic solutions. Remarkably, in the small-charge limit, Born--Infeld electrogravity admits a fundamental extremal black hole whose mass and horizon area are determined exclusively by the Born--Infeld and Newton constants and the speed of light.

### [100] [Quadrupolar bremsstrahlung waveform at the third-and-a-half post-Newtonian accuracy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21522)
*Donato Bini,Thibault Damour,Andrea Geralico*

TL;DR: 本文在多重后闵可夫斯基（MPM）框架下，计算了双质量散射过程中引力波波形四极矩部分的时间域和频率域表达式，达到3.5后牛顿（3.5PN）精度和2圈阶，并验证了非线性记忆项与软极限的一致性，以及与有效场论（EFT）结果在1圈截断下的匹配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确计算双体散射过程中引力波形的高阶修正，特别是频率域的四极辐射，对于引力波天文学和基础物理检验具有重要意义。

Method: 采用多重后闵可夫斯基（MPM）形式体系，利用3.5后牛顿（3.5PN）辐射反应准开普勒表示描述双曲运动，计算时间域的四极辐射矩$U_2$；进而通过频率域分析，将波形展开至2圈阶（$O(G^4)$）。

Result: 得到了3.5PN精度下频率域MPM波形在1圈截断下与现有有效场论（EFT）结果一致，前提是扣除连接MPM与EFT的Bondi-Metzner-Sachs（BMS）坐标架之间的Veneziano-Vilkovisky超平移偶极部分。

Conclusion: 本文结果验证了MPM与EFT两种形式体系在引力波形计算中的一致性，并为非线性记忆效应提供了频率域验证，有助于提升引力波形建模的精度。

Abstract: We study the quadrupolar part of the gravitational waveform $h_{ij}$ (encoded in the helicity-($-2)$ radiative quadrupole moment $U_2 = \frac{1}{2!} \bar m^{i} \bar m^{j } U_{i j} \in\frac{R}{4G} \bar m^{i} \bar m^{j } h_{i j}\equiv W $) emitted during the scattering of two masses. Working within the Multipolar Post-Minkowskian (MPM) formalism, we compute the time-domain value of $U_2$ at the third-and-a-half post-Newtonian (3.5PN) accuracy by using the 3.5PN radiation-reacted quasi-Keplerian representation of the hyperbolic motion. We then explicitly evaluate the {\it frequency-domain} value of $U_2$ up to the 2-loop level, i.e. $ O(G^4)$ contributions to $h_{ij}(ω, θ,φ)$, corresponding to $O(G^3)$ contributions to $\hat U_2(ω, θ,φ)$. The nonlinear memory contribution to the waveform in the center-of-mass frame is computed too, and checked against the soft-limit of the waveform. The 1-loop truncation of our 3.5PN frequency-domain MPM waveform is found to agree with corresponding existing Effective Field Theory (EFT) results when subtracting the dipolar part of the Veneziano-Vilkovisky supertranslation connecting the MPM and EFT Bondi-Metzner-Sachs (BMS) frames.

### [101] [Accelerating scaling solutions from dark matter particle creation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21770)
*Sudip Halder,Jaume de Haro,Supriya Pan,Emmanuel N. Saridakis,Tapan Saha,Subenoy Chakraborty*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过分析两种流体（无压暗物质与正压流体）在六种常见相互作用形式下的宇宙学动力学，发现加速标度吸引子（accelerating scaling attractors）仅在相互作用由暗物质密度主导且能量从暗物质流向第二流体时出现，从而在不引入暗能量（dark energy）的情况下模拟类似暗能量的行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在不引入暗能量成分的前提下，通过物质粒子绝热创生（adiabatic particle creation）机制获得宇宙加速膨胀的标度吸引子解，以寻找暗能量的替代解释。

Method: 研究一个包含无压暗物质（dark matter, DM）与正压流体（barotropic fluid）的两流体系统，其中暗物质经历绝热粒子创生并与第二流体交换能量。针对六种广泛采用的相互作用形式，在紧致相空间（compact phase space）中构建对应的自治系统（autonomous systems），并进行统一的动力学分析（dynamical analysis）。

Result: 加速标度吸引子（两种流体共存且能量分数固定的晚期状态）仅当相互作用由暗物质密度控制且能量从暗物质流向第二流体时才出现。这类吸引子存在于全局型与局域型暗物质基相互作用以及全局混合相互作用中，但在依赖第二流体或局域混合项的相互作用下完全缺失，后者会导致宇宙进入暗物质主导的加速相。

Conclusion: 结果表明，物质创生（matter creation）模拟暗能量行为的条件具有独特性，明确了在不引入暗能量成分的前提下实现类似暗能量效应的机制边界。

Abstract: This article opens new window to obtain accelerating scaling attractors without any need of dark energy. We study cosmological dynamics in a two-fluid system where pressureless dark matter (DM) undergoes adiabatic particle creation and exchanges energy with a barotropic fluid. Considering six widely used interaction prescriptions, we formulate the corresponding autonomous systems in a compact phase space and perform a unified dynamical analysis. We find that accelerating scaling attractors, namely late-time states where both fluids coexist with fixed energy fractions, arise only when the interaction is controlled by the DM density and energy flows from DM to the second fluid. Such attractors appear in the global and local DM-based interactions, and in the global mixed case, but are entirely absent when the interaction depends on the second fluid or on local mixed terms, which instead drive the universe to a DM-dominated accelerating phase. These results clarify the unique conditions under which matter creation can mimic dark-energy-like behaviour without introducing a dark-energy component.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将黑洞视界建模为基本量子长度单元的离散集合，构建长度系综（length ensemble）——类似于Krasnov的面积正则系综（area canonical ensemble）；利用视界附近观测者视角下熵与黑洞能量之间的关系，推导黑体谱。

Result: 从长度系综直接获得了黑体辐射谱；同时发现，对于视界附近的局域观测者，Hawking谱的温度需通过Tolman因子（Tolman factor）进行修正。

Conclusion: 该模型为黑洞视界的有效量子几何提供了一种新的描述框架，并通过长度系综将量子几何与Hawking辐射的黑体谱直接联系起来，局域温度修正进一步统一了量子引力与热力学关系。

Abstract: The paper develops a model to understand the effective quantum geometry of a black hole horizon and the emission of Hawking spectrum in 2+1 dimensions. We argue that one may view the black hole horizon as formed out of quantised lengths of elementary quanta of value $8π\ell_{P}\, n$, where $n\in \mathbb{N}$, and $\ell_{P}$ is the Planck length. To an observer near the black hole horizon, the entropy (or length of horizon cross-section) is related to the black hole energy. Hence, one may develop a formulation of length ensemble (similar to the area canonical ensemble of Krasnov) from which the black body spectrum may be obtained directly. To this local observer, the temperature of the Hawking spectrum is modified due to the Tolman factor.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究结果显示，模型参数a越大，吸积盘的有效辐射面积越大。在大观测角条件下，参数a的增大会显著增强直接像和次级像的不对称性（asymmetry）以及多普勒聚束效应（Doppler boosting effect）。

Conclusion: 该正则黑洞模型可通过实际观测数据（M87*和Sgr A*）有效约束参数a；a和观测角是调控黑洞光学外观的关键因素，大a和大观测角共同导致更显著的图像不对称与多普勒效应。

Abstract: We investigate the shadow, timelike geodesic structure, radiation properties of thin accretion disks, and optical appearance of a static spherically symmetric regular black hole, constructed based on the Dehnen-type density profile. Using observational data from M87* and Sgr A*, we constrain the model parameter $a$ at both $1σ$ and $2σ$ confidence levels. Based on the Page--Thorne model, we calculate the local radiative flux, redshift factor distribution, and the radiation flux received by a distant observer, systematically examining the effects of the parameter $a$ and the viewing angle on the black hole image. The results show that larger $a$ will enlarge the effective radiation area of the accretion disk and significantly enhance the asymmetry and Doppler boosting effects of the direct and secondary images at large viewing angles.

### [104] [Chaotic dynamics of charged particles near weakly magnetized black holes in Einstein-ModMax Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21622)

Abstract: This paper presents a systematic study of the chaotic dynamics of charged test particles around purely magnetically charged black holes immersed in a uniform external magnetic field within the framework of Einstein-ModMax theory. By constructing an explicit symplectic integrator, we obtain high-precision numerical solutions of the equations of motion. Combining the observational constraints from the Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) shadow images, we further restrict the parameter ranges of the model. We apply Shannon entropy and MIPP (mutual information for particle pairs) as effective indicators to identify the chaotic behavior of charged test particles in the spacetime of this black hole. Numerical results indicate that these indicators can clearly distinguish between regular and chaotic motion of orbits in strong gravitational field systems. Further analysis reveals that, compared to the key conserved quantities that determine the global dynamical behavior of the system -- energy $E$ and angular momentum $L$, the sensitivity of the system parameters $e^{-ν}$ and $Q_{m}$ to transitions in the orbital dynamical states is significantly reduced. This study provides a new perspective for a deeper understanding of the characterization and evolution mechanisms of chaotic dynamics in strong gravitational fields.

### [105] [Exploring the statistical anisotropy of primordial curvature perturbations with pulsar timing arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21642)
*Fengting Xie,Zhi-Chao Zhao,Qing-Hua Zhu,Xin Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究在唯象框架下研究原初功率谱中的偶极型统计各向异性，发现原初偶极会在标量诱导引力波（SIGWs）能量密度谱中同时诱导偶极和四极各向异性，而不会产生额外极化模式。基于该各向异性谱推导出脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）重叠约化函数（ORFs），该函数具有频率依赖性且在小尺度上各向异性增强。NANOGrav 15年数据集贝叶斯分析未发现显著的优势方向，对各向异性振幅给出了弱上限（g≲0.5），原因是观测频段位于谱峰之下，各向异性贡献被抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）对随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational wave background）的探测为理解超大质量黑洞双星和早期宇宙提供了新窗口，最近的PTA合作进一步推进了对随机引力波背景中各向异性的探测。本研究旨在系统分析原初功率谱中偶极型统计各向异性对标量诱导引力波（SIGWs）能量密度谱及各向异性观测信号的影响。

Method: 采用唯象框架，从原初功率谱中的偶极型各向异性出发，推导其对标量诱导引力波（SIGWs）能量密度谱的影响；进一步推导对应的脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）重叠约化函数（ORFs），并利用NANOGrav 15年数据集进行贝叶斯分析以约束各向异性。

Result: 原初偶极在能量密度谱中同时诱导偶极和四极各向异性，不产生额外极化模式；重叠约化函数（ORFs）具有频率依赖性，小尺度上各向异性增强；由于毫秒脉冲星在天空中的非均匀分布，ORFs的形态显式依赖于各向异性的优势方向；NANOGrav 15年数据未发现显著优势方向，各向异性振幅上限为g≲0.5。

Conclusion: 观测频段位于谱峰之下导致模型预测的各向异性贡献被抑制，这是当前约束较弱的原因。未来具有更宽频率覆盖的PTA观测数据集有望显著收紧对偶极型各向异性的约束，验证该理论框架的预测。

Abstract: The recent detection of a stochastic gravitational wave background by pulsar timing arrays has opened a new window in understanding supermassive black hole binaries and in probing the universe at the early time. Recently, pulsar timing array (PTA) collaborations have been further paving the way to probe anisotropies in the stochastic gravitational wave background. This study investigates dipole-type statistical anisotropy in the primordial power spectrum within a phenomenological framework. We demonstrate that the primordial dipole induces both dipolar and quadrupolar anisotropies in the energy density spectrum of scalar-induced gravitational waves (SIGWs), without generating extra polarization modes. Based on this anisotropic spectrum, we derive the corresponding PTA overlap reduction functions (ORFs), which exhibit frequency dependence, with the anisotropies enhanced on small scales. Furthermore, owing to the non-uniform distribution of millisecond pulsars over the sky in current PTA dataset, the ORFs exhibit a morphology that explicitly depends on the preferred direction of the anisotropy. However, our bayesian analysis of the NANOGrav 15-year dataset still yields no significant evidence for a preferred direction and a weak upper limit on anisotropy amplitude $(g\lesssim0.5)$. This result arises because the observational frequency band lies below the spectral peak, where our models predict suppressed anisotropic contributions. This limitation highlights the potential of future PTA observations. Specifically, datasets with broader frequency coverage are expected to tighten constraints on dipole-type anisotropy.

</details>


### [106] [Conformal anomaly transport induced by dark photon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21664)
*Marek Rogatko,Karol I. Wysokinski*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用暗光子（dark photon）模型作为暗区模型，暗区由辅助U(1)规范场（auxiliary U(1)-gauge field）描述并与可见区耦合；假设外尔型共形变换（Weyl type conformal transformation）与闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）差异较小，从而避免使用弯曲背景下的量子场论复杂方法。

Result: 可见区与暗区产生的电流均正比于各自系统相应的贝塔函数（beta functions）；对于无电荷暗区，预测暗区尺度电导率存在α的线性修正，可见区尺度电导率存在α的二次修正。

Conclusion: 引力场不均匀性通过共形变换近似可有效纳入分析，并导致可见区与暗区的输运性质出现可预测的修正，为暗物质与引力耦合的场论描述提供了新的可检验预言。

Abstract: We have considered the problem of the influence of inhomogeneity of gravitational field on transport effects predicted by the field theory describing massless Dirac fermions in the Maxwell and dark matter background. As a model of dark sector one takes into account dark photon model, where the hidden sector is described by the auxiliary U(1)-gauge field coupled to the visible sector. Elaborating the model we restrict our considerations to the case when Weyl type conformal transformation slightly differs from the Minkowski spacetime. This assumption simplifies the calculations and enables us not to use complicated methods of the quantum field theory in the curved background. The resulting currents stemming both from visible and dark sectors are proportional to the adequate beta functions appearing in the elaborated systems. For charge-less dark sector we predict corrections to the scale conductivities in both sectors: linear in α in the dark sector and quadratic in the visible one.

### [107] [Quantum-information diagnostics of cosmological perturbations with nontrivial sound speed in inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21755)
*Shi-Cheng Liu,Lei-Hua Liu,Bichu Li,Hai-Qing Zhang,Peng-Zhang He*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用归一化双模压缩态框架，系统研究了非平凡声速对宇宙学扰动量子信息诊断的影响，发现非平凡声速显著抑制纯度、增强纠缠与熵信号，并推迟经典化（classicality）的 onset。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非平凡声速（nontrivial sound speed）如何动态重塑宇宙学扰动的量子信息特征，特别是压缩参数（squeezing parameters）$r_k$ 和 $φ_k$ 的薛定谔演化，进而影响可观测扇区约化密度矩阵的量子信息诊断量。

Method: 采用归一化双模压缩态（normalized open two-mode squeezed-state）框架，引入声速共振参数化（sound-speed-resonance parametrization），并利用有界变量 $x = \tanh r_k$ 对后暴胀（post-inflationary）方程的多尺度刚性（multiscale stiffness）进行部分正则化，仅在暴胀（inflationary）区域内进行数值模拟。

Result: 数值结果表明，非平凡声速显著抑制了约化态的纯度（purity），表明有效混合度（effective mixedness）增强；同时，它强烈放大并调制了熵（熵：entropy）和纠缠（entanglement）诊断量；具体而言，非平凡声速通过调制退相干（decoherence）过程推迟了经典化（onset of classicality）的 onset。

Conclusion: 非平凡声速在早期宇宙的纠缠结构中留下了清晰可辨的量子信息印记（quantum-information signatures），为识别声速效应提供了可观测的诊断依据。

Abstract: In this work, we systematically investigate the quantum-information diagnostics of cosmological perturbations with a nontrivial sound speed, utilizing a normalized open two-mode squeezed-state framework. Rather than introducing new observables, our analysis focuses on how a modified sound speed dynamically reshapes the Schrödinger evolution of the squeezing parameters ($r_k$ and $φ_k$). We demonstrate how these dynamical changes are inherited by the reduced density matrix of the observable sector. By employing a sound-speed-resonance parametrization, we derive and evaluate the purity, von Neumann entropy, Rényi entropies, and logarithmic negativity. To overcome the intrinsic multiscale stiffness of the post-inflationary equations, we introduce a bounded variable $x = \tanh r_k$ as a partial regularization, which enables reliable numerical simulations exclusively within the inflationary regime. Our numerical results reveal that a nontrivial sound speed significantly suppresses the purity of the reduced state, indicating enhanced effective mixedness. Simultaneously, it strongly amplifies and modulates both the entropic and entanglement diagnostics. More precisely, a nontrivial sound speed postpones the onset of classicality by modulating the decoherence process. Ultimately, we show that a nontrivial sound speed leaves distinct and identifiable quantum-information signatures within the entanglement structure of the early universe.

### [108] [A Nearest-Neighbor Hard-Core Model on a Penrose Graph](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21086)
*A. Mazel,I. Stuhl,Y. Suhov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明彭罗斯P3平铺（视为平面无向图）中独立集的最大图密度为(57-25√5)/2 ≈ 0.54915，尽管该图是二部图（bipartite）。由此推出该图上最近邻硬核粒子模型（hard core particle model）在粒子活性足够大时极端吉布斯测度（extreme Gibbs measure）唯一，否定了关于偶奇相共存的自然预期。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管彭罗斯P3平铺图是二部图（bipartite），但独立集（independent set）的最大图密度存在非平凡约束，且关于偶相与奇相（even and odd phases）共存的自然预期可能不成立，因而需要精确计算该密度并分析对应统计力学模型的相行为。

Method: 将彭罗斯P3平铺视为平面无向图（planar non-directed graph），通过组合优化方法证明独立集（independent set）的最大图密度精确值，并利用该结果分析最近邻硬核粒子模型（hard core particle model）的极端吉布斯测度（extreme Gibbs measure）的唯一性条件。

Result: 独立集最大图密度精确值为(57-25√5)/2，约等于0.54915；当粒子活性（particle activity）足够大时，该模型在彭罗斯P3平铺上的极端吉布斯测度唯一。

Conclusion: 该结果否定了偶奇相共存（coexistence of even and odd phases）的自然预期，表明在该非周期平铺结构中，二部图性质并不自动导致低温下有序相（ordered phases）的共存。

Abstract: We prove that the maximal graph-density of an independent set in a Penrose P3 tiling considered as a planar non-directed graph is equal to $(57 - 25 \sqrt{5})/2 \approx 0.54915$ despite the fact that the graph is bipartite. Accordingly, the extreme Gibbs measure of the nearest-neighbor hard core particle model on this graph is unique for sufficiently large values of the particle activity. This invalidates a natural expectation to observe the coexistence of even and odd phases.

### [109] [How it cools? Studying the heat flow out of a semi-infinite slab in welding: An analytical approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21250)
*Fawzi Aly,Alex Kitt,Luke Mohr*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个解析框架，通过引入类似牛顿冷却定律的冷却边界条件，利用拉普拉斯变换和傅里叶级数两种等价方法，推导出高斯、椭球、双椭球及时间依赖性热源下的瞬态和稳态温度场的闭式解。该框架在显著降低计算成本和实验需求的同时，与数值模拟结果高度吻合，可用于优化金属制造中的热预测、缓解残余应力，并为机器学习模型生成合成数据集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 增材制造（additive manufacturing）和焊接过程对热耗散高度敏感，不当的热管理会导致残余应力（residual stresses）、变形和开裂。现有的热传导模型（如Rosenthal解）无法处理有限三维几何体、冷却效应或瞬态行为，精度受限。因此，需要一种既能处理复杂边界条件又能保持解析可解性的新框架。

Method: 开发了一个分析框架，引入符合牛顿冷却定律（Newton's Law of Cooling）的冷却边界条件。采用拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transform）和傅里叶级数（Fourier series）两种已被证明等价的方法，针对高斯（Gaussian）、椭球（ellipsoidal）、双椭球（double-ellipsoidal）以及时间依赖性开关（time-dependent on/off switch）等多种热源，推导出瞬态和稳态温度场的闭式解（closed-form solutions）。

Result: 该解析解与数值实现（numerical implementations）结果高度一致，同时提供了更深入的物理洞察。该方法显著降低了计算成本和实验需求，使热预测和残余应力缓解成为可扩展的工具。此外，该框架还能够为机器学习模型生成合成数据集（synthetic datasets），用以高效预测热分布。

Conclusion: 所提出的解析框架克服了传统热传导模型在有限三维几何和冷却边界条件下的局限性，为金属基制造过程提供了一种兼具精度与效率的热管理优化工具，并拓展了数据驱动方法的应用可能。

Abstract: Additive manufacturing and welding processes are highly sensitive to heat dissipation, where improper thermal management leads to residual stresses, distortions, and cracking. Existing heat transfer models, such as Rosenthal's solutions, fail to handle finite 3D geometries, cooling effects, or transient behavior, limiting their accuracy. We overcome these limitations by developing an analytical framework that incorporates cooling boundary conditions mimicking Newton's Law of Cooling. Using two different and proven-equivalent approaches, Laplace transform and Fourier series, we derive closed-form solutions for transient and steady-state temperature profiles under various heat sources, including Gaussian, ellipsoidal, double-ellipsoidal, and time-dependent on/off switch sources. We compare our analytical solutions to numerical implementations, demonstrating strong agreement while providing deeper physical insight. This approach significantly reduces computational cost and experimental requirements, making it a scalable tool for optimizing thermal predictions and mitigating residual stresses in metal-based manufacturing. Additionally, our framework enables the generation of synthetic datasets for machine learning models to predict heat distribution efficiently.

### [110] [On invariant solutions of linear time-fractional diffusion-wave equations with variable coefficients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21267)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分数阶扩散方程和分数阶波动方程分别描述了反常扩散（anomalous diffusion）以及振荡与波传播等物理过程，但含变系数情形下的精确解求解仍具有挑战性，需要借助对称性方法进行系统研究。

Method: 首先通过李群对称性分析确定与变系数相关的无穷小对称性（infinitesimal symmetries），然后利用这些对称性构造不变解，最终解以Mittag-Leffler函数、广义Wright函数（generalized Wright functions）和Fox H-函数（Fox H-functions）等特殊函数形式给出。

Result: 获得了含变系数的时间分数阶扩散波方程的不变精确解，这些解表达为Mittag-Leffler函数、广义Wright函数和Fox H-函数。

Conclusion: 李群对称性分析为求解含变系数的分数阶扩散波方程提供了有效途径，所得精确解有助于理解反常扩散和波传播等物理系统的动力学行为。

Abstract: We study invariant solutions of a certain class of time-fractional diffusion-wave equations with variable coefficients via Lie symmetry analysis. In physics, the fractional diffusion equation describes transport dynamics that are governed by anomalous diffusion while the fractional wave equation describes oscillations and wave propagation in various physical systems. In order to obtain exact invariant solutions of these equations, we firstly determine infinitesimal symmetries with respect to the variable coefficients of the equations. ### [111] [The Geometry Underlying the Quantum Harmonic Oscillator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21373)
*Alexander D. Popov*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 二维谐振子中存在量子本征态与经典几何结构的明确对应关系；类似地，Kepler/氢原子问题（Kepler/hydrogen atom problem）中也存在经典态与量子态之间的对应关系。

Abstract: We consider two-dimensional harmonic oscillator in the complex Bargmann-Fock-Segal representation with $T^*{\mathbb R}^{2}={\mathbb C}^2$ as classical phase space. We show that the eigenfunctions $ψ_n$ of the quantum Hamiltonian correspond to complex radial coordinates in the reduced phase space ${\mathbb C}^2/{\mathbb Z}_n\subset{\mathbb C}^2$. They describe ${\mathbb Z}_n$-invariant motion of particle along a circle $S^1$ in lens space $S^3/{\mathbb Z}_n\subset{\mathbb C}^2/{\mathbb Z}_n$, where ${\mathbb Z}_n$ is the cyclic group of rotation by an angle $2π/n$ on the circle $S^1$, $n=1,2,...\,$. Thus the general solution of the Schrödinger equation carries information about an infinite number of admissible classical states $ψ_n$ that can be mapped to other states after lifting into the quantum bundle. We show that in the Kepler/hydrogen atom problem there is a similar correspondence between classical and quantum states.

### [112] [Yang-Baxter Integrability and Exceptional-Point Structure in Pseudo-Hermitian Quantum Impurity Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21547)
*Vinayak M. Kulkarni*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文为周期驱动狄拉克型浴场（bath）中的伪厄米量子杂质系统（pseudo-Hermitian quantum impurity systems）建立了数学受控的Yang–Baxter可积性（Yang–Baxter integrability）框架。通过构建基于双正交投影算符（biorthogonal projector）的Lax算符（Lax operator），证明了在PT对称性（$\PT$ symmetry）未破缺相和奇异点（exceptional point, EP）处的可积结构，导出了双正交Bethe方程（biorthogonal Bethe equations）及区分EP奇异性和近藤临界性（Kondo criticality）的诊断量，并验证了EP处Bethe快度的平方根汇聚与$\mathbb{Z}_2$单值性（monodromy）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 周期驱动下狄拉克型浴场耦合的量子杂质系统缺乏系统的可积性分析框架；伪厄米哈密顿量在奇异点（EP）处变为不可对角化，传统可积性方法在此失效，亟需建立能同时覆盖PT对称相和EP处的数学受控的可积性理论。

Method: 基于秩1双正交投影算符构建Lax算符，在投影代数（projector algebra）中证明RLL关系及$\etamet$修正的RTT结构；通过双正交投影算符的正则化（regularization），将理性投影型R矩阵（rational projector-type $R$-matrix）从PT未破缺相连续延拓至EP处；利用Floquet–Magnus展开（Floquet–Magnus expansion）从周期驱动微观系统以$\mathcal{O}(1/Ω)$算符-范数误差得到有效伪厄米哈密顿量。

Result: 在PT未破缺相得到满足Yang–Baxter方程的投影型R矩阵；导出了双正交Bethe方程，并证明了Gaudin矩阵（Gaudin matrix）在EP处变为缺陷（defective），由此提出诊断量$\mathcal{R}=κ(G)|\det G|$以区分EP奇异性和近藤临界性；证明了EP处Bethe快度呈现平方根汇聚和$\mathbb{Z}_2$单值性，反映了底层若尔当结构（Jordan structure）。

Conclusion: 该框架为伪厄米量子杂质系统的可积性提供了严格的数学基础，揭示了EP处可积结构的连续延伸及其独特的若尔当块特征，并给出了区分EP与近藤临界性的实用诊断工具。

Abstract: We develop a mathematically controlled framework for Yang--Baxter integrability in pseudo-Hermitian quantum impurity systems arising from periodic driving of a Dirac-like bath. The effective impurity Hamiltonian possesses a dynamically generated $\PT$ symmetry and exhibits exceptional points (EPs) where it becomes non-diagonalizable. We construct a Lax operator based on a rank-one biorthogonal projector associated with the impurity contact sector and prove that it satisfies an RLL relation within a projector algebra, leading to an $\etamet$-modified RTT structure and a commuting family of transfer matrices. The associated rational projector-type $R$-matrix satisfies the Yang--Baxter equation in the $\PT$-unbroken phase and extends continuously to the EP through a regularization of the biorthogonal projector. Within this framework we derive biorthogonal Bethe equations and show that the Gaudin matrix becomes defective at the EP, motivating the diagnostic $\mathcal{R}=κ(G)\,|\det G|$ that sharply separates EP singularities from Kondo criticality. We further prove that Bethe rapidities exhibit square-root coalescence and $\mathbb{Z}_2$ monodromy at the EP, reflecting the underlying Jordan structure, and that the effective pseudo-Hermitian Hamiltonian emerges from the periodically driven microscopic system with controlled operator-norm error $\mathcal{O}(1/Ω)$ via the Floquet--Magnus expansion.

</details>


### [113] [Derivation of Gibbs measure from Gibbs state with the fractional Bessel interaction in Two Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21583)
*Phan Thành Nam,Rongchan Zhu,Xiangchan Zhu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文推导了与分数阶贝塞尔相互作用势相关联的经典吉布斯测度，从同一相互作用的重新规范化巨正则量子玻色气体出发，覆盖了$\frac32<β\leq2$范围内不可求和的情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究无法处理$\frac32<β\leq2$范围内不可求和的分数阶贝塞尔相互作用势$\widehat{v}_β(k)=\langle k\rangle^{-β}$，此时量子模型自能发散，无法写成通常的密度平方形式，因此需要新的重正化方案。

Method: 采用零模（zero mode）的居中数涨落项（centered number-fluctuation term）进行重正化（renormalization），并对高频剩余项做详细分析，进而实施低频局域化（low-frequency localization）策略。

Result: 证明了量子相对自由能（quantum relative free energy）收敛到经典分数阶贝塞尔自由能，同时约化密度矩阵（reduced density matrices）收敛到极限吉布斯测度。

Conclusion: 成功在非可和相互作用势情形下建立了量子玻色气体到经典吉布斯测度的场论对应关系，拓展了现有结果的参数适用范围。

Abstract: We derive the classical Gibbs measure on $\mathbb{T}^2$ associated with the fractional Bessel interaction potential $\widehat{v}_β(k)=\langle k\rangle^{-β}$ from a renormalized grand-canonical quantum Bose gas with the same interaction. Our result covers the whole range $\frac32<β\leq2$, where $\widehat{v}_β(k)$ is not summable and the quantum model cannot be written in the usual density-square form, as the associated self-energy diverges. We therefore need to renormalize the zero mode by a centered number-fluctuation term and then develop a detailed analysis for the high-frequency remainders. All this allows us to implement a low-frequency localization and obtain the convergence of the quantum relative free energy to the classical fractional-Bessel free energy, as well as the convergence of the reduced density matrices to the limiting Gibbs measure.

</details>


### [114] [The KMS and GNS Spectral Gap of Quantum Markov Semigroups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21630)
*Melchior Wirth*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，对于任意冯·诺依曼代数上具有忠实正规不变态的量子马尔可夫半群（quantum Markov semigroup），其关于KMS内积的指数衰减率（exponential decay rate）不小于关于GNS内积的指数衰减率，从而证实了Fagnola等人的猜想，并将结论推广至更广泛的算子单调函数诱导的内积类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Fagnola、Poletti、Sasso和Umanità猜想：对于高斯量子马尔可夫半群（Gaussian quantum Markov semigroup），关于KMS内积的指数衰减率被关于GNS内积的指数衰减率所下界约束。本文旨在检验该猜想是否成立，并考察其是否可推广至更一般的量子马尔可夫半群。

Method: 通过分析量子马尔可夫半群在不同内积下的指数衰减率之间的数学关系，将研究范围从高斯量子马尔可夫半群扩展至任意冯·诺依曼代数（von Neumann algebra）上具有忠实正规不变态（faithful normal invariant state）的量子马尔可夫半群，并进一步将KMS内积替换为由算子单调函数（operator monotone function）诱导的一整类内积。

Result: 该猜想成立，且不仅限于高斯情形：对于任意冯·诺依曼代数上具有忠实正规不变态的量子马尔可夫半群，KMS内积下的指数衰减率确实不小于GNS内积下的指数衰减率。此外，KMS内积可被算子单调函数诱导的更广泛内积类所取代。

Conclusion: 不同内积下量子马尔可夫半群指数衰减率之间的下界关系具有普遍性，不依赖于高斯结构，且可拓展至由算子单调函数诱导的内积类。

Abstract: We establish a relation between the exponential decay rates of quantum Markov semigroups with respect to different inner products. More precisely, it was conjectured by Fagnola, Poletti, Sasso and Umanità that for a Gaussian quantum Markov semigroup, the exponential decay rate with respect to the KMS inner product is bounded below by the exponential decay rate for the GNS inner product. We show that this is indeed the case and not limited to Gaussian quantum Markov semigroups, but holds for quantum Markov semigroups with a faithful normal invariant state on arbitrary von Neumann algebras. Additionally, the KMS inner product can be replaced by a whole class of inner products induced by operator monotone functions.

</details>
