### [115] [Local Electroneutrality Violation as a Universal Constraint in Confined Electrolytes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20976)
*M. Lozada-Cassou*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了受限电解质中局部电中性违反（local electroneutrality violation）的强度由受限空间的拓扑结构决定，在球、柱、平面三种几何中形成普适的强度层级：球形腔体最强，柱状次之，平面狭缝最弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解受限空间中局部电中性违反的机制，并找出其结构起源——特别是拓扑（topology）而非局部几何细节如何影响电荷分布。

Method: 在泊松-玻尔兹曼理论（Poisson-Boltzmann theory）框架下，引入一个电中性偏离比率（electroneutrality deviation ratio），用以量化由受限域的紧致性（compactness）与边界重数（boundary multiplicity）所引入的全局静电约束对电荷平衡的修正。

Result: 在所有几何下电中性的渐进恢复均成立，但有限尺寸偏离表现出一致层级：球最强、柱次之、平面最弱，说明拓扑是结构起源。

Conclusion: 局部电中性违反是由全局约束主导的普遍现象，其强度由受限域拓扑而非局部几何细节控制，是过充电（overcharging）与电荷反转（charge reversal）等现象的共同基础。

Abstract: We show that finite-size violations of local electroneutrality in confined electrolytes are governed by the topology of the confining domain, yielding a universal hierarchy of deviations across spherical, cylindrical, and planar geometries. Within Poisson-Boltzmann theory, we introduce an electroneutrality deviation ratio that quantifies how global electrostatic constrains associated with compacness and boundary multiplicity modify charge balance inside confined domains. Although electroneutrality is asymptotically restored in all geometries, finite-size deviations are strongest in compact spherical cavities, weaker in cylindrical confinement, and weakest in planar slits. These results identify topology as the structural origin of confinement-induced charge redistribution and stablish the violation of local electroneutrality as global constraint underlying phenomena such as overcharging anf charge reversal, demostrating that confinement-not local-not local geometric details-controls the emergence of these effects.

Conclusion: 成功获得了Smith Hat Tile在多种逾渗模型下的精确临界阈值，为这一新型非周期结构的逾渗行为提供了定量基准。

Abstract: The Smith Hat tile is the first known aperiodic monotile, having been discovered in 2023. The simple structure, constructed using only 8 kites, is unique and well motivated for analysis within percolation theory. The primary goal of this paper is to discover the critical threshold $p_c$ in both site and bond Bernoulli structures using Monte Carlo simulation for the Smith hat tile(1,$\sqrt3$). Our findings are site and bond values of $p_c^s = 0.822725 \pm 0.000044$ and $p_c^b = 0.798161 \pm 0.000044$ for edge percolation and $0.544247 \pm 0.000101$ for site percolation on the dual graph.

### [117] [Fractals of Simple Random Walks in Two Dimensions: A Monte Carlo Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21341)
*Jiang Zhou,Ziru Deng,Pengcheng Hou*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟，研究了二维周期方格上离散时间简单随机游走（simple random walk, sRW）簇的分形几何。结果表明簇质量呈现边际“对数分形”（logarithmic fractals）行为，外缘（hull）的分形维数精确符合 Schramm-Loewner 演化（SLE₈/₃）的预测，而化学距离（chemical distance）标度律恰好达到二维高斯自由场水平集逾渗（level-set percolation）的理论上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索简单随机游走（sRW）簇的几何结构，特别是其分形维数、外缘性质以及化学距离的标度行为，以检验其与 Schramm-Loewner 演化（SLE）和二维高斯自由场（Gaussian free field）理论预测的一致性。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟方法，在周期边界条件的 $L\times L$ 方格上生成离散时间简单随机游走（sRW），步数为 $L^2$，以此构建游走簇并分析其几何特征。

Result: 簇质量渐近行为符合 $M/L^2 \simeq (\ln L)^{-1} [\fracπ{2}+b (\ln L)^{-2}]$，呈现“对数分形”（logarithmic fractals）；外缘分形维数 $d_{\rm hull}=1.333\,29(14)$，精确吻合 SLE₈/₃ 预测值 $4/3$；化学距离 $S$ 渐近标度为 $S\sim L(\ln L)^{1/4}$，恰好达到二维高斯自由场水平集逾渗的理论上界。

Conclusion: 简单随机游走（sRW）簇具有共形不变（conformally invariant）的外缘，并包含渐近高效的线型连接路径。

Abstract: We present a Monte Carlo study of the fractal geometry of clusters formed by discrete-time simple random walks (sRW) of $L^2$ steps on a periodic square $L\times L$ lattice. We verify with high precision that the asymptotic behavior of the cluster mass follows $M/L^2 \simeq (\ln L)^{-1} [\fracπ{2}+b (\ln L)^{-2}]$, with $b\approx -(π/2)^{-2}$, demonstrating marginal ``logarithmic fractals". We further determine the fractal dimension of the hull to be $d_{\rm hull}=1.333\,29(14)=4/3$, in excellent agreement with the prediction of Schramm-Loewner evolution ($\rm SLE_{8/3}$) for the Brownian frontier universality class. More importantly, we analyze the chemical distance $S$ spanning the cluster and obtain strong evidence that it asymptotically scales as $S\sim L(\ln L)^{1/4}$, lying exactly on the theoretical upper bound for the chemical distance for level-set percolation clusters on the two-dimensional Gaussian free field. Our numerical results show that the sRW cluster exhibits a conformally invariant external frontier and contains highly efficient asymptotically linear connective paths.

### [118] [Time-Uniform Error Bound for Temporal Coarse Graining in Markovian Open Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21366)
*Teruhiro Ikeuchi,Takashi Mori*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对从Born-Markov量子主方程（如Redfield方程）推导Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad（GKSL）生成元时使用的多种近似方法，引入了一种称为时间粗粒化（temporal coarse graining）的统一分析框架，并推导出了具有时间一致性的严格误差界，解决了现有误差界在长时间极限下发散的根本问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立从Born-Markov量子主方程（如Redfield方程）到GKSL生成元的各类近似方法（如旋转波近似、时间平均近似等）的严格误差界，在基础理论和实际应用中均具有重要意义。然而，现有误差界存在两大缺陷：一是具有高度方法特异性，缺乏统一性；二是更关键的是，在长时间极限下发散，仅能保证短时间尺度下的近似准确性。

Method: 作者提出了一种称为时间粗粒化（temporal coarse graining）的一般性近似方法类，将旋转波近似（rotating-wave approximation）、时间平均近似（time-averaging approximation）和几何-算术近似（geometric-arithmetic approximation）等所有前述方案统一纳入该框架，并基于此推导了统一的、严格的误差界。

Result: 推导出的误差界具有时间均匀性（time-uniform），即在耗散时间尺度（dissipation timescale）显著长于环境关联时间尺度（bath correlation timescale）的条件下，通过时间粗粒化获得的GKSL生成元能够在任意长时间尺度下保持准确性。

Conclusion: 该工作同时解决了现有误差界面临的缺乏统一性和长时间发散两大问题，为量子主方程近似方法的可靠性提供了更坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: Several approximation procedures, such as the full or partial rotating-wave, time-averaging, and geometric-arithmetic approximations, have been proposed to derive Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad (GKSL) generators from the Born-Markov quantum master equation (e.g., the Redfield equation). Establishing rigorous error bounds for these approximations is of fundamental and practical importance. However, existing bounds face two major limitations: they are highly specific to individual methods, and, more critically, they diverge in the long-time limit, ensuring the accuracy of the derived GKSL generator only in short-time regimes. In this Letter, we resolve both issues by deriving a unified, rigorous error bound for a general class of approximation methods -- termed temporal coarse graining -- that encompasses all aforementioned schemes. Crucially, our error bound is time-uniform. This guarantees that GKSL generators obtained via temporal coarse graining remain accurate for arbitrarily long times, provided the dissipation timescale is significantly longer than the bath correlation timescale.

</details>


### [119] [How to quantify long-time rotational motion in molecular systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21512)
*Romain Simon,Hadrien Bobas,François Villemot,Jean-Louis Barrat,Ludovic Berthier*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量化分子流体旋转运动的方法在处理复杂旋转动力学（如过冷液体接近玻璃转变时的慢速、异质或间歇性旋转）时会失效，导致文献中存在不一致结果，尤其影响对旋转-平移运动解耦以及德拜-斯托克斯-爱因斯坦关系违背等问题的讨论。

Method: 本文首先简要综述现有旋转量化方法，指出它们无法从扩散流体到受阻固体的全过程准确捕捉旋转动力学演化。随后提出一套经验性方法，并设计了一族基于连续时间随机行走（continuous time random walk, CTRW）的旋转动力学模型进行基准测试。

Result: 新方法能够正确量化自由旋转运动与被囚禁旋转运动的统计特征，以及非高斯（non-Gaussian）和非菲克（non-Fickian）旋转动力学行为。

Conclusion: 提出的经验方法有效解决了现有方法的系统性缺陷，有望为过冷分子流体旋转运动中的动态异质性（dynamic heterogeneity）提供更优的表征。

Abstract: We show that all existing methods quantifying rotational motion in molecular fluids eventually fail in systems undergoing complex rotational motion characterised by slow, heterogeneous, or intermittent dynamics. This impacts in particular the study of rotational dynamics in molecular supercooled liquids near their glass transition, as well as discussions of the decoupling between rotational and translational motion and violations of the Debye-Stokes-Einstein relation. We present a brief overview of existing methods and explain why none of them can accurately capture the evolution of rotational dynamics from a diffusive fluid to an arrested solid, thus resolving inconsistent literature results. We then introduce an empirical method that efficiently solves all issues. We benchmark our method devising a family of continuous time random walk models for rotational dynamics. Our method correctly quantifies the statistics of free and caged rotational motion, as well as non-Gaussian and non-Fickian rotational dynamics, and should allow a better characterisation of dynamic heterogeneity in the rotational motion of supercooled molecular fluids.

</details>


### [120] [Dean-Kawasaki fluctuating hydrodynamics for backscattering hard rods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21553)
*Mrinal Jyoti Powdel*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究一维反向散射硬杆（backscattering hard rods）系统，其中硬杆以速率 γ 翻转速度符号，导致速度奇次矩衰减而偶次矩守恒，即守恒量数量减半。通过 Dean-Kawasaki 涨落流体力学（fluctuating hydrodynamics）框架，发现当时间 t ≫ 1/γ 时密度-密度关联呈扩散传播，而 t ≪ 1/γ 时呈弹道传播。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准一维硬杆系统具有弹道输运特性，而本文通过在硬杆中引入速度翻转率 γ 作为可积性破坏（integrability-breaking）扰动，探究该扰动如何改变系统的输运性质。

Method: 基于 Dean-Kawasaki 涨落流体力学（Dean-Kawasaki fluctuating hydrodynamics）形式，对一维反向散射硬杆系统的密度-密度关联函数进行理论分析。

Result: 在长时间尺度 t ≫ 1/γ，密度-密度关联表现为扩散（diffusive）传播；在短时间尺度 t ≪ 1/γ，关联表现为弹道（ballistic）传播。

Conclusion: 速度翻转率的引入破坏了系统的可积性，导致输运行为从弹道转变为扩散，且时间标度由 1/γ 主导。

Abstract: We study a system of backscattering hard rods in one dimension. Contrary to the usual ballistic hard rods, these hard rods flip the sign of their velocities with a rate $γ$. This leads to the decay of the odd moments of velocity while preserving the even moments: the number of conserved quantities in the system becomes half. The introduction of the flipping rate, $γ$, is a kind of integrability-breaking perturbation. One expects a change in the transport properties in the system due to the integrability breaking. We show using a Dean-Kawasaki fluctuating hydrodynamic formulation that for $t \gg 1/γ$, the two-time density density correlation spreads in a diffusive manner, and for $t \ll 1/γ$, the correlation spreads ballistically.

</details>


### [121] [Novel dynamics for an inertial polar tracer in an active bath](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21762)
*Jing-Bo Zeng,Ji-Hui Pei*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过投影算符形式将沉浸于活性浴中的重极性示踪粒子约化为随机洛伦兹方程，发现其诱导动力学远非简单推进，而是呈现多种运动模式，包括活性布朗运动、手性活性布朗运动、复杂混沌运动及锯齿状活性布朗运动，并数值验证了相关解析结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知极性示踪粒子（polar tracer）在活性浴（active bath）中会被推动向前并被激活，但惯性示踪粒子的诱导动力学可能比预期更丰富，因此需要深入探索其潜在的多模态行为。

Method: 采用投影算符形式（projection-operator formalism）对独立活性布朗粒子（active Brownian particles）浴进行积分消去，将示踪粒子的约化动力学映射为随机洛伦兹方程（stochastic Lorenz equation）。

Result: 依据洛伦兹方程吸引子的类型，示踪粒子的运动可被分类为活性布朗运动（active Brownian motion）、手性活性布朗运动（chiral active Brownian motion）、复杂混沌运动（complex chaotic motion）及锯齿状活性布朗运动（zigzag active Brownian motion）。对于特定运动模式，推导出了推进速度、速度协方差及有效扩散系数（effective diffusion coefficient）的解析表达式。

Conclusion: 理论预测得到了数值模拟（numerical simulations）的验证，表明惯性示踪粒子在活性浴中的诱导动力学比传统认知更为丰富多样。

Abstract: A polar tracer immersed in an active bath is known to be propelled forward and therefore activated. Here we report that the induced dynamics of an inertial tracer can be much richer than expected. We investigate a heavy polar tracer immersed in a bath of independent active Brownian particles. Using the projection-operator formalism to integrate out the bath, we show that the tracer's reduced dynamics can be mapped to a stochastic Lorenz equation. According to the attractors in the Lorenz equation, the tracer motion is classified into several different dynamical regimes, including active Brownian motion, chiral active Brownian motion, complex chaotic motion, and zigzag active Brownian motion. For certain regimes, we derive analytical expressions for the propulsion speed, the velocity covariance, and the effective diffusion coefficient. Numerical simulations corroborate these theoretical predictions.

</details>

### [122] [Chaotic migration of LISA Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals in a turbulent accretion disk: effect on waveform de-phasing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20971)
*Mudit Garg,Lucio Mayer,Yinhao Wu,Yacine Ali-Haïmoud,Douglas N. C. Lin*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究针对LISA引力波探测器将观测到的极端质量比旋进（EMRI）系统，提出了一种基于高斯分布模拟湍流力矩（$T_{\rm turb}$）的通用参数化方案。计算表明，在某些参数条件下，仅考虑线性力矩（$T_{\rm lin}$）时气体引起的引力波相位偏移（$Δψ_{\rm gas}$）不可观测；但若EMRI因湍流气体发生混沌迁移，则该偏移可能变得可探测，从而驱动未来开展长时标磁流体动力学（MHD）模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有的EMRI气体效应研究大多假设吸积盘为薄层流盘（thin laminar disk），忽略湍流，但盘内部因磁旋转不稳定性（magneto-rotational instability）必然存在湍流。因此，需要发展更一般的湍流力矩模型来评估其对引力波相位偏移的影响。

Method: 基于一项全局流体动力学（hydrodynamical, HD）研究的最新进展，将湍流力矩（$T_{\rm turb}$）建模为围绕线性力矩（$T_{\rm lin}$）的高斯分布（Gaussian distribution），提出一种通用的、与具体模型无关的参数化方案。然后针对一个“黄金”圆轨道EMRI系统（总质量$M=10^6~{\rm M}_\odot$，质量比$q=5\times10^{-5}$），在其最后四年演化期内，改变Eddington比率（${\rm f}_{\rm Edd}$）、湍流归一化系数$C$、盘厚宽比（$h_0$）及湍流-黏滞系数（$α$）等参数，计算气体引起的相位偏移$Δψ_{\rm gas}$。

Result: 当${\rm f}_{\rm Edd}\gtrsim0.3$、$C\gtrsim300$、$h_0\gtrsim0.03$、$α\gtrsim0.1$时，仅考虑$T_{\rm lin}$的相位偏移不可观测；但若考虑湍流引起的混沌迁移（chaotic migration），$Δψ_{\rm gas}$可超过可探测阈值（$Δψ_{\rm gas}>8/{\rm SNR}$），变得可被LISA探测。

Conclusion: 该研究为EMRI在湍流环境中的引力波可探测性提供了理论依据，并推动未来在EMRI早期旋进阶段开展长时标磁流体动力学（MHD）模拟，以理解其轨道演化及湍流环境对引力波波形的影响。

Abstract: Gravitational wave (GW) detector LISA will observe near-coalescence extreme mass ratio inspirals (EMRIs), which typically form in galactic central accretion disks. Gas torques on EMRI will alter its GW-driven inspiral trajectory from the vacuum expectation, leading to potentially LISA-observable GW dephasing ($Δψ_{\rm gas}$). Most studies compute $Δψ_{\rm gas}$ for a thin, laminar disk, with negligible flow turbulence, where the disk exerts a fairly well-understood linear torque ($T_{\rm lin}$). However, these disks must be turbulent due to magneto-rotational instability in the inner regions. Hence, we present a proof-of-concept general, agnostic prescription for the turbulent torque ($T_{\rm turb}$) acting on an EMRI by modeling it as a Gaussian distribution around $T_{\rm lin}$, based on recent advances from a global hydrodynamical (HD) study. We compute $Δψ_{\rm gas}$ for the ``golden'' circular EMRI with total source mass $M=10^6~{\rm M}_\odot$ and mass ratio $q=5\times10^{-5}$ in its final four-year evolution at redshift $z=0.276$ and signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) $=50$ by varying Eddington ratio ${\rm f}_{\rm Edd}$, turbulence normalization $C$ ($=~360$ in the aforementioned HD study), disk aspect ratio $h_0$, and turbo-viscous coefficient $α$ in a reasonable parameters space. We find that for ${\rm f}_{\rm Edd}\gtrsim0.3$, $C\gtrsim300$, $h_0\gtrsim0.03$, and $α\gtrsim0.1$, gas-induced dephasings are unobservable if only considering $T_{\rm lin}$ but could become detectable ($Δψ_{\rm gas}>8/$SNR) if EMRIs exhibit chaotic migration due to turbulent gas flow. Hence, this work motivates running MHD simulations of accretion disks with embedded LISA EMRIs in the early in-spiral phase over long enough timescales to understand the evolution of their orbital elements and the imprint of the turbulent environment on their gravitational waveforms.

</details>

### [123] [Universal Local Roughness from Disorder Crossover in Urban-Front Growth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21437)
*Martin Hendrick,Maximilian Trique,Gabriele Manoli*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过引入受地理约束（geographic constraints）影响的Eden模型，揭示了城市扩展前沿（urban expansion fronts）中局部粗糙度稳定（约1/2）与非通用动态标度行为共存的现象，源于由无序（disorder）控制的前沿生长从二维逾渗（percolation）到KPZ行为的交叉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 城市扩展前沿的观测数据显示，局部粗糙度指数（local roughness exponent）鲁棒但动态指数（dynamic exponents）高度分散且非普适，现有理论难以同时解释这两种矛盾特征。作者旨在建立最小模型来解释这一共存现象。

Method: 引入一个最小Eden模型（minimal Eden model），将地理约束建模为淬灭稀释（quenched dilution），将聚并（coalescence）建模为淬灭局部加速（quenched local acceleration），模拟投影前沿（projected-front）的生长过程。

Result: 模型中的前沿生长经历一个长的预渐近（preasymptotic）标度区，受普通二维逾渗（ordinary two-dimensional percolation）控制，随后交叉到渐近的KPZ（Kardar–Parisi–Zhang）生长。在该预渐近区，局部粗糙度保持在约1/2附近，而大尺度指数随无序和加速参数发生广泛变化。

Conclusion: 该模型为城市前沿的粗糙化提供了最小解释，并暗示了一种在异质介质（heterogeneous media）中随机生长的更一般机制。

Abstract: Urban expansion fronts display a robust local roughness exponent together with strongly dispersed growth and nonuniversal dynamic exponents. We show that this coexistence can arise from a disorder-controlled crossover in projected-front growth. Introducing a minimal Eden model, in which geographic constraints act as quenched dilution and coalescence as quenched local acceleration, we demonstrate that the resulting front evolves through a long preasymptotic regime controlled by ordinary two-dimensional percolation before crossing over to asymptotic KPZ growth. In this regime, the local roughness remains close to $1/2$, while the large-scale exponents vary broadly with disorder and acceleration. These results provide a minimal explanation of urban-front roughening and suggest a more general mechanism for stochastic growth in heterogeneous media.

</details>

### [124] [Unified Hydrodynamic Analogue of Aharonov-Bohm and Lense-Thirring Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21543)
*Aditya Singh,Joseph Samuel,Chien-chia Liu,Luiza Angheluta,Andrés Concha,Mahesh Bandi*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过浴缸排水涡旋（draining-bathtub vortex）中的表面波，在一个单一流体系统中同时实现了阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆相位偏移（Aharonov-Bohm phase shifts）和伦斯-瑟林框架拖曳（Lense-Thirring frame dragging）的流体动力学类比。实验验证了理论预测，从而建立了一个可通过可测速度场研究拓扑相位和惯性效应的实验室平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该工作的动机是在一个统一的实验系统中，同时实现规范物理（gauge physics）中的阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆效应和引力物理（gravitational physics）中的伦斯-瑟林框架拖曳的流体动力学类比，从而为研究拓扑相位和惯性效应提供一个可控的实验室平台。

Method: 通过一个静态时间变换将平坦的(2+1)维波动方程映射到对流浅水方程，得到一个由背景流场设置的有效矢量势（effective vector potential）。在该几何中，环量（circulation）定义了一个全局相位和乐（global phase holonomy），用于控制波结构。对于非整数环量，问题在通用覆盖空间（universal cover）上自然定义，以确保单值分波解。

Result: 行波呈现出阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆散射特征的波前位错（wavefront dislocations）；驻波叠加产生以环量决定的角速度旋转的节线模式，提供了框架拖曳的直接类比。在受控涡旋上的实验验证了这些理论预测。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个可测量的速度场来模拟规范物理和引力物理中核心的拓扑相位与惯性效应的实验室平台，表明经典流体系统可用于模拟量子与引力现象。

Abstract: We show that surface waves in a draining-bathtub vortex provide a hydrodynamic realization of both Aharonov-Bohm phase shifts and Lense-Thirring frame dragging within a single system. A static time transformation maps the flat (2+1)-dimensional wave equation onto the convected shallow-water equation, yielding an effective vector potential set by the background flow. In this geometry, the circulation defines a global phase holonomy that controls wave structure. Traveling waves exhibit wavefront dislocations characteristic of Aharonov-Bohm scattering, while standing-wave superpositions produce nodal patterns that rotate at an angular velocity fixed by the circulation, providing a direct analogue of frame dragging. For noninteger circulation, the problem is naturally defined on the universal cover, ensuring single-valued partial-wave solutions. Experiments on a controlled vortex confirm these predictions and establish a laboratory platform in which topological phase and inertial effects, central to gauge and gravitational physics, emerge from a measurable velocity field.

</details>

### [125] [Embedded special Legendrian surfaces in $\mathbb S^5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21521)
*Sebastian Heller,Franz Pedit,Charles Ouyang*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文首次构造了\(\mathbb S^5\)中亏格大于1的光滑嵌入紧致特殊勒让德曲面（special Legendrian surfaces）。具体而言，对于每个足够大的整数\(k\)，构造了一个嵌入的特殊勒让德曲面，其共形结构（conformal structure）为费马曲线（Fermat curve），次数为\(k\)，亏格为\(\tfrac12(k-1)(k-2)\)。方法结合了初等隐函数定理（implicit function theorem）、基于环代数（loop algebra）值亚纯联络（meromorphic connections）的特殊勒让德曲面描述，以及三穿孔球面（thrice-punctured sphere）的\(\mathrm{SL}_3(\mathbb C)\)-特征簇（character variety）中幺正化轨迹（unitarizability locus）的刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在五维球面\(\mathbb S^5\)中构造亏格大于1的光滑嵌入紧致特殊勒让德曲面，这一几何对象此前未有构造实例，填补了相关研究的空白。

Method: 方法包括三个核心要素：初等隐函数定理（用于存在性和光滑性论证）、利用环代数值亚纯联络描述特殊勒让德曲面（提供代数—几何框架），以及对三穿孔球面的\(\mathrm{SL}_3(\mathbb C)\)-特征簇中幺正化轨迹的刻画（确保嵌入性与紧致性）。

Result: 对于每个足够大的整数\(k\)，成功构造了嵌入的特殊勒让德曲面，其共形结构为次数\(k\)的费马曲线，亏格为\(\tfrac12(k-1)(k-2)\)。这是首批亏格大于1的光滑嵌入紧致特殊勒让德曲面在\(\mathbb S^5\)中的构造实例。

Conclusion: 该构造展示了隐函数定理与环代数联络、特征簇刻画相结合的有效性，为高维球面中特殊拉格朗日几何（special Lagrangian geometry）的类比对象——特殊勒让德几何提供了新的非平凡例子，并为进一步研究其模空间与形变理论奠定了基础。

Abstract: We construct the first smooth embedded compact special Legendrian surfaces in \(\mathbb S^5\) of genus greater than one. More precisely, for every sufficiently large integer \(k\), we construct an embedded special Legendrian surface whose conformal structure is the Fermat curve of degree \(k\) and genus \(\tfrac12(k-1)(k-2)\). Our approach combines an elementary implicit function theorem with the description of special Legendrian surfaces via loop algebra-valued meromorphic connections and a characterization of the unitarizability locus in the ${SL}_{3}(\mathbb C)$-character variety of the thrice-punctured sphere.

### [126] [Quantum Mixing for Schrödinger eigenfunctions in Benjamini-Schramm limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21582)
*Kai Hippi,Félix Lequen,Søren Mikkelsen,Tuomas Sahlsten,Henrik Ueberschär*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文证明了一类双曲曲面上的薛定谔算子在 Benjamini-Schramm 收敛条件下的量子混合（quantum mixing）性质，适用于大度数提升、随机双曲曲面及 Hartree 单粒子算子等场景；证明基于双曲波动方程的 Duhamel 公式与测地流（geodesic flow）的指数混合性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在双曲曲面上建立量子混合性质，特别是当曲面序列 Benjamini-Schramm 收敛到双曲平面 $\mathbb{H}$ 时，验证势能扰动下的特征函数在充分大的谱窗口内的混合行为。

Method: 利用双曲波动方程（hyperbolic wave equation）的 Duhamel 公式，并结合切丛 $T^1 X_n$ 上测地流（geodesic flow）的指数混合性（exponential mixing）进行证明。

Result: 对于均匀离散且具有一致谱间隙（uniform spectral gap）的紧致双曲曲面序列 $(X_n)$，当 $V \in L^p(\mathbb{H}) \cap L^\infty(\mathbb{H})$ 且 $p>0$ 时，扰动薛定谔算子 $-Δ_{X_n}+V_n$ 在任意足够大的谱窗口 $I$ 内满足量子混合。

Conclusion: 该结果适用于大度数提升、算术曲面的同余覆盖（congruence covers）、Weil-Petersson 模型下的高亏格随机双曲曲面，以及双曲曲面上多体玻色气体热力学极限中的 Hartree 单粒子算子。

Abstract: Let $-Δ_{\mathbb{H}}+V$ be the Schrödinger operator on $\mathbb{H}$ where $V \in L^p(\mathbb{H}) \cap L^\infty(\mathbb{H})$ for some $p > 0$. If $(X_n)$ is a uniformly discrete sequence of compact hyperbolic surfaces with a uniform spectral gap that Benjamini-Schramm converges to $\mathbb{H}$, we prove quantum mixing for the eigenfunctions of $-Δ_{X_n}+V_n$ in any sufficiently large spectral window $I$, where $V_n$ is the potential on $X_n$ induced by $V$. These apply to large degree lifts of a potential on a base surface such as congruence covers of arithmetic surfaces, with high probability to random hyperbolic surfaces in the Weil-Petersson model of large genus, and to Hartree one-particle operators arising in thermodynamic limit of many-body Bose gas on hyperbolic surfaces. The proof uses the Duhamel formula for the hyperbolic wave equation together with exponential mixing of the geodesic flow on $T^1 X_n$.

Abstract: Scalable synthesis remains the gate between MOF discovery and industrial deployment, as scale-up know-how is fragmented across disparate reports. ### [128] [Evolution of the Saddle Point in Antimony Telluride Homologous Superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21037)
*Yi-Hsin Shen,Shane Smolenski,Ming Wen,Yimo Hou,Eoghan Downey,Jakob Hammond-Renfro,Katharine Moncrieffe,Chun Lin,Makoto Hashimoto,Donghui Lu,Kai Sun,Dominika Zgid,Emanuel Gull,Pierre Ferdinand P. Poudeu,Na Hyun Jo,Rachel S. Goldman*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过扫描隧道谱（scanning tunneling spectroscopy）和角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy）实验，在碲化锑同系超晶格中证实了M点附近的存在鞍点（saddle point）及其相关的范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularity），并揭示了Sb和Te的p_z轨道杂化在驱动该奇点向费米能级移动中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理论预测碲化锑在M点存在鞍点，且锑烯层会将M点价带推向费米能级（Fermi level），但此前该鞍点尚未被实验证实，且同系超晶格的研究仅限于添加一到两层锑烯的情况。

Method: 采用扫描隧道谱（scanning tunneling spectroscopy, STS）和角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES），对一系列包含二至四层锑烯（antimonene）的碲化锑同系超晶格（homologous superlattices）进行了系统研究。

Result: 实验证实了M点附近存在鞍点及其关联的范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularity），并发现Sb和Te的p_z轨道杂化（orbital hybridization）是将范霍夫奇点驱动至费米能级的关键因素。

Conclusion: 将拓扑绝缘体（topological insulators）与拓扑半金属（topological semimetals）以同系超晶格形式结合，是一种通过费米能级与能带极值对齐来产生关联量子物质（correlated quantum matter）的有效途径；Sb和Te的p_z轨道杂化在其中起核心作用。

Abstract: Combining topological insulators with topological semimetals in the form of homologous superlattices is a promising approach for generating correlated quantum matter based upon Fermi level alignment with band extrema. For antimony telluride, a saddle point is predicted to occur at the M-point, while antimonene layering is predicted to move the M-point valence band towards the Fermi level. To date, the predicted saddle point at the M-point has not yet been demonstrated, and studies of antimony telluride homologous superlattices have been limited to one or two layers of antimonene added to antimony telluride. Here, we present scanning tunneling spectroscopy and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy studies of a series of antimony telluride homologous superlattices with two to four layers of antimonene. In addition to demonstrating the presence of a saddle point and associated van Hove singularity near the M-point, we identify the key role of Sb and Te $p_z$ orbital hybridization in driving the van Hove singularity toward the Fermi level.

### [129] [Expanding the extreme-k dielectric materials space through physics-validated generative reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21068)
*Hossain Hridoy,Tahiya Chowdhury,Md Shafayat Hossain*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出DielecMIND框架，将材料发现从数据库筛选问题重构为基于推理的探索过程，首次将大语言模型（large language model）假设生成与第一性原理（first-principles）计算相结合。在high-κ介电材料这一数据稀缺领域，该框架在已知仅14种材料的基础上，新发现并验证了5种高介电常数化合物（κ > 150），将此类稀有材料类别单次扩充了35%。其中Ba₂TiHfO₆的介电常数达637、低频损耗极低且热稳定性高达800 K，展示了AI引导发现稀有高影响力功能材料的新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 技术关键材料往往存在于化学空间中极为狭窄的区域，受多重物理约束制约，在现有数据库中稀疏出现。这种稀缺性从根本上限制了当前基于机器学习的数据驱动材料发现方法，因为模型擅长插值（interpolation）却难以生成真正的新候选物。因此，需要一种能够在数据稀缺条件下有效探索新化学空间的方法。

Method: DielecMIND框架将材料发现重新定义为推理驱动的探索（reasoning-driven exploration）。该框架首次结合了大语言模型（large language model, LLM）的假设生成能力与经过物理验证的第一性原理计算（first-principles calculation），以在已知化合物之外导航化学空间。以高介电常数（high-κ）电介质作为数据稀缺且技术要求严苛的测试案例。

Result: 在已知仅有14种实验或计算验证的κ > 150材料的前提下，DielecMIND发现并验证了5种新的此类化合物，将这一稀有材料类别单次扩充了35%。其中Ba₂TiHfO₆的介电常数达637，在低光频率下损耗极小，且热稳定性高达800 K。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了一种AI引导发现的新范式：不依赖大规模数据库筛选，而是生成数量有限但物理基础扎实、实验可行的候选物，却能显著扩展稀疏的功能材料空间。DielecMIND指向了一种在数据稀缺长期制约进展的情况下，发现稀有、高影响力功能材料的通用策略。

Abstract: The most technologically consequential materials are often the rarest: they occupy narrow regions of chemical space, obey competing physical constraints, and appear only sparsely in existing databases. High-kappa dielectrics, high-Tc superconductors, and ferromagnetic insulators are to name a few. This scarcity fundamentally limits today's data-driven materials discovery, where machine-learning models excel at interpolation but struggle to generate genuinely new candidates. Here, we introduce DielecMIND, an artificial intelligence framework that reframes materials discovery as a reasoning-driven exploration instead of a database-screening problem. Using high-kappa dielectrics as a data-scarce and technologically stringent test case, DielecMIND combines large-language-model hypothesis generation for the first time with physics validated first-principles calculation to navigate chemical space beyond known compounds. Prior to our work, only 14 experimentally or computationally validated materials with kappa > 150 were known. Our framework discovers and validates 5 new such compounds, expanding this rare-materials class by a remarkable = 35% in a single study. Among them, we find that Ba2TiHfO6 exhibits a dielectric constant of 637, minimal loss at low optical frequencies, and stability up to 800 K. Beyond dielectrics, this work demonstrates a new paradigm for artificial-intelligence-guided discovery: one that generates a small number of physically grounded, experimentally plausible candidates yet measurably expands sparsely populated functional materials spaces. Thus, DielecMIND points toward a general strategy for discovering rare, high-impact functional materials where data scarcity has long constrained progress.

</details>

*Arun Mannodi-Kanakkithodi,Menglin Huang,Prashun Gorai,Seán R. Kavanagh*

Conclusion: 数据驱动和机器学习方法为加速固态点缺陷模拟提供了有效途径，未来应进一步将模型输出与实验数据连接，推动该新兴子领域的持续发展。

Abstract: Point defects in solid-state materials are now routinely simulated using large supercell structures, requiring efficient quantum mechanical solutions. In this article, we provide an overview of prominent efforts to accelerate defect simulations using these approaches. In addition to geometry relaxation and formation energy predictions, these interatomic potentials are capable of predicting phonon modes and vibrational free energies to yield defect energetics at finite temperatures -- representing a key frontier for computational defect research. We finish with a discussion on how to connect these approaches and their outputs with experimental data, and provide an outlook on this burgeoning sub-field.

### [131] [Generative Discovery of Magnetic Insulators under Competing Physical Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21073)
*Qiulin Zeng,Tahiya Chowdhury,Md Shafayat Hossain*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出MagMatLLM，一种基于约束引导生成（constraint-guided generative）的材料发现框架，整合语言模型晶体生成、进化选择、代理筛选与第一性原理验证，成功识别出12种此前未知的磁性绝缘体（magnetic insulators），其中10种经声子分析证实具有动态稳定性（dynamic stability）、有限带隙（finite band gaps）与非零磁矩（nonzero magnetic moments）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: MagMatLLM框架集成四个模块：基于语言模型（language model）的晶体生成、进化选择（evolutionary selection）、代理筛选（surrogate screening）和第一性原理验证（first-principles validation）。与传统的稳定性优先（stability-first）方法不同，该框架在生成和筛选阶段同时施加功能约束（functional constraints），将搜索导向由竞争性物理需求定义的稀疏材料空间区域。

Conclusion: 这项工作建立了面向多目标材料发现（multi-objective materials discovery）的通用约束引导范式（constraint-guided paradigm），适用于稀疏化学空间（sparse chemical spaces），并为在竞争性物理约束下设计量子材料（quantum materials）提供了可迁移的策略。

Abstract: Discovering materials that must simultaneously satisfy multiple competing constraints remains a central challenge in computational materials design, particularly in data-scarce regimes where conventional data-driven approaches are least effective. Magnetic insulators represent a stringent example: the electronic conditions that favor magnetic order often also promote metallicity, while insulating behavior suppresses the interactions that stabilize magnetism. As a result, experimentally viable magnetic insulators are rare and difficult to identify through conventional screening. Here, we introduce MagMatLLM, a constraint-guided generative discovery framework that integrates language-model-based crystal generation with evolutionary selection, surrogate screening, and first-principles validation to target simultaneous stability, magnetism, and insulating behavior. Unlike stability-first approaches, the framework enforces functional constraints during generation and selection, steering the search toward sparsely populated regions of materials space defined by competing physical requirements. Using this workflow, we identify twelve previously unreported candidate magnetic insulators, including Tm$_4$Co$_2$Cr$_2$O$_{12}$ and Cr$_4$Nb$_2$O$_{12}$. Of these, ten are dynamically stable by phonon analysis and exhibit finite band gaps and nonzero magnetic moments in spin-polarized density functional theory calculations. Beyond the specific compounds identified here, this work establishes a general constraint-guided paradigm for multi-objective materials discovery in sparse chemical spaces and provides a transferable strategy for the design of quantum materials under competing physical constraints.

### [132] [Neutron and X-ray Diffraction Reveal the Limits of Long-Range Machine Learning Potentials for Medium-Range Order in Silica Glass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21222)
*Sai Harshit Balantrapu,Atul C. Thakur,Chris Benmore,Ganesh Sivaraman*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过结合中子/X射线衍射实验和基于MACE的短程与长程势模型，系统研究了机器学习原子间势（MLIPs）在预测无序二氧化硅中程有序（MRO）时的局限性。结果表明，在短程势过度结构化网络产生过高第一尖锐衍射峰（FSDP），而引入长程相互作用虽改善液态结构，却仍无法正确描述玻化后的非晶MRO。两类模型均因保留过多母液网络记忆而导致动力学陷阱和非物理的中程构型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 玻璃态二氧化硅是光学和电子学中的基础材料，但准确预测其中程有序（medium-range order, MRO）对机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potentials, MLIPs）而言仍是重大挑战。局域MLIP虽能复现短程SiO4四面体网络，但局域性是否足以恢复第一尖锐衍射峰（first sharp diffraction peak, FSDP）——MRO的主要实验标志——尚不清楚。因此，本研究旨在探究MLIPs在预测无序二氧化硅MRO方面的能力与局限。

Method: 结合中子与X射线衍射实验，以及基于两个MACE模型（短程势SR和引入倒易空间门控注意力的长程扩展LR）驱动的大规模分子动力学模拟。采用环统计和键角分析比较模型与实验的结构特征，并评估短程势与长程势在液态和玻璃态下的表现。

Result: 短程势SR模型对网络进行了过度结构化，在液态和玻璃态均产生过高的FSDP。长程LR模型降低了液态中过多的有序性，改善了与实验的吻合度，但淬火后仍未能恢复实验非晶MRO。环统计和键角分析显示，SR模型具有以六元环为主的过窄分布，LR模型环分布更宽但仍存偏差；两个模型在Si-O-Si角度上均表现出有限变异性，表明网络柔性受约束。这些结构特征说明两种模型都保留了对母液网络的过度记忆。

Conclusion: 明确的远程相互作用对于无序二氧化硅的预测建模是必要的但非充分的。准确预测中程有序还需要能够充分表征液-玻璃转变的训练数据和采样策略。

Abstract: Glassy silica is a foundational material in optics and electronics, yet accurately predicting its medium-range order (MRO) remains a major challenge for machine-learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs). While local MLIPs reproduce the short-range SiO4 tetrahedral network well, it remains unclear whether locality alone is sufficient to recover the first sharp diffraction peak (FSDP), the principal experimental signature of MRO. Here, we combine neutron and X-ray diffraction measurements with large-scale molecular dynamics driven by two MACE-based models: a short-range (SR) potential and a long-range (LR) extension incorporating reciprocal-space gated attention. The SR model systematically over-structures the network, producing an overly intense FSDP in both the liquid and glassy states. Incorporating long-range interactions improves agreement with experiment for the liquid structure by reducing this excess ordering, but the LR model still fails to recover the experimental amorphous MRO after quenching. Ring-statistics and bond-angle analyses reveal that SR model exhibits an artificially narrow distribution dominated by six-membered rings, while the LR model produces a broader but still biased ring population. Despite preserving the correct tetrahedral geometry, both models show limited variability in Si-O-Si angles, indicating constrained network flexibility. These structural signatures demonstrate that both models retain excessive memory of the parent liquid network, leading to kinetically trapped and nonphysical medium-range configurations during vitrification. These results show that explicit long-range interactions are necessary but not sufficient for predictive modelling of disordered silica and suggest that accurate MRO further requires training data and sampling strategies that adequately represent the liquid-to-glass transition.

### [133] [Velocity-field characteristics and device performance in nanoscale amorphous oxide Thin-Film-Transistors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21225)
*Chankeun Yoon,Xiao Wang,Jatin Vikram Singh,Sanjay K. Banerjee,Ananth Dodabalapur*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于铟镓锌氧化物（IGZO）FETs的实验测量数据，结合基于物理的模型进行分析。载流子迁移率针对陷阱载流子散射（trapped carrier scattering）和光学声子散射（optical phonon scattering）等主要散射机制进行计算，载流子速度则通过修正的Caughey-Thomas方程从迁移率导出。模型还考虑了接触电阻（contact resistance）、焦耳热（Joule heating）和电场诱导的载流子加热（electric-field-induced carrier heating）。

Result: 载流子速度在高电场下呈现饱和趋势，所有诱导载流子（包括陷阱态和能带中）的平均速度超过2×10⁶ cm/s，而仅考虑能带载流子时速度超过4×10⁶ cm/s。

Conclusion: 该方法以IGZO为示例半导体进行了验证，可推广应用于多种新兴薄膜半导体，包括若干非晶氧化物半导体，为短沟道FETs的物理分析与设计提供通用框架。

Abstract: The electron velocity-electric field characteristics in short channel length (50-100 nm) amorphous oxide field-effect transistors (FETs) are described using measured experimental data from indium gallium zinc oxide (IGZO) FETs in conjunction with a physics-based model. Such understanding is crucial for the design of FETs for emerging applications such as in back-end-of-line circuitry for advanced memories and artificial intelligence hardware. In such semiconductor systems, there is an interplay between trapping and extended state (band) transport that has to be considered in detail for a more complete physical understanding of device operation. The approach described in this paper demonstrates such a method and its use for an exemplary semiconductor IGZO. It can be used in many emerging thin-film semiconductors, including several amorphous oxide semiconductors. The carrier mobility is calculated for dominant scattering mechanisms such as trapped carrier scattering and optical phonon scattering. The carrier velocity is computed from the mobility using a modified Caughey-Thomas equation. The physical model considers contact resistance, Joule heating, and electric-field-induced carrier heating, all of which are very important in small geometry FETs. The carrier velocity exhibits a tendency to saturate at high electric fields and reaches values > 2*10^6 cm/s when averaged over all induced carriers (both trapped and in the band) and > 4*10^6 cm/s for carriers in the band.

### [134] [Electrically switchable vacancy state revealed by in-operando positron experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21283)
*Ric Fulop,Laurence Lyons,Robert Nick,Marc H. Weber,Ming Liu,Haig Atikian,Uwe Bauer,Alexander C. Barbati,Neil Gershenfeld*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过正电子湮没谱学实验证明，铜在电流驱动下的“闪烧（flash）”状态涉及非平衡态弗仑克尔缺陷（Frenkel pair）的产生，而非仅由焦耳热（Joule heating）解释。空位浓度远超热平衡值（>10⁶倍），且完全可逆、依赖于电流存在；成核速率随电流陡增，将分钟级动力学与陶瓷烧结中的亚秒级闪光事件联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自2010年以来，关于电驱动固体中“闪烧（flash）”状态究竟是源于非平衡缺陷（non-equilibrium defect）的产生，还是仅由焦耳热（Joule heating）引起，一直存在争议。本文旨在通过实验手段直接区分这两种机制。

Method: 本文使用正电子湮没谱学（positron annihilation spectroscopy）中的多普勒展宽谱（Doppler Broadening Spectroscopy, DBS）和正电子寿命谱（positron lifetime spectroscopy）对铜进行原位测量，通过S参数的变化和寿命成分分析，定量表征电流作用下的空位缺陷浓度及其演化过程。

Result: 当施加电流超过临界密度时，DBS的S参数立即升高，撤去电流后数分钟内完全恢复，呈现完全可逆的电开关特性（electrically switchable）。正电子寿命谱独立确认了开路体积缺陷（open-volume defect）的存在，并揭示了从空位团簇（void）到空位簇（cluster）的弛豫层次。电流诱导的空位浓度比352°C下的热平衡浓度高出10⁶倍以上，且仅在电流施加期间存在；成核速率随电流呈陡峭标度关系。

Conclusion: 这些结果首次在金属中证实了电流诱导的弗仑克尔缺陷对（Frenkel-pair production）产生，并识别出闪烧状态中存在缺陷介导（defect-mediated）的非平衡贡献，而非单纯的焦耳热效应。

Abstract: Whether the flash state in electrically driven solids involves non-equilibrium defect production or is accounted for by Joule heating alone has been debated since 2010. Using positron annihilation spectroscopy on copper, we observe a fully reversible, electrically switchable vacancy population: the DBS S-parameter rises above baseline whenever applied current exceeds a critical density and returns on current removal. Positron lifetime spectroscopy independently confirms open-volume defect formation and reveals a void to cluster relaxation hierarchy. The current-induced vacancy concentration exceeds the thermal-equilibrium value at 352C by > 106x, is present only while current is applied, and vanishes within minutes. The nucleation rate scales steeply with the applied current, connecting the minute-scale kinetics resolved here to the sub-second flash events observed in ceramic sintering. These results demonstrate current-induced Frenkel-pair production in a metal and identify a defect-mediated, non-equilibrium contribution to the flash state.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在铁磁金属Fe₃GaTe₂中进行电输运测量，通过磁场的扫描观测第三阶NLAHE的磁滞行为，并利用标度分析（scaling analysis）确定其可能的物理起源。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一种通过非线性电输运研究磁性材料的途径，并为未来开发室温下工作的三阶非线性电子器件开辟了可能性。

Abstract: Berry curvature, as the imaginary component of quantum geometry, plays a crucial role in condensed matter physics. The spatial distribution of Berry curvature can be characterized by its dipole and multipole moments, which can induce the nonlinear anomalous Hall effect (NLAHE). To date, the NLAHE has been demonstrated in various materials, yet reports on room-temperature NLAHE are still limited. In this work, we report the observation of the third-order NLAHE in ferromagnetic metal Fe3GaTe2. The third-order NLAHE shows hysteretic behavior with the variation of magnetic field, where the coercive field is the same as that of the anomalous Hall effect, and the third-order NLAHE remains observable up to the Curie temperature (~350 K). The scaling analysis suggests that the third-order NLAHE may be attributed to the Berry curvature quadrupole. Our work not only provides an approach to study magnetic materials through nonlinear electric transports, but also opens up possibilities for the future development of room-temperature third-order nonlinear electronic devices.

### [136] [Navigating Order-(Dis)Order Family Trees via Group-Subgroup Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21386)
*Shuya Yamazaki,Yuyao Huang,Martin Hoffmann Petersen,Wei Nong,Kedar Hippalgaonkar*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于对称性的序-(无)序家系树（order-(dis)order family trees）框架，通过群-子群关系（group-subgroup relations）组织有序与无序结构，使新异性（novelty）评估得以显式化。实验表明，许多看似新颖的有序结构实际上是已知无序母相（disordered parent）的有序子相（ordered child），且对称性感知（symmetry-aware）的生成模型比对称性无关（symmetry-agnostic）模型更不易产生这类伪新颖结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着闭循环材料发现系统（closed-loop materials discovery systems）规模扩大至数百万候选化合物，所奖励新异性的可信度成为关键问题。现有新异性评估通常仅基于有序晶体结构（ordered crystal structures）数据库，忽略了许多预测的有序结构可能是已知无序相（disordered phase）的某种有序化排列，从而造成虚假的新颖性判断。

Method: 提出序-(无)序家系树框架，利用群-子群关系建立有序与无序结构之间的对称性关联。开发高通量家系匹配流程（high-throughput family matching procedure），为给定有序结构识别可能的无序母相及对称性相关的有序亲属，并应用于实验数据库（ICSD）、计算数据集（MP-20, Alex-MP-20, GNoME）以及晶体生成模型（crystal generative models）的基准测试。

Result: 在A-Lab合成案例研究中，该框架正确恢复了目标有序结构的已知无序母相。对实验与计算数据集的扩展分析揭示，许多单独看似新颖的有序结构实际上是已知序-(无)序家系树的成员。对称性无关的全原子生成模型（all-atom generative models）更频繁地产生源自已知无序母相的有序结构，而对称性约束模型（symmetry-constrained models）出现该行为的概率低2-4倍。

Conclusion: 序-(无)序家系树框架是实现数据驱动材料发现中真正新异性的关键要求。该工作为材料发现系统提供了一个基于对称性的新异性质控基准，揭示了对无序相的忽视可能导致大量伪新颖结构的系统性风险。

Abstract: As closed-loop materials discovery systems scale to produce millions of candidate compounds, the credibility of the novelty they reward becomes a critical concern. Novelty is commonly assessed against databases of ordered crystal structures, in which atomic sites are fully occupied. Yet, a predicted ordered structure may simply correspond to a particular ordering of a known disordered phase, whose sites are occupied by multiple species in the statistical average structure; we refer to such a structure as an ordered child of a disordered parent. Here, we introduce order-(dis)order family trees, a symmetry-based framework that organizes ordered and disordered structures through group-subgroup relations and enables novelty to be explicitly evaluated. We develop a high-throughput family matching procedure, to identify possible disordered parents and symmetry-related ordered relatives for a given ordered structure. As validation, we test our framework on synthesis-facing case studies (A-Lab), where it correctly recovers existing disordered parents for the targeted ordered structures. Extending this family-tree-based benchmark to experimental structure databases (ICSD), computational datasets (MP-20, Alex-MP-20, and GNoME), and crystal generative models further reveals that many ordered structures that appear novel as individual entries are, in fact, better understood as members of experimentally known order-(dis)order family trees. We also show that this is particularly evident in symmetry-agnostic all-atom generative models, which more frequently produce ordered structures derived from known disordered parents, whereas symmetry-constrained models are 2-4x less prone to this behavior. Our results establish order-(dis)order family trees as a key requirement for achieving genuine novelty in data-driven materials discovery.

</details>


### [137] [Identifying Oriented Spin Space Groups and Related Physical Properties Using an Online Platform FINDSPINGROUP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21397)

Conclusion: FINDSPINGROUP计算架构通过统一SSG与MSG框架，填补了不同时代发展的群论描述之间的空白，为非常规磁体的系统化发现和设计提供了计算基础设施，有望推动下一代自旋电子学材料的发展。

Abstract: Unconventional magnets that combine antiferromagnetic structures with ferromagnetic-like responses are essential for the development of next-generation spintronics. Their emergent properties are fundamentally dictated by the interplay between exchange-driven magnetic geometry and spin-orbit coupling, which are described by spin space group (SSG) and magnetic space group (MSG) frameworks, respectively. However, the lack of direct correspondence between these frameworks, developed in different eras, hinders the systematic tracking of symmetry evolution of these intertwined physical contributions. In this work, we introduce FINDSPINGROUP, a computational architecture that implements the recently emerged, oriented spin space group framework to unify SSG and MSG descriptions. By automating the tracking of symmetry-breaking pathways from the non-relativistic to the relativistic limit, this online platform enables the classification of magnetic phases and the derivation of symmetry-constrained tensors for phenomena such as momentum-dependent spin splitting and the anomalous Hall effect. By standardizing data exchange through the spin crystallographic information file, this architecture establishes a computational infrastructure for the high-throughput discovery and design of unconventional magnets.

By bridging the gap between uMLIPs and automated high-throughput workflows, GEWUM serves as a valuable framework to facilitate efficient and scalable materials exploration.

Preferential formation of single FA domains and a similar $χ_{33}$ anomaly are also observed in the isostructural compound PbMn$_2$Ni$_6$Te$_3$O$_{18}$. These findings suggest that the ferroaxial and magnetic characteristics within this structural framework are robust against Sr-Pb replacement.

### [140] [Intertwined charge density wave, tunable anti-dome superconductivity, and topological states in kagome metal VSn](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21488)

Method: 通过理论计算预测一种新型1:1 kagome金属VSn，并系统研究压力（pressure）和掺杂浓度（doping concentration）对其CDW序和超导电性的调控作用，分析声子模（phonon modes）硬化与软化以及能带重构（band reconstruction）的机制。

Conclusion: VSn中CDW、超导电性和拓扑现象的相互交织揭示了多种量子态之间的关联，为设计1:1 kagome超导拓扑金属提供了新思路，并为探索kagome体系中多相相互作用建立了研究平台。

Abstract: These years, kagome materials with 1:1 stoichiometry have garnered increasing attention, among which FeSn, CoSn, and FeGe have been the focus of current studies. However, all of them are antiferromagnetic, thereby hindering the observation of superconductivity and other novel physical properties. Here, we predict a novel 1:1 kagome metal VSn, which is an intrinsic charge density wave (CDW) material. Interestingly, with increasing pressure or doping concentration, the CDW order is progressively suppressed, followed by the emergence of superconductivity characterized by a non-monotonic transition temperature that exhibits a rare anti-dome-shaped dependence. Above a critical threshold, a reentrance of the CDW phase occurs. The anti-dome superconductivity originates from the first hardening and then softening of phonon modes, together with band reconstruction. Crucially, VSn retains nontrivial topological properties across the entire superconducting regime, a feature of paramount importance for realizing robust topological superconductivity. These intertwined CDW, superconductivity, and topological phenomena elucidate the correlations among multiple quantum states in VSn. Therefore, this research paves the way for for designing 1:1 kagome superconducting topological metals and establishes a platform for exploring the interplay of multiple phases in kagome systems.

To address this challenge, we have assessed the performance of a set of machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIP) capable of efficient large-scale simulations of COFs with quantum accuracy. ### [143] [Self-consistent evaluation of the Berry connection for Wannier functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21660)
*Martin Thümmler,Alexander Croy,Thomas Lettau,Ulf Peschel,Stefanie Gräfe*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于矩阵对数（matrix logarithm）的自洽插值方案，用于高精度地计算贝里联络（Berry connection），并讨论了基组不完备性对精度的影响。在单层MoS2和体相Si上的数值计算表明，该方法对瓦尼尔化（Wannierization）细节不敏感，且能显著提升速度矩阵与光导率的计算质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的贝里联络插值方案未显式处理重叠矩阵（overlap matrices）的矩阵结构，而是将矩阵元视为独立或仅区分对角与非对角元，导致精度受限。

Method: 提出一种基于矩阵对数的自洽插值方案，显式利用重叠矩阵的矩阵结构；并通过重叠矩阵的奇异值（singular values）量化基组不完备性，将其与瓦尼尔函数的展开泛函不变部分（$Ω_\mathrm{I}$）关联。

Result: 在单层MoS2和体相Si上的数值计算表明，该方法对瓦尼尔化细节的敏感性显著降低，速度矩阵和光导率（optical conductivity）的计算质量得到改善。

Conclusion: 基于矩阵对数的自洽插值方案能有效提升贝里联络的计算精度，且对瓦尼尔化过程的依赖性较弱，适用于光响应性质的高精度第一性原理计算。

Abstract: The Berry connection is a gauge-dependent quantity frequently used to describe the optical response of solids. Its evaluation requires a k-derivative with respect to the cell periodic-part of the Bloch-functions and is commonly calculated in the Wannier basis by using overlap matrices of cell-periodic parts of Bloch-functions at neighboring k-points. So far, all proposed interpolation schemes for the Berry connection do not account for the matrix structure of the overlap matrices explicitly but treat the matrix elements as independent, or only distinguish between diagonal and off-diagonal entries. In this work, we propose a self-consistent interpolation scheme based on the matrix logarithm resulting in a strongly improved accuracy. Furthermore, we discuss how the basis set incompleteness of the bands used in the ab-initio calculation imposes constraints on the accuracy. We quantify the basis incompleteness based on the singular values of the overlap matrices and relate it to the invariant part of the spread functional $Ω_\mathrm{I}$ of the Wannier functions. Numerical calculations for monolayer MoS2 and bulk Si demonstrate that the proposed interpolation scheme is much less sensitive to the Wannierization details and leads to an improved quality of the velocity matrix and the optical conductivity.

</details>

Abstract: Two-dimensional (2D) magnetic materials integrated with graphene offer a compelling platform for next-generation spintronic devices, yet nickel in its 2D form remains largely unexplored, due to fundamental synthesis limitations. ### [145] [Neural surrogates for crystal growth dynamics with variable supersaturation: explicit vs. implicit conditioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21753)
*Matteo Rigoni,Daniele Lanzoni,Francesco Montalenti,Roberto Bergamaschini*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用卷积递归神经网络（Convolutional Recurrent Neural Network）代理模型模拟晶体生长，基于Allen-Cahn动力学数值积分数据训练，比较了隐式与显式过饱和度参数处理两种架构的性能，发现显式参数条件化模型精度最优，且具有良好的可扩展性和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Allen-Cahn动力学（Allen-Cahn dynamics）数值积分生成含刻面（faceting）效应的时序数据集，训练卷积递归神经网络代理模型。开发两种架构：第一种通过处理少量演化帧的输入子序列隐式推断过饱和度（supersaturation）并延续演化；第二种将过饱和度作为显式输入，结合单帧初始状态预测完整序列。

Result: 显式参数条件化模型在点误差和平均绝对误差上表现最优，能够高保真地再现真实演化轮廓。隐式子序列方法仅在训练数据集更大时才能达到可比效果。两种模型均能准确再现过饱和度对生长速率和刻面形态的全局与局部影响，且可在256倍尺度域上完美缩放，在超过10倍序列长度上误差累积有限。

Conclusion: 显式参数条件化的卷积递归神经网络代理模型适用于晶体生长模拟，兼具高精度、可扩展性和泛化能力，为这类方法的广泛工程应用提供了潜力与局限性的分析基础。

Abstract: Simulations of crystal growth are performed by using Convolutional Recurrent Neural Network surrogate models, trained on a dataset of time sequences computed by numerical integration of Allen-Cahn dynamics including faceting via kinetic anisotropy. Two network architectures are developed to take into account the effects of a variable supersaturation value. The first infers it implicitly by processing an input mini-sequence of a few evolution frames and then returns a consistent continuation of the evolution. The second takes the supersaturation parameter as an explicit input along with a single initial frame and predicts the entire sequence. The two models are systematically tested to establish strengths and weaknesses, comparing the prediction performance for models trained on datasets of different size and, in the first architecture, different lengths of input mini-sequence. The analysis of point-wise and mean absolute errors shows how the explicit parameter conditioning guarantees the best results, reproducing with high-fidelity the ground-truth profiles. Comparable results are achievable by the mini-sequence approach only when using larger training datasets. The trained models show strong conditioning by the supersaturation parameter, consistently reproducing its overall impact on growth rates as well as its local effect on the faceted morphology. Moreover, they are perfectly scalable even on 256 times larger domains and can be successfully extended to more than 10 times longer sequences with limited error accumulation. The analysis highlights the potential and limits of these approaches in view of their general exploitation for crystal growth simulations.

### [146] [Amorphous Nanoconfinement Enables Self-sustaining Sabatier Reaction at Ambient Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21768)

Result: 该催化剂在环境条件下达到创纪录的CH4产率0.50 mol gcat⁻¹ h⁻¹，选择性100%，稳定运行超2000小时，催化剂床层温度低至100°C。原位测量表明CH4在低至54°C即可生成，并鉴定出*CO介导的CO2甲烷化路径（*CO-mediated pathway）。反应可由打火机或聚焦阳光轻松引发，甚至在电风扇强制对流下仍能维持，展现出强大的环境耐受性。

Conclusion: 该“点火即忘”（ignite-and-forget）系统消除了持续能量输入的需求，为分布式Power-to-Gas系统以及火星等资源受限环境下的自主燃料生产开辟了道路。

Abstract: The Sabatier reaction, the catalytic hydrogenation of CO2 into CH4, offers a cornerstone for carbon capture and utilization, and in-situ resource utilization during space exploration; however, it faces a fundamental thermodynamic-kinetic paradox: although highly exothermic, conventional catalysts still require continuous external heating to activate CO2 and maintain stable operation. Here we report an amorphous silica-embedded ruthenium catalyst that enables a long-term self-sustaining autothermal Sabatier reaction dispensing with external energy supply. Operating under ambient conditions, this system achieves a record-high CH4 yield of 0.50 mol gcat-1 h-1 with 100% selectivity, stable operation for over 2,000 hours, and a record-low catalyst bed temperature down to 100 oC. This exceptional self-sustaining behavior stems from the synergistic effect of the catalyst's ultralow effective thermal conductivity (0.27 W m-1 K-1), induced by amorphous nanoconfinement, and its superior intrinsic activity. This synergy generates localized hot spots at Ru sites while suppressing macroscopic heat loss. In situ measurements further reveal CH4 formation even at 54 oC and identify a *CO-mediated pathway for CO2 methanation. The reaction ignites readily with a lighter or focused sunlight and persists even under forced convection from an electric fan, demonstrating strong environmental tolerance. By removing the need for constant energy input, this "ignite-and-forget" system paves the way for decentralized Power-to-Gas systems and autonomous fuel production in resource-constrained environments like Mars.

### [147] [Nearly Complete Charge--Spin Conversion via Strain-Eliminated Fermi Pockets in a $d$-Wave Altermagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21779)
*Wancheng Zhang,Zhenhua Zhang,Rui Xiong,Zhihong Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，发现面内双轴拉伸应变能有效消除室温交变磁体KV₂Se₂O中残余的椭圆形费米口袋，恢复近乎正交的平费米面，从而将电荷-自旋转换效率（CSE）提升至约96%（4%应变），接近d波极限下的理论值100%。同时，倾斜电场下还发现了一种可实现近55% CSE的面外自旋电流，为无场垂直磁化翻转提供了可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 室温交变磁体（altermagnet）KV₂Se₂O在理想d波极限下可实现100%的电荷-自旋转换效率（charge-to-spin conversion efficiency, CSE），但实际样品中残留的椭圆形费米口袋会增强电荷电导率并抑制自旋电导率，导致CSE大幅下降。因此，需要寻找一种可行的方法来消除这些寄生口袋，恢复高性能自旋转换。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）研究面内等双轴拉伸应变（equibiaxial tensile strain）对KV₂Se₂O电子结构的影响；构建有效紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）拟合计算得到的能带结构，以捕获费米面（Fermi surface）的演化并分析CSE增强的微观机制。

Result: 面内双轴拉伸应变可系统性地消除残余的椭圆形费米口袋，恢复平带几何结构；CSE随应变单调增加，在4%应变时达到约96%的记录值。有效紧束缚模型表明，次近邻跃迁（next-nearest-neighbor hoppings）的减少是口袋被抑制并导致CSE增强的主导机制。倾斜电场下还发现了一种非常规面外自旋电流（out-of-plane spin current），在最优取向下的CSE接近55%。

Conclusion: 应变工程（strain engineering）是接近交变磁体中自旋转换极限的实用途径，为设计高效率自旋电子学器件（spintronic devices）提供了设计原则。

Abstract: The room-temperature altermagnet \mathrm{KV_2Se_2O} possesses nearly orthogonal flat Fermi surfaces, which in an idealized $d$-wave limit enable complete spin-channel separation and a theoretical charge-to-spin conversion efficiency (CSE) of 100%. Realistic samples, however, host residual elliptical Fermi pockets that enhance charge conductivity while suppressing spin conductivity, drastically reducing the CSE. Here we show that in-plane equibiaxial tensile strain systematically eliminates these parasitic pockets, restoring the flat-band geometry. Our first-principles calculations reveal that the CSE increases monotonically with strain, reaching a record value of approximately 96% at 4% strain. An effective tight-binding model fitted to the computed band structure accurately captures the evolution of the Fermi surface and confirms that the suppression of the pockets -- governed by reduced next-nearest-neighbor hoppings -- is the dominant mechanism for the strain-enhanced CSE. We further identify an unconventional out-of-plane spin current that emerges under tilted electric fields and achieves a CSE of nearly 55% at optimal orientations, offering a promising pathway for field-free perpendicular magnetization switching. Our work establishes strain engineering as a practical route to approach the ultimate conversion limit in altermagnets and provides a design principle for high-efficiency spintronic devices.

### [148] [Direct observation of surface bandgap shrinkage and negative electronic compressibility in SrTiO3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21783)
*Warakorn Jindata,Trung-Phuc Vo,Chutchawan Jaisuk,Sung-Kwan Mo,Thanh-Tien Nguyen,Ján Minár,Worawat Meevasana*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 与 KTaO3 不同，SrTiO3 表面带隙缩小约 390 meV，价带峰向低结合能方向移动达 200 meV，呈现负电子压缩性（NEC）光谱特征。DFT 计算表明表面形成已减小表观近带隙分离，额外电子积累进一步推动体系向金属态转变，氧空位模型也产生强带隙缩减。

Conclusion: SrTiO3 表面带隙工程与负电子压缩性（NEC）效应之间存在直接光谱联系，表明 SrTiO3 在下一代氧化物电子学、光电子学及高性能电容储能器件中具有应用潜力。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate and compare the electronic structures of SrTiO3 and KTaO3 under ultraviolet (UV) light induced electron doping. Using angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES), the evolution of the surface electronic structures of SrTiO3 and KTaO3 is systematically examined as a function of electron density. In contrast to KTaO3, SrTiO3 exhibits a pronounced shrinking of its surface bandgap by approximately 390 meV, accompanied by a counterintuitive shift of the valence band peak toward lower binding energies of up to 200 meV with increasing electron density. This anomalous behavior constitutes a spectroscopic signature of negative electronic compressibility (NEC). Density-functional-theory calculations provide qualitative support for the experimental observations. The calculations show that surface formation already reduces the apparent near-gap separation in SrTiO3, while additional electron accumulation further drives the slab toward a more metallic state; oxygen-vacancy models likewise produce strong bandgap reduction, identifying plausible mechanisms contributing to the observed surface bandgap shrinkage. These findings establish a direct spectroscopic link between bandgap engineering and the NEC effect at the SrTiO3 surface, highlighting the potential of SrTiO3 for next-generation oxide electronic, optoelectronic, and high-performance capacitive energy storage devices applications.

### [150] [Optical nonlinear anomalous Hall effect reveals the hidden spin order in antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21802)
*A. Schmid,D. Siebenkotten,D. Dai,J. Godinho,T. Ostatnický,N. Zou,Y. Zhang,J. Železný,Z. Šobáň,F. Křížek,V. Novák,S. Fairman,A. Hoehl,A. Hertwig,T. Janda,M. A. Huber,R. Huber,B. Kästner,J. Wunderlich*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文首次实验观测到光学非线性反常霍尔效应（optical nonlinear anomalous Hall effect），该效应源于PT对称反铁磁体中的光致电偶极跃迁，可产生时间反演奇宇称的光电流，其极性随Néel矢量180°翻转而改变。利用近场激发在CuMnAs中实现了亚100纳米分辨率反铁磁纹理成像，并直接读取了XMLD等方法无法区分的180°反铁磁态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）存储器件的核心障碍在于零净磁化导致传统磁读出的不可行。现有的X射线磁线二色性（XMLD）显微技术依赖于同步辐射光源，且由于XMLD在时间反演下为偶宇称（even under time reversal），无法区分180°翻转的反铁磁态。因此，需要寻找一种能够直接读出反铁磁180°态的新机制。

Method: 在具有联合宇称-时间反演（PT）对称性的反铁磁体CuMnAs中，利用近场激发（near-field excitation）技术，基于光致带间电偶极跃迁（light-induced interband electric-dipole transitions）以及自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）导致的±k态不对称性，产生时间反演奇宇称（time-reversal-odd）的光电流。在电流诱导的自旋-轨道力矩（spin-orbit-torque）切换后，以亚100纳米空间分辨率对该光电流进行成像。

Result: 成功实现了光学非线性反常霍尔效应的首次实验观测。信号极性（signal polarity）随局域Néel矢量翻转而改变，实现了反铁磁纹理（antiferromagnetic texture）的纳米级成像，并直接读出了XMLD及其他时间反演偶宇称线二色性探针无法区分的180°反铁磁态。

Conclusion: 光学非线性反常霍尔效应揭示了一种新的光-自旋相互作用，为隐藏自旋序（hidden spin order）的纳米级读出提供了一条可扩展的技术路径，并有望应用于超快全电和全光反铁磁自旋电子学（ultrafast all-electrical and all-optical antiferromagnetic spintronic technologies）技术。

Abstract: Reading antiferromagnetic order remains a central obstacle for antiferromagnetic memory and logic because zero net magnetisation precludes conventional magnetic readout. Domain imaging typically relies on x-ray magnetic linear dichroism (XMLD) microscopy at synchrotron sources, but XMLD is even under time reversal and cannot distinguish 180°-reversed magnetic states. Here we report the first experimental observation of the optical nonlinear anomalous Hall effect, predicted for antiferromagnets with combined parity - time-reversal ($PT$) symmetry. The effect stems from light-induced interband electric-dipole transitions, where spin-orbit coupling induces an asymmetry between $\pm k$ states and generates a time-reversal-odd photocurrent whose sign flips upon 180° reversal of the Néel vector. In $PT$-symmetric CuMnAs, we use near-field excitation to map this photocurrent with sub-100-nm spatial resolution after current-induced spin-orbit-torque switching. The signal polarity follows local Néel vector reversal, enabling nanoscale imaging of antiferromagnetic texture and direct readout of 180°-reversed antiferromagnetic states that remain indistinguishable in XMLD and other time-reversal-even linear-dichroic probes. The optical nonlinear anomalous Hall effect thus reveals a new light-spin interaction and provides a scalable route to nanoscale readout of hidden spin order, with potential for ultrafast all-electrical and all-optical antiferromagnetic spintronic technologies.

</details>


### [151] [Modeling High Entropy Alloys' Mechanical Property through Natural Language-Derived Descriptors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21807)
*Li-Cheng Hsiao,Zi-Kui Liu,Wesley Reinhart*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究验证了通过变压器嵌入（transformer embeddings）可以有效表达合金加工处理（processing treatment）信息，并利用这些嵌入作为描述符（descriptors）来提升高熵合金（high-entropy alloys）硬度预测的准确性，预测性能提升了20%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器学习辅助的合金设计中，加工处理信息对合金性能影响显著，但由于难以表达而常被忽略；本研究旨在探索能否利用自然语言处理（NLP）技术有效表达加工处理信息，从而改进合金性能预测。

Method: 通过合成退火加工处理文本（synthesized annealing processing treatment text），研究变压器嵌入的表达能力；并利用合金加工处理描述的向量表示（vector representations）作为描述符，对高熵合金的硬度进行建模预测。

Result: 变压器嵌入能够有效重建合金加工参数，R²值超过0.99；将加工处理描述的自然语言派生描述符用于硬度预测，相较于未使用该信息的模型，预测性能提升了20%。

Conclusion: 自然语言派生的加工处理描述符能够有效提升合金性能预测，表明将加工处理信息纳入机器学习辅助合金设计是可行且有价值的路径。

Abstract: Processing treatments of alloys, despite being influential to alloy properties, are often neglected in machine-learning aided alloy designs due to the difficulties in expressing this information. We investigated the expressiveness of transformer embeddings through synthesized annealing processing treatment text and verified that embeddings could be utilized to reconstruct the processing parameters of alloys effectively with an R2>0.99. We then utilized the vector representations of alloys' processing treatment descriptions as descriptors to model high-entropy alloys' hardness and achieved a 20% improvement in prediction, verifying that natural language-derived descriptors of processing treatment information could be utilized to improve prediction of alloy properties.

</details>


### [152] [Critical role of phase-dependent properties in modeling photothermal sintering of LiCoO2 cathodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21842)
*Yang Hu,Benoit Sklénard,Wouter Vels,Yaroslav E. Romanyuk,Vladyslav Turlo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一个多尺度、数据驱动的框架，为LiCoO2（LCO）正极的光热烧结过程提供分相与晶粒尺寸分辨的热物理与光学输入，揭示了非晶LCO更强的光吸收与更低的导热性，表明传统结晶相恒定性质模型会系统性地高估安全操作窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光热烧结（photothermal sintering）在固态薄膜电池的LiCoO2（LCO）正极制造中具有应用前景，但传统一维模型使用相位平均（phase-averaged）且温度无关的性质，导致对峰值温度和热损伤边界的预测出现偏差。

Method: 采用多尺度数据驱动框架：训练Allegro神经网络势（neural network potential）达到近第一性原理精度，结合Green-Kubo方法计算晶相与非晶相的热导率；构建薄界面模型（thin-interface model）以非晶LCO作为有效晶间相，再现晶粒尺寸依赖的热传输行为；并将波长分辨光学性质集成到一维多物理场模拟中。

Result: 非晶LCO具有低且弱密度依赖的热导率，使其成为有效的晶间相；非晶LCO比晶相LCO吸收光更强且达到更高的峰值温度；采用晶相、恒定性质模型的传统方法会系统性地高估安全操作窗口（safe operating windows）。

Conclusion: 利用相分辨的热物理与光学数据能够更准确地预测光热烧结过程中的温度场与热损伤范围，为工艺设计提供可靠依据；晶相恒定性质假设可能导致工艺参数选择过于乐观，存在热损伤风险。

Abstract: Photothermal (photonic) sintering crystallizes as-deposited amorphous LiCoO2 (LCO) cathodes for solid-state thin-film batteries using millisecond, surface-localized heating. However, process design often relies on 1D models with phase-averaged, temperature-independent properties, which can mispredict peak temperatures and thermal damage margins. Here we develop a multiscale, data-driven framework that provides phase- and grain size-resolved thermophysical inputs for stoichiometric LCO. We train an Allegro neural network potential with near-ab initio accuracy, enabling Green-Kubo calculations of thermal conductivity for crystalline and amorphous phases. The low, weakly density-dependent conductivity of amorphous LCO motivates its use as an effective intergranular phase in a thin-interface model that reproduces observed grain-size-dependent thermal transport. Combined with measured wavelength-resolved optical properties in 1D multiphysics simulations, we show amorphous LCO absorbs more strongly and reaches higher peak temperatures than crystalline LCO; thus crystalline, constant-property models systematically overestimate safe operating windows.

</details>


### [153] [OptiMat Alloys: A FAIR End-to-End Agent with Living Database for Computational Multi-Principal Alloy Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21850)
*Yang Hu,Vladyslav Turlo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出 OptiMat Alloys，一个基于大语言模型（large language model, LLM）的对话式智能体，用于多主元合金（multi-principal element alloy）探索。该系统通过活数据库、零编程门槛的网页界面以及内置的不确定性量化（uncertainty quantification），将 FAIR 原则从预计算存储库扩展到按需知识生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有材料科学数据库只能服务预计算条目，覆盖面永久不完整且无法按需适应新问题，难以满足多主元合金探索中对动态、可交互计算的需求。

Method: OptiMat Alloys 基于三大支柱构建：存储每次计算及其来源的活数据库（living database）、无需编程知识的低门槛网页界面，以及通过交叉势函数（cross-potential）和交叉构型（cross-configuration）验证实现的内置不确定性量化。系统将覆盖近全部元素周期表的基础机器学习原子间势函数（machine learning interatomic potentials）与自然语言交互（natural-language interaction）相结合。

Result: 该系统实现了由用户领域知识引导的定向按需计算，将 FAIR 原则从预计算存储库扩展到按需知识生成，使任何材料科学家都能无障碍地进行计算合金筛选（computational alloy screening）。

Conclusion: OptiMat Alloys 通过大语言模型驱动的对话式界面，成功降低了多主元合金计算探索的门槛，解决了传统数据库覆盖面有限和无法动态响应新问题的核心局限。

Abstract: The FAIR principles have transformed how computational data and workflows are shared in materials research, yet existing repositories can only serve pre-computed entries -- broad coverage is perpetually incomplete and cannot adapt to new questions on demand. To address these challenges, we present OptiMat Alloys, a large language model-powered conversational agent for multi-principal element alloy exploration built on three pillars: a living database that stores every calculation with provenance, low-barrier accessibility through a web interface requiring zero programming expertise, and built-in uncertainty quantification via cross-potential and cross-configuration validation (see demo here https://youtu.be/lQzuorkzPMc). Coupling foundational machine learning interatomic potentials covering near-all periodic table of elements with natural-language interaction, OptiMat Alloys enables targeted, on-demand computation guided by the user's domain knowledge-extending FAIR from pre-computed repositories to on-demand knowledge generation and making computational alloy screening accessible to any materials scientist.

</details>


### [154] [Extending Hamiltonian-Adaptive Resolution Simulation to Interfaces: An Updated LAMMPS Implementation and Application to Porous Solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21867)
*Hari Haran Sudhakar,Alessandra Serva,Rocio Semino*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文在LAMMPS 2023中实现了哈密顿自适应分辨率模拟（H-AdResS）方法的新版本，扩展了相互作用势的适用范围、简化了输入文件准备，并改进了补偿例程以支持密度波动系统。通过水的参考模拟进行基准测试，并将其应用于多孔金属有机框架（MOF）的气体吸附结构与输运性质建模，验证了该方法在保持全原子精度下提升模拟效率的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多自然现象涉及在不同特征长度和时间尺度上同时发生的过程，目标区域通常受其周围涨落的影响。建模这类系统需要有效组合不同模拟分辨率，而H-AdResS方法通过在同一模拟盒子中结合原子尺度（atomistic）与基于粒子的粗粒化（coarse graining）模型，能在与分子扩散兼容的尺度上模拟双分辨率系统。本文旨在扩展该方法的应用范围并提升其易用性与效率。

Method: 在LAMMPS 2023中重新实现了H-AdResS方法，新增支持更多样化的相互作用势（interaction potentials），通过专用lammps输入命令简化输入文件准备，并在补偿例程（compensation routines）中引入变更以支持密度波动（fluctuating density）系统。基准测试通过再现参考全原子模拟的水性质完成，应用示例为多孔金属有机框架及其气体吸附与输运建模。

Result: 新实现成功再现了水的参考全原子性质，并将方法应用于金属有机框架的气体吸附结构与输运特性建模。结果表明，在双分辨率方案（dual-resolution scheme）的原子区域中，结构性质和动力学性质与全原子系统保持一致，未受影响，同时模拟效率得到提升。

Conclusion: 本工作为使用H-AdResS方法模拟复杂界面铺平了道路，潜在应用涵盖能量存储、电催化（electrocatalysis）和膜技术等领域。

Abstract: Many natural phenomena involve processes that happen simultaneously at different characteristic length- and timescales. Typically, the region where the process of interest happens is affected by fluctuations in its surroundings. Modeling these systems requires an effective combination of simulation resolutions. The Hamiltonian-Adaptive Resolution Simulation (H-AdResS) method allows to model dual-resolution systems in length- and time-scales compatible with molecular diffusion, by combining atomistic and particle-based coarse graining models in the same simulation box. In this work, a new implementation of H-AdResS is provided in LAMMPS 2023. New features extend the usage to more diverse interaction potentials and simplify the preparation of input files via dedicated lammps input commands, while keeping the efficiency gain of the basis method. The implementation is benchmarked by reproducing water properties from a reference atomistic simulation. Importantly, the new implementation includes changes in compensation routines allowing to simulate systems with fluctuating density. As an example, the method in its new implementation is applied to modeling a porous metal-organic framework and its gas adsorption structure and transport properties. We demonstrate that structural and dynamic properties in the atomistic region of the dual-resolution scheme are unaffected and remain those of the fully atomistic system, while increasing simulation efficiency. This paves the way for using H-AdResS to simulate complex interfaces across applications in energy storage, electrocatalysis, and membrane technologies.

</details>

### [155] [Impact of Photoelectric Readout Noise on Magnetic Field Sensitivity of NV Centers in Diamond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20901)
*Ilia Chuprina,Genko Genov,Christoph Findler,Johannes Lang,Petr Siyushev,Fedor Jelezko*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文系统比较了基于金刚石氮-空位（NV）色心的光电读取出（photoelectrical readout）与光学读取出（optical readout）在磁场传感中的性能，通过高斯统计（Gaussian statistics）分析光电探测中的电子噪声，证明约翰逊-奈奎斯特噪声（Johnson-Nyquist noise）限制下的光电磁场灵敏度可比光学测量提高一个数量级，为片上磁力计（on-chip magnetometer）的开发奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于NV色心的磁场传感（magnetic field sensing）依赖光学读取出（optical readout），但受限于光子散粒噪声（photon shot noise）。新近发展的光电读取出（photoelectrical readout）有望突破这一限制，但其噪声特性及对读取出效率的影响尚未被系统研究，因此需要深入分析。

Method: 利用单个及多NV色心（NV center ensemble）的金刚石样品，分别采用光学读取出和光电读取出进行磁场传感实验；结合高斯统计（Gaussian statistics）分析光电探测中的电子噪声（electronic noise），并估算读取出效率（readout efficiency）。

Result: 定量分析表明，在约翰逊-奈奎斯特噪声（Johnson-Nyquist noise）限制下，光电读取出实现的磁场灵敏度可比光学测量提升一个数量级（an order of magnitude）。

Conclusion: 本研究是迈向基于金刚石光电探测的片上磁力计（on-chip magnetometer）开发的关键步骤，证明光电读取出在灵敏度上具有显著优势。

Abstract: Nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers in diamond are of great interest for nano- and macro-scale magnetic field sensing. Most sensing protocols rely on conventional optical readout, which is limited by photon shot noise. The recently developed photoelectrical (PE) readout of the NV center electron spin state promises to overcome these limitations. However, the noise of the PE readout and its influence on readout efficiency have not been thoroughly studied. In this work, we perform magnetic field sensing and estimate the sensitivity using optical and PE readout with a single and an ensemble of NV centers in diamond. We investigate the electronic noise associated with the photoelectric detection and estimate the readout efficiency, using Gaussian statistics. Our quantitative analysis shows that the Johnson-Nyquist noise-limited photoelectric magnetic field sensitivity could outperform optical measurements by an order of magnitude. This work is an essential step towards the development of on-chip magnetometers using photoelectrical detection in diamond.

</details>

*F. Beall,A. Rimal,O. Seidel,Y. Mei,A. D. McDonald,I. Parmaksiz,V. A. Chirayath,J. Asaadi,D. Braga,J. B. R. Battat*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在室温和液氮温度下对SKY130低阈值电压晶体管进行直流（DC）特性测量；基于测量数据，采用低温建模方法构建了SPICE兼容的等温BSIM4模型，针对选定尺寸的晶体管在77K下进行参数提取与拟合。

Result: 所构建的BSIM4模型在77K下与实验数据吻合，平均相对均方根误差（relative RMS）约为20%，且模型误差不依赖于漏极电压（drain voltage）。模型已通过GitHub公开获取。

Conclusion: 该工作为高能物理领域在77K低温下的开源CMOS电路设计提供了准确的器件模型，有助于推动低温电路设计的民主化（democratization），使研究人员能够更便捷地进行低温CMOS电路的仿真与设计。

Abstract: Cryogenic applications in high-energy physics (HEP) demand reliable, low-power CMOS electronics capable of operating at liquid nitrogen temperatures (77 K). The open-source SkyWater 130nm (SKY130) CMOS process has previously been shown to operate at temperatures as low as 4 K making it a promising candidate for HEP applications. In this work, we characterize and model SKY130 low-threshold voltage transistors at 77 K, which is a temperature commonly used in modeling applications for liquid argon detectors. DC characteristic measurements were performed at both room temperature and liquid nitrogen temperature. We created a cryogenic modeling approach to produce a SPICE-compatible, isothermal BSIM4-based model for select transistor sizes at 77 K. The resulting model agrees with data at 77 K with an average error on the order of 20% (relative RMS) and shows no dependence on drain voltage. Due to the open-source nature of SKY130, we have made our models publicly available on Github. We hope this work will continue the trend for democratizing circuit design at cryogenic temperatures in high-energy physics by enabling open access to accurate cryogenic CMOS device models at 77 K.

### [157] [Higher odd-order nonlinear Hall effect in magnetic topological insulator Mn(Bi1-xSbx)2Te4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21293)
*Xiubing Li,Zheng Dai,Shuai Zhang,Heng Zhang,Congcong Li,Boyuan Wei,Fengyi Guo,Chunfeng Li,Fucong Fei,Minhao Zhang,Xuefeng Wang,Huaiqiang Wang,Fengqi Song*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该实验在磁性拓扑绝缘体Mn(Bi1-xSbx)2Te4薄片中观测到了高阶（三阶、五阶、七阶）奇数阶非线性霍尔效应（higher odd-order nonlinear Hall effect），并发现其与贝里曲率多极矩（Berry curvature multipoles）相关，为高阶非线性输运研究开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前非线性霍尔效应的研究主要集中于二阶和三阶响应，而对更高阶（higher-order）非线性霍尔效应的实验研究十分匮乏。本文旨在填补这一空白，探索高阶奇数阶非线性霍尔效应是否存在及其物理机制。

Method: 以磁性拓扑绝缘体（magnetic topological insulator）Mn(Bi1-xSbx)2Te4薄片为实验体系，通过电输运测量方法，分别观测了第三阶、第五阶和第七阶奇数阶非线性霍尔效应（odd-order nonlinear Hall effect）的电压信号，并结合理论分析探讨其起源。

Result: 高阶奇数阶非线性霍尔电压表现出两重角依赖性（twofold angular dependence），且仅存在于奈尔温度（Néel temperature）以下；该效应在电荷中性点（charge neutral point）附近达到最大值，并随非线性霍尔效应阶数的升高呈指数衰减；在奇数和偶数层样品中均观测到幅度相当的高阶奇数阶非线性霍尔效应。

Conclusion: 高阶奇数阶非线性霍尔效应响应可能源于贝里曲率多极矩（Berry curvature multipoles）。该工作为研究高阶非线性输运现象（higher-order nonlinear transport phenomena）奠定了基础。

Abstract: The nonlinear Hall effect is a new member of the Hall effect family, which attracts intense research interests, and it is closely related to the quantum geometry of quantum materials. The previous studies primarily concentrate on the second-order and third-order nonlinear Hall effect. However, the experimental study of higher-order nonlinear Hall effect is scarce at present. In this work, we report the observations of the higher odd-order (third-, fifth-, seventh-order) nonlinear Hall effect in magnetic topological insulator Mn(Bi1-xSbx)2Te4 thin flakes. The higher odd-order nonlinear Hall voltage exhibits a twofold angular dependence and exists only below the Néel temperature. It reaches its maximum near the charge neutral point and decays exponentially as the order of the nonlinear Hall effect increases. Furthermore, such higher odd-order nonlinear Hall effect is observed in both odd- and even-layer samples with comparable magnitudes. Theoretical analysis indicates that the higher odd-order nonlinear Hall effect responses may arise from the Berry curvature multipoles. Our work paves the way for the study of the higher-order nonlinear transport phenomena.

</details>


### [158] [Collective Excitations and Stability of Nonequilibrium Polariton Supersolids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21353)
*A. Grudinina,J. Cao,A. Kavokin,N. Voronova,A. Nalitov*

Method: 通过解析理论分析集体激发谱，并结合数值模拟对半导体超表面中极化激元非平衡超固体的稳定性条件进行系统研究，重点考察激子库（excitonic reservoir）介导的吸引性相互作用的角色。

Result: 明确展示了由于连续相位对称性和平移对称性的自发破缺而产生的零能Nambu-Goldstone模；证实了吸引性极化激元相互作用对非平衡超固体相稳定性的关键作用；给出了负质量非平衡超固体中存在对角与非对角长程序的具体条件。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了非平衡超固体中对称性破缺与集体激发的内在关联，阐明了半导体超表面实验中稳定该相的核心物理机制——激子库介导的吸引性相互作用，并为负质量体系中长程序的存在性提供了定量判据。

Abstract: Formation of nonequilibrium counterparts of supersolids, simultaneously characterized with spontaneous superfluid and crystalline order, was recently reported in incoherently pumped polariton condensates. We investigate collective excitation spectra of this phase and explicitly demonstrate the emergence of gapless Nambu-Goldstone modes due to spontaneously broken continuous phase and translation symmetries. For the recent implementation of the polariton nonequilibrium supersolidity in semiconductor metasurfaces [D. Trypogeorgos et al., Nature 639, 337 (2025)], we demonstrate the key role of attractive polariton interactions, mediated by the excitonic reservoir, for stability of the supersolid phase. Performing a thorough numerical investigation, we identify the conditions for existence of the diagonal and off-diagonal long-range order in negative-mass nonequilibrium supersolids.

Method: 首先，基于有限元模拟（finite element simulation）研究FC气隙几何参数对磁增益的影响。其次，基于磁阻（magnetic reluctance）提出与仿真结果一致的解析公式。最后，推导传感器检测率（detectivity）的解析模型，据此提取最优传感器设计参数。

Result: 所提出的解析模型能够从设计空间中提取最优传感器结构；相比单个MTJ，优化后的传感器性能提升了三个数量级（three orders of magnitude）。

Conclusion: 通过系统性的设计优化，可在磁通集中器的高增益与磁隧道结阵列的低噪声效应之间实现最佳平衡，从而大幅提升微型磁传感器的整体性能。

Abstract: Miniaturized, ultra-sensitive and easily integrable magnetometers are needed for many applications, like space exploration or health monitoring. Achieving this goal requires a magnetic sensor with high sensitivity and low noise. High sensitivity (>1000 %/mT) can be obtained by integrating high gain permalloy flux concentrators (FC). And reducing the magnetic 1/f noise can be realized by increasing the number of magnetic tunnel junctions (MTJs) in the air-gap of the FC. However, this is obtained at the expense of a wider air-gap and consequently a decrease of the magnetic gain and thus of the sensitivity. In this paper, we explore a design optimization scheme in order to find the best trade-off between high FC gain and low magnetic noise. To model the gain of the flux concentrator, we propose two complementary approaches; one is based on finite elements simulations of the FC gain where the influence of geometrical parameters of the air-gap is investigated. Then, in a second step, we propose an analytical formula consistent with all our simulations results and based on magnetic reluctance. Finally, we derive an analytical model of the sensor detectivity from which we can extract the optimal sensor design which allows an improvement by three orders of magnitude of the performances compared to a single junction.
