Method: 本文为综述类研究，系统总结了vdW异质结中手性自旋织构形成的基本机制，涵盖交换相互作用（exchange interactions）、磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy）、Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction, DMI）及偶极效应（dipolar effects）的作用。

Abstract: Chiral spin textures such as skyrmions have attracted considerable attention due to their nontrivial topology, chirality, stability at the nanoscale, and potential for low-power spintronic devices. The recent discovery of intrinsic magnetism in van der Waals (vdW) materials and the ability to engineer their heterostructures has opened a new platform to study and manipulate such textures. In these layered systems, atomically sharp interfaces, strong spin-orbit coupling, and tunable symmetry breaking provide unique opportunities to stabilize and control chiral magnetic states. This review summarizes the fundamental mechanisms underlying the formation of chiral spin textures in vdW heterostructures, including the roles of exchange interactions, magnetic anisotropy, Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction, and dipolar effects. We highlight key experimental advances in the observation and manipulation of chiral textures, discuss their dynamical properties and transport signatures, while overviewing selected theoretical investigations. Finally, we outline current challenges and future directions toward realizing robust, room-temperature chiral spin textures for practical spintronic technologies.

### [161] [Magnetic-flux tunable electronic transport through domain walls in a three-dimensional second-order topological insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21562)
*Zhe Hou,Ai-Min Guo*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了三维拓扑绝缘体纳米线中磁畴壁对拓扑铰链态电子输运的影响，发现通过外加平行磁场可产生完美的正弦阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆振荡，并进一步在双磁畴壁结构中观测到法布里-珀罗振荡，为利用磁通精细调控拓扑铰链态的量子输运提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维拓扑绝缘体（3D topological insulator）在引入对角塞曼项后可转变为二阶拓扑绝缘体，存在手性一维拓扑铰链态（topological hinge states, THSs）。然而，THSs在磁畴壁（magnetic domain wall）中的电子输运行为尚不清楚，亟需探索其输运特性及调控机制。

Method: 采用现象学散射矩阵方法（scattering matrix approach），研究THSs通过三维TI纳米线中磁畴壁的电子输运；通过外加与纳米线平行的均匀磁场，分析两端电导G对磁通Φ的依赖关系。

Result: 发现两端电导G呈现完美的正弦阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆（Aharonov-Bohm）振荡，公式为G = (e²/2h)[1 − cos(πΦ/Φ₀)]，其中Φ₀ = h/2e为磁通量子；在双磁畴壁（double-DW）结构中观察到法布里-珀罗（Fabry-Pérot）振荡，且电导极小值可由磁通调控。

Conclusion: 将Aharonov-Bohm振荡归因于THSs穿过磁畴壁时发生的π自旋旋转导致的相长/相消干涉；结果为利用磁通精细控制磁性系统中THSs的量子输运开辟了新方向，并为实验探测THSs提供了可靠方法。

Abstract: The three-dimensional (3D) topological insulators (TIs), hosting topologically protected helical surface states, can be promoted into second-order TIs when a diagonal Zeeman term, typical of magnetic doping, is introduced. The latter hosts exotic chiral one-dimensional (1D) topological hinge states (THSs). In this paper, we investigate the electronic transport of THSs through a magnetic domain wall (DW) in a 3D TI nanowire. Due to the sign reversal of the out-of-plane magnetization across the DW, four 1D topological boundary states, residing on the edge of the DW, arise and form an enclosed loop mediating the counterpropagating THSs. By applying a uniform magnetic field parallel to the nanowire, we obtain a perfect sinusoidal Aharonov-Bohm oscillation in the two-terminal conductance $G$, formulated by $G=\frac{e^2}{2h} \left[ 1- \cos(πΦ/Φ_0) \right]$, with $Φ$ the magnetic flux through the DW and $Φ_0 = h/2e$ the flux quantum. Applying a phenomenological scattering matrix approach, we explain this novel Aharonov-Bohm oscillation perfectly, and attribute the constructive (destructive) interference of transmission at $Φ= Φ_0$ (0) to the $π$-spin rotation of the THSs traveling through the DW. Extending our study to a double-DW junction, where the central region has antiparallel magnetization to the leads, we observe Fabry-P{é}rot oscillations, in which the conductance minima are tuned by the magnetic flux. Our findings open a new avenue for finely controlling the quantum transport of THSs in magnetic systems using magnetic flux, and provide a faithful way for detecting THSs in experiments.

### [162] [Stable Wave-Function Zeros Indicate Exciton Topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21643)
*Yoonseok Hwang,Henry Davenport,Frank Schindler*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文揭示了激子（exciton）波函数中的稳定零点由晶体对称性强制产生，这些零点约束了激子能带拓扑与相对能带拓扑（价带与导带拓扑不变量之差），无需依赖能带结构或相互作用的细节。结论基于一维和二维具有反转或旋转对称性的两带系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激子是电子-空穴束缚态，其能带拓扑（band topology）源于电子能带拓扑与电子-空穴相互作用结构的共同影响。本文旨在探索晶体对称性如何在不需详细能带或相互作用信息的情况下，约束激子波函数的结构及相关的拓扑不变量。

Method: 通过分析晶体对称性对激子包络波函数（envelope wave function）的约束，推导稳定零点（stable zeros）在高对称动量（包括光学可及的总动量 p=0）的存在条件。利用这些零点模式约束激子能带拓扑与相对能带拓扑，具体针对一维和二维具有反转（inversion）或旋转（rotation）对称性的两带激子系统。

Result: 晶体对称性能在激子波函数中强制产生稳定零点。这些零点约束了相对激子能带拓扑（激子与非相互作用拓扑不变量之差）和相对能带拓扑（价带与导带拓扑不变量之差）。在一维中相关拓扑不变量为贝里相位（Berry phase），在二维中为陈数（Chern number）模旋转阶数。二维中激子陈数本身也受零点模式约束。

Conclusion: 激子波函数的稳定零点提供了连接晶体对称性、激子波函数结构与拓扑不变量的普适框架，无需依赖能带或相互作用的详细知识。该结果拓展了对激子拓扑性质的理解，并为预测材料中激子的拓扑行为提供了对称性驱动的方法。

Abstract: Excitons are bound states of electrons and holes whose band topology arises from an interplay between the topology of the underlying electronic bands and the structure of the electron-hole interaction. In crystalline solids, symmetry representations and topological invariants of the conduction and valence bands constrain the structure of the exciton envelope wave function. In particular, we show that crystalline symmetry can enforce stable zeros in the exciton wave function. These occur at high-symmetry momenta, including the optically accessible total momentum p=0. We work out how the stable zeros constrain both the relative exciton-band topology (the difference of exciton and non-interacting topological invariants) and the relative band topology (the difference of valence and conduction band invariants), all without requiring detailed knowledge of the band structure or interactions. We establish these results for two-band excitons in inversion- and rotation-symmetric systems in one and two dimensions, where the relevant topological invariants are the Berry phase in one dimension and the Chern number (modulo the rotation order) in two dimensions. In two dimensions, the exciton Chern number itself can also be constrained by zero patterns.

### [163] [Disorder-induced crossover from phase-averaging to mode-mixing regimes in magnetic domain walls of a second-order topological insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21702)
*Dong Zhou,Zhe Hou*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究三维二阶拓扑绝缘体中磁畴壁（DW）在安德森无序下的电子输运。干净极限下，畴壁支持两个共传播的一维拓扑边缘态，构成有效阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆（AB）干涉仪，产生正弦电导振荡；引入无序后，AB振荡被抑制，系综平均电导出现半量子化平台0.5 e²/h，且电导涨落呈现独特的双台阶结构。通过建立随机相位干涉和模式混合的理论框架，分别识别出相位平均区（PAR）和模式混合区（MMR），并进一步计算了Fano因子对应的双台阶结构。工作揭示了无序诱导的PAR到MMR的交叉，并强调了二阶电导累积量在识别这些输运区域中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索三维二阶拓扑绝缘体中磁畴壁在无序影响下的电子输运行为，理解无序如何调控拓扑边缘态之间的量子干涉和模式混合。

Method: 通过理论分析建立随机相位干涉和模式混合两个框架，分别对应电导涨落的两个台阶；计算系综平均电导、电导涨落、Fano因子等输运量，并分析电导的统计分布（beta分布和均匀分布）。

Result: 干净极限下出现AB振荡的正弦电导；无序下系综平均电导呈现0.5 e²/h的半量子化平台；电导涨落依次在中等无序和强无序下形成约0.35 e²/h和约0.29 e²/h的两个台阶；Fano因子对应出现1/4和1/3的双台阶；PAR中电导服从U形beta分布，MMR中演化为均匀分布。

Conclusion: 无序可诱导从相位平均区到模式混合区的交叉，二阶电导累积量是识别这些输运区域的关键指标；无序工程有望成为调控基于畴壁器件的电子输运的有效手段。

Abstract: We investigate electronic transport across a magnetic domain wall (DW) in a three-dimensional (3D) second-order topological insulator subject to Anderson disorder. In the clean limit, the DW hosts two co-propagating one-dimensional (1D) topological edge states that act as the two arms of an effective Aharonov-Bohm (AB) interferometer, inducing a sinusoidal conductance oscillation. Upon the introduction of disorder, the AB oscillations are suppressed, while a half-quantized plateau of $0.5 e^2/h$ for the ensemble-averaged conductance emerges. Notably, within this plateau, the conductance fluctuation exhibits a distinctive two-step plateau structure, with values of $\sim 0.35 e^2/h$ at moderate disorder, followed by a second plateau at $\sim0.29 e^2/h$ under strong disorder. By developing theoretical frameworks that account for the random-phase interference and inter-mode mixing of the two arms, we identify the first fluctuation plateau as a signature of the phase-averaging regime (PAR) and the second as a signature of the mode-mixing regime (MMR). Furthermore, we show that, in the PAR the conductance follows a U-shaped beta distribution, while it evolves into a uniform distribution in the MMR. The Fano factor associated with shot noise is also computed, which exhibits a similar two-step plateau structure at $1/4$ and $1/3$, corresponding to the PAR and MMR, respectively. Our work provides a clear demonstration of the disorder-induced crossover from PAR to MMR, and highlights the crucial role of second-order conductance cumulants in identifying these transport regimes. The results suggest disorder-engineering as a powerful route for controlling electronic transport across DW-based devices.

### [164] [Tailoring Germanium Heterostructures for Quantum Devices with Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21732)
*Patrick Del Vecchio,Kevin Rossi,Giordano Scappucci,Stefano Bosco*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出在无应变的锗沟道中引入局域化的应变硅尖峰（strained silicon spike）来修饰异质结构；利用多目标贝叶斯优化（multi-objective Bayesian optimization）优化硅尖峰的剖面（profile），在最大化SOI的同时，确保与现有外延生长工艺的兼容性，并具备对实际生长参数波动的鲁棒性。

Result: 该异质结构设计将SOI提升了多达三个数量级；量子点自旋量子比特（quantum-dot spin qubit）的品质因子（quality factor）相比最先进材料提升了两个数量级；对于超导安德烈夫自旋量子比特（Andreev spin qubit），预测可实现GHz尺度的自旋分裂。

Conclusion: 本工作表明，通过工程化硅浓度剖面（Si concentration profiles）的新型锗异质结构，有望为可扩展的量子计算和自旋电子学（spintronics）应用开辟新路径。

Abstract: Germanium (Ge) quantum wells are emerging as versatile platforms for quantum devices, supporting high-quality spin qubits and integration with superconducting leads. These applications benefit from strong intrinsic spin-orbit interaction (SOI), enabling efficient electrical control and engineering of spin degrees of freedom. The most advanced Ge/SiGe heterostructures to date, based on compressively strained Ge channels within strain-relaxed silicon-germanium (SiGe) barriers, exhibit weak SOI due to the heavy-hole character of the wave function, posing challenges for spin-based quantum devices and requiring complex device designs for fast qubit manipulation. In this work, we demonstrate that concrete heterostructure modifications can overcome these limitations, enhancing SOI by up to three orders of magnitude. Specifically, we propose to enrich unstrained Ge channels by localized, strained silicon spikes. Leveraging a multi-objective Bayesian optimization, we optimize the spike profile to maximize SOI, while ensuring compatibility with current epitaxial growth processes and robustness against realistic variations of growth parameters. Our heterostructure substantially enhances device performance, yielding up to two orders of magnitude higher quantum-dot spin qubit quality factors than state-of-the-art materials. We also predict GHz-scale spin splittings for hybrid superconducting Andreev spin qubits. These novel Ge heterostructures with engineered Si concentration profiles can open pathways to scalable quantum and spintronic applications.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将二维铋（bismuth）与磁性层界面结合是实现高阶拓扑相（higher-order topological phases）的重要途径，先前理论（Chen et al., 2020）提出铁磁绝缘体衬底上的铋烯可作为磁二阶拓扑绝缘体（magnetic second-order topological insulators）的通用平台，但缺乏实验验证。

Method: 在铁磁绝缘体EuO(111)上制备外延铋薄膜，利用高分辨扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）观察原子结构，结合扫描隧道谱（scanning tunneling spectroscopy, STS）测量局域态密度，并进行低温磁输运（magnetotransport）实验。

Result: 获得原子有序的双层铋薄膜，呈(012)取向准方晶格（quasi-square lattice），对应稳定的α相铋烯；薄膜异常平坦，体现其二维本性；STS显示约400 meV的稳健能隙，符合量子自旋霍尔绝缘体（quantum spin Hall insulator）相且室温保持；空间分辨STS识别出岛屿边界增强的边缘局域态（edge-localised states）；磁输运测量呈现线性磁电阻（linear magnetoresistance）和霍尔符号反转（Hall sign reversal），表明量子限域驱动的表面主导输运。

Conclusion: 铋烯-磁绝缘体异质结构是实现磁可调拓扑相（magnetically tunable topological phases）的可行实验平台，为在二维体系中观测高阶拓扑提供了关键实验进展。

Abstract: Interfacing two-dimensional bismuth with a magnetic layer provides a promising route towards realizing higher-order topological phases. In particular, bismuthene on a ferromagnetic insulator substrate has been theoretically proposed by \citet{Chen2020} as a universal platform for magnetic second-order topological insulators. Here, we report the experimental realization of epitaxial bismuth films grown on the ferromagnetic insulator EuO(111). Using high-resolution scanning tunneling microscopy, we observe atomically ordered bi-layer bismuth with a (012)-oriented quasi-square lattice, corresponding to a stabilized $α$-phase bismuthene. The resulting film is exceptionally flat compared to conventional metallic films, reflecting the intrinsic two-dimensional nature of the Bi(012) phase. Tunneling spectroscopy(STS) reveals a robust energy gap of about 400 meV in the local density of states, consistent with a quantum spin Hall insulating phase persisting up to room temperature. Spatially resolved STS further identifies enhanced edge-localised states at the island boundaries. Complementary low-temperature magnetotransport measurements on proximity-coupled ultrathin Bi films exhibit linear magnetoresistance and a Hall sign reversal, indicative of quantum-confinement-driven surface-dominated transport. Our results establish bismuthene-magnetic-insulator heterostructures as a viable experimental platform for realizing magnetically tunable topological phases, providing a critical step toward the observation of higher-order topology in two dimensions.

</details>


### [166] [Cryogenic shock exfoliation for ultrahigh mobility rhombohedral graphite nanoelectronics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21912)
*Ludwig Holleis,Youngjoon Choi,Canxun Zhang,Jack H. Farrell,Gabriel Bargas,Audrey Hsu,Zexing Chen,Ian Sackin,Wenjie Zhou,Yi Guo,Thibault Charpentier,Yifan Jiang,Benjamin A. Foutty,Aidan Keough,Martin E. Huber,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Andrew Lucas,Andrea F. Young*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出“低温冲击剥离法”（cryogenic shock exfoliation）制备大面积菱面体多层石墨烯（RMG）薄片，结合低压范德华组装技术，实现了面积超过1300 μm²、制备产率达90%的高度均匀器件。通过扫描纳米SQUID-on-tip成像和横向磁聚焦测量，验证了器件在低温下具有均匀的自旋磁性和超过200 μm的无序平均自由程，并在中间温度区间观测到从泊肃叶流到多孔电子流的尺寸驱动转变，表明器件质量极高，克服了菱面体石墨烯器件制备的关键材料瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 菱面体多层石墨烯（RMG）因其可调谐的关联电子物理特性（如磁性、超导和拓扑相）而备受关注，但天然石墨中菱面体堆垛的丰度极低，严重限制了样品产额和可用面积，成为该领域发展的关键材料瓶颈。

Method: 提出“低温冲击剥离法”（cryogenic shock exfoliation）以制备大面积菱面体石墨烯薄片，并结合低压范德华（van der Waals）组装技术以保持堆垛顺序。采用扫描纳米SQUID-on-tip成像和横向磁聚焦（transverse magnetic focusing）技术对器件质量进行表征。

Result: 成功制备面积超过1300 μm²、产率达90%的高度均匀RMG器件；扫描纳米SQUID-on-tip成像显示器件中心10×10 μm²区域内自旋磁性均匀；横向磁聚焦测得低温无序平均自由程（mean free path）超过200 μm；在强电子-电子流体动力学（electron hydrodynamics）的中间温度区间，观测到从泊肃叶流（Poiseuille flow）到多孔电子流（porous electron flow）的尺寸驱动转变。

Conclusion: 该方法克服了菱面体石墨烯介观器件制备的关键材料瓶颈，为将强关联电子相（strongly correlated phases）集成到二维纳米电子学（two-dimensional nanoelectronics）中铺平了道路。

Abstract: Rhombohedral multilayer graphene (RMG) offers a highly tunable platform for correlated electron physics, featuring field-effect control of magnetic, superconducting, and topological phases[1-24]. The promise of these materials has been held back by the limited abundance of rhombohedral stacking in natural graphite, which constrains both sample yield and useful area. Here we introduce 'cryogenic shock exfoliation' to produce large area rhombohedral graphene flakes which, combined with a low-pressure van der Waals assembly technique that preserves stacking order, enable highly uniform devices exceeding 1300 $μm^2$ with fabrication yields of 90%. Using scanning nanoSQUID-on-tip imaging, we demonstrate uniform spin magnetism over the full central 10 times 10 $μm^2$ area of our devices. Transverse magnetic focusing reveals a disorder mean free path exceeding 200 $μm$ at low temperatures. Within the flat surface bands of RMG[20], we observe a size-driven crossover from Poiseuille to porous electron flow in the intermediate-temperature regime of strong electron-electron hydrodynamics[16, 25], providing a further signature of ultrahigh device quality. Our approach overcomes a key materials bottleneck in the fabrication of mesoscopic rhombohedral graphene devices, paving the way for incorporating strongly correlated phases into two-dimensional nanoelectronics.

</details>

### [167] [Shaping nematic order in bacterial films with single-cell resolution patterning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21655)
*Matthias Le Bec,Guillem Pérez Martín,Cameron Boggon,Yiyao Hu,Leonardo Puggioni,Rosa Heydenreich,Alexander Mathys,Luca Giomi,Eleonora Secchi,Lucio Isa*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用毛细管组装技术以单细胞精度控制枯草芽孢杆菌（Bacillus subtilis）内孢子的位置和取向，研究了初始条件对细菌活性向列相流体（active nematic fluid）自组织动力学的影响，发现平行取向播种可实现毫米级向列有序及同步屈曲（buckling），并通过结构色与光偏振实现了宏观细菌薄膜的光学各向异性控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细菌菌落形成的活性向列相流体表现出自组织有序和混沌流动等动力学行为，但初始条件对其组织的影响因缺乏精准图案化方法而尚未被充分探索。

Method: 采用毛细管组装（capillary assembly）技术，在单细胞分辨率下精确控制枯草芽孢杆菌内孢子的位置和取向；通过萌发和细胞链生长，定量分析细菌薄膜的动力学与形态；结合数值模拟和基于单个细丝力学性质的模型描述屈曲动力学。

Result: 正交取向播种的内孢子导致混沌动力学，而平行取向播种则产生毫米级高度向列有序的薄膜，并在进一步生长后发生同步屈曲。通过编程局部细胞取向，利用向列排列实现了具有局部光学各向异性的宏观细菌薄膜。

Conclusion: 初始条件在细菌活性向列流体的时空组织中起关键作用，为控制细菌组装以回答开放性生物学问题和实现具有定制特性的活体材料提供了新机遇。

Abstract: Bacterial colonies composed of elongated cells form active nematic fluids that spontaneously self-organise into ordered domains of aligned cells and exhibit self-generated chaotic flows powered by cell growth. While their dynamics have attracted significant attention, the role of initial conditions remains largely unexplored due to a lack of precise patterning methods. Here, we harness the precision of capillary assembly to pattern Bacillus subtilis endospores into arrays with controlled positions and orientations at single-cell resolution. Upon germination and growth of cell chains, we quantify the dynamics and morphologies of the resulting bacterial films. While orthogonally seeded spores lead to chaotic dynamics, seeding them with parallel orientations yields films with high nematic order across millimetres, which subsequently synchronously buckle upon further growth. Our observations are captured by numerical simulations and a model that describes the buckling dynamics starting from the mechanical properties of individual filaments. By programming local cell orientation with single-cell precision, we finally harness nematic alignment to create macroscopic bacterial films with local optical anisotropy, via structural colouration and light polarisation. Our findings demonstrate that initial conditions play a key role and offer exciting opportunities to control the spatio-temporal organization of bacterial assemblies towards addressing open biological questions and realizing living materials with tailored properties.

</details>

### [168] [Enhanced Reconstruction of Sub-GeV Neutrinos Charged Current Interactions in LArTPC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20957)
*Stone Chou,Sanskar Jain,Wei Shi,Ciro Riccio*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了液氩时间投影室（LArTPC）中亚GeV中微子带电电流相互作用的能量重建与粒子鉴别方法，发现闪烁光信号具有自补偿效应，联合电荷与光信号可实现70%的电子中微子与反中微子分离效率，并利用近邻算法结合轻子排锥几何方法提升反中微子方向重建约20度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于电荷的能损量热法（charge-based calorimetry）在亚GeV（sub-GeV）能区受到显著的复合涨落（recombination fluctuations）和强子能量缺失的限制，亟需探索更优的能量重建与粒子鉴别方案以提升未来液氩时间投影室（Liquid Argon Time Projection Chamber, LArTPC）大气中微子分析的物理潜力。

Method: 利用闪烁光信号（scintillation light）能量沉积进行重建，利用了此前报道的自补偿光效应（self-compensating light effect）；联合电荷与光两种探测器信号进行信息融合；采用基于近邻的算法（proximity-based algorithm）与几何轻子排锥（geometric lepton-exclusion cone）方法实现中子诱导能量沉积的分离。

Result: 光信号单独重建在400 MeV以上优于可分离电磁（EM）与强子（hadronic）对象的电荷方法，300 MeV以下两者性能相当；联合两种信号实现70%的电子中微子（electron neutrinos）与反中微子（antineutrinos）分离效率；中子能量沉积分离使反中微子的方向重建改善约20度。

Conclusion: 该研究为未来LArTPC大气中微子分析提供了增强物理潜力（physics reach）的新思路，证明了联合光-电信号在亚GeV能区中微子重建中的优势以及中子标记在方向重建中的关键作用。

Abstract: This paper presents a comprehensive study of the reconstruction of sub-GeV neutrino charged-current interactions within a Liquid Argon Time Projection Chamber (LArTPC). We demonstrate that traditional charge-based calorimetry is fundamentally limited at sub-GeV scales by significant recombination fluctuations and missing hadronic energy. We show that energy reconstruction using energy deposited as scintillation light (L) partially benefits from the previously reported self-compensating light effect. At neutrino energies above 400 MeV, the light-only reconstruction still outperforms charge-only methods that can separate EM and hadronic objects. The performance of the two remains comparable below 300 MeV. Using the energy-deposit information from both detector signals, we demonstrate a 70% efficiency in separating electron neutrinos and antineutrinos. By using a proximity-based algorithm coupled with a geometric lepton-exclusion cone, we also demonstrate the ability to isolate neutron-induced energy depositions from background. This enables an improvement of sub-GeV direction reconstruction by about 20 degrees for antineutrinos. This study provides new insights into how to enhance the physics reach of future LArTPC atmospheric neutrino analyses.

</details>


### [169] [Search for dark matter produced in association with a dark Higgs boson decaying into a bottom quark-antiquark pair in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20999)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 利用CMS探测器在质心能量13 TeV的质子-质子对撞数据（积分亮度138 fb⁻¹），搜寻伴随暗希格斯玻色子衰变为正反底夸克对产生的暗物质信号，给出了目前最严格的95%置信水平上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗物质（dark matter）的存在已获广泛间接证据，但其粒子性质尚不明确。理论模型预言暗区存在类希格斯玻色子（dark Higgs boson），通过与自旋1规范玻色子（spin-1 gauge boson mediator）的耦合产生暗物质信号。该研究旨在直接搜索这一特定产生通道，以检验暗物质的理论模型。

Method: 使用欧洲核子研究中心（CERN）大型强子对撞机（LHC）上CMS探测器在2016–2018年收集的质子-质子对撞数据，质心能量（center-of-mass energy）13 TeV，积分亮度（integrated luminosity）138 fb⁻¹。搜索基于暗物质产生导致的大缺失横向动量（large missing transverse momentum）以及暗希格斯玻色子衰变为正反底夸克对（bottom quark-antiquark pair）在不变质量谱上的共振结构（resonant structure）。

Result: 对暗希格斯玻色子质量假设低于160 GeV的区域，给出了95%置信水平（confidence level）的信号强度上限。暗希格斯玻色子质量为50 (150) GeV时，中介子质量（mediator mass）分别排除至4.5 (2.5) TeV。这是针对所研究暗希格斯玻色子质量范围目前最严格的限制（most stringent limits）。

Conclusion: 该搜索未发现明显超出标准模型背景的暗物质信号，在95%置信水平上对暗希格斯玻色子质量低于160 GeV及相应中介子质量区域给出了迄今最强的排除上限。

Abstract: A search for dark matter produced in association with a dark Higgs boson decaying into a bottom quark-antiquark pair has been performed using proton-proton collision data at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV. The search uses data collected with the CMS detector at the CERN LHC during the 2016$-$2018 data-taking period, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. The results are interpreted in terms of a theoretical model of dark matter production that, together with a spin-1 gauge boson mediator, predicts the existence of a Higgs-boson-like particle in the dark sector (i.e., a dark Higgs boson). This search focuses on an experimental signature with large missing transverse momentum from dark matter production and a resonant structure in the invariant mass of the bottom quark-antiquark pair from the dark Higgs boson decay. Upper limits at 95% confidence level on the signal strength for dark Higgs boson mass hypotheses below 160 GeV are set. Values of the mediator mass up to 4.5 (2.5) TeV are excluded at 95% confidence level for a dark Higgs boson mass of 50 (150) GeV. This represents the most stringent limits set to date for the dark Higgs boson masses considered in this study.

</details>

*P. Albicocco,M. Anelli,F. Archilli,M. Atzeni,W. Baldini,A. Balla,S. Belin,N. Bondar,D. Brundu,S. Cadeddu,S. Calì,A. Cardini,M. Carletti,A. Casais Vidal,V. Chulikov,A. Chubykin,P. Ciambrone,L. Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: LHCb实验在LHC Run 3期间将瞬时亮度提高至原来的5倍，并对缪子探测器（muon detector）进行了硬件升级和软件触发（software trigger）算法改进。2024年校准数据表明，升级后的系统实现了超过90%的缪子识别效率（muon identification efficiency），同时强子误识别概率（hadron misidentification probability）低于1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LHC Run 3期间，LHCb对撞点的瞬时亮度（instantaneous luminosity）从$4\times 10^{32}\rm{cm}^{-2}\rm{s}^{-1}$提升至$2\times 10^{33}\rm{cm}^{-2}\rm{s}^{-1}$，增加了五倍。为应对更高粒子率（particle rate）下的运行挑战，需要对缪子探测器进行升级改造，以保持Run 2时期的缪子识别性能。

Method: 对缪子探测器进行了多项硬件干预（hardware interventions），包括读出电子学（readout electronics）的全面改造；同时对软件触发中的缪子识别算法（muon identification algorithms）进行了改进。基于2024年收集的数据校准样本（data calibration samples）评估探测器性能。

Result: 在2024年校准数据上，缪子探测效率（muon detection efficiency）和缪子识别性能（muon identification performance）得到评估。实现了超过90%的缪子识别效率，同时强子误识别概率低于1%。

Conclusion: 升级后的缪子探测器及其软件触发算法成功在高亮度LHCb Run 3环境中运行，并在保证极低的强子误识别概率的前提下维持了高缪子识别效率。

Abstract: In Run 3 of the LHC, the instantaneous luminosity at the LHCb interaction point has been increased by a factor of five, from $4\times 10^{32}\rm{cm}^{-2}\rm{s}^{-1}$ to $2\times 10^{33}\rm{cm}^{-2}\rm{s}^{-1}$. Several hardware interventions, including a complete overhaul of the readout electronics, have been carried out on the muon detector. The muon identification algorithms in the software trigger were improved with the aim of ensuring Run 2 performance under a higher particle rate. The operation and calibration of the upgraded muon detector are presented. The muon detection efficiency and muon identification performance are evaluated on data calibration samples collected during the year 2024. A muon identification efficiency above 90\% with sub-percent hadron misidentification probability is achieved by exploiting the pattern of hits in the muon detector.

</details>

Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用LHCb实验在13 TeV质子-质子对撞中采集的5.4 fb⁻¹数据，通过对B⁰ → D⁺ D⁻ K⁺ π⁻衰变全过程进行振幅分析，发现了一个新激发态粲奇介子D_{s1}(2933)⁺，其统计显著性超过10个标准差，质量与宽度分别为m₀ = 2933^{+6}_{-5}(stat)^{+4}_{-3}(syst) MeV和Γ₀ = 72^{+18}_{-12}(stat)^{+7}_{-10}(syst) MeV，自旋宇称J^P = 1⁺，是D_s(2P₁^{(′)})⁺态的一个候选者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找并确认新的激发态粲奇介子（excited charm-strange meson），以检验强子谱中关于重夸克-轻夸克系统的理论预言，特别是D_s介子家族的激发态结构。

Method: 基于LHCb实验在质心能量√s = 13 TeV下采集的质子-质子对撞数据（积分亮度5.4 fb⁻¹），对B⁰ → D⁺ D⁻ K⁺ π⁻衰变的完整相空间（full phase space）进行振幅分析（amplitude analysis）来提取新态的信号。

Result: 发现了一个统计显著性超过10个标准差的新共振态，其Breit-Wigner质量为m₀ = 2933^{+6}_{-5}(stat)^{+4}_{-3}(syst) MeV，宽度为Γ₀ = 72^{+18}_{-12}(stat)^{+7}_{-10}(syst) MeV，自旋宇称（spin-parity）量子数确定为J^P = 1⁺。

Conclusion: 新发现的介子被命名为D_{s1}(2933)⁺，是D_s(2P₁^{(′)})⁺态的一个候选者，为理解粲奇介子激发态谱系提供了新的实验依据。

Abstract: A new excited charm-strange meson is observed through an amplitude analysis of the full phase space of $B^0\to D^+ D^- K^+ π^-$ decays. The analysis is based on a proton-proton collision data sample collected by the \lhcb experiment at a center-of-mass energy $\sqrt{s} = 13\,\text{TeV}$, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $5.4\text{fb}^{-1}$. The statistical significance of the new state exceeds $10$ standard deviations. Its Breit--Wigner mass and width are measured to be $m_0 = {2933}^{+6}_{-5}(\text{stat})^{+4}_{-3}(\text{syst}) \,\text{MeV} $ and $Γ_0 = {72}^{+18}_{-12}(\text{stat})^{+\phantom{0}7}_{-10}(\text{syst}) \,\text{MeV} $, respectively, and its spin-parity quantum numbers are determined to be $J^P = 1^+$. This new meson, denoted as $D_{s1}(2933)^+$, is a candidate for a $D_s(2P^{(\prime)}_{1})^+$ state.

</details>

Wolf,F. L. H. Wolfs,S. Woodford,D. Woodward,C. J. Wright,Q. Xia,J. Xu,Y. Xu,M. Yeh,D. Yeum,J. Young,W. Zha,H. Zhang,T. Zhang,Y. Zhou*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文通过多散射事件分析与预活化数据约束背景，在LUX-ZEPLIN实验中首次以5.5σ统计显著性确认了$^{125}$Xe的正电子发射（positron emission），测得总分支比（branching ratio）为$0.29\pm0.08_{\text{stat.}}\pm0.04_{\text{sys.}}$%，并对$^{125}$I的各个衰变能级给出了首次约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: $^{125}$Xe作为LUX-ZEPLIN实验中子校准产生的短寿命活化产物（$T_{1/2}\sim16.9$ h），其衰变主要通过电子捕获（electron capture），但正电子发射虽已在高能级得到确认，低能级衰变（188 keV）仍未直接证实。本研究旨在通过更高精度的测量手段直接确认该衰变通道并给出分支比约束。

Method: 采用多散射事件分析（multiple-scatter event analysis）方法，并利用预活化数据（pre-activation data）约束本底（background），以提高对正电子发射信号的检测灵敏度。

Result: 以5.5σ的统计显著性（statistical significance）确认了$^{125}$Xe的正电子发射，测得总分支比为$0.29\pm0.08_{\text{stat.}}\pm0.04_{\text{sys.}}$%。这是首次对$^{125}$I各个衰变能级的分支比给出独立约束。

Conclusion: 该工作证实了$^{125}$Xe在188 keV能级也存在正电子发射，填补了此前仅通过三重符合测量（triple-coincident measurement）间接推断但未直接验证的空白，并为相关核衰变数据提供了实验依据。

Abstract: The radioisotope $^{125}\text{Xe}$ is a short-lived ($T_{1/2}\sim16.9 h$) activation product of the neutron calibrations performed in the LUX-ZEPLIN experiment. Subsequently, $^{125}$Xe decays primarily ($>99\%$) via electron capture, but positron emission has been confirmed by direct measurement to at least the 243 keV level of $^{125}\text{I}$. An additional decay to the 188keV level is expected from triple-coincident measurements of the annihilation and relaxation $γ$ rays, but has not been directly confirmed. By utilizing multiple-scatter event analysis and the pre-activation data to constrain backgrounds, this work reports positron emission with a statistical significance of 5.5$σ$. This corresponds to a total branching ratio of $0.29\pm0.08_{\text{stat.}}\pm0.04_{\text{sys.}}$ %, and is the first constraint to the individual branching levels of $^{125}\text{I}$.

</details>


### [173] [Effective field theory interpretation of ATLAS measurements involving the Higgs boson, electroweak bosons and the top quark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21670)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于ATLAS实验的多过程联合拟合，对维度-6有效场论（dimension-six effective field theory）中的Wilson系数（Wilson coefficients）进行了最全面的约束，未发现与标准模型（Standard Model）的显著偏离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了在有效场论（Effective Field Theory, EFT）框架下，利用ATLAS实验的多类测量数据对超出标准模型的新物理信号进行系统性搜索与约束。

Method: 采用联合拟合（combined fit）方法，同时约束48个参数（包括Warsaw基（Warsaw basis）下的单个Wilson系数及其线性组合），并通过对匹配（matching）过程将结果映射到双希格斯二重态模型（Two-Higgs-Doublet Model）和重矢量玻色子模型（Heavy-Vector-Boson Model）的参数空间。

Result: 联合拟合同时约束了Higgs玻色子多产生与衰变道、双Higgs、双玻色子、电弱Zjj、高质量Drell-Yan以及top-antitop过程的多类ATLAS测量，并纳入LEP、SLD和ATLAS的精密电弱可观测量（precision electroweak observables）。未观测到与标准模型的显著偏离。

Conclusion: 该联合拟合代表了ATLAS合作组迄今对实验数据最为全面的有效场论诠释，表明当前数据在EFT框架下与标准模型一致。

Abstract: Wilson coefficients in dimension-six effective field theory are constrained in a combined fit to several ATLAS measurements. These inputs probe Higgs-boson processes across multiple production and decay modes, di-Higgs signatures in the $b\bar{b}γγ$ and $b\bar{b}ττ$ final states, $WW$ and $WZ$ diboson signatures, electroweak $Zjj$ final states, high-mass Drell-Yan interactions, and top-antitop events in both resolved and boosted topologies. Precision electroweak observables from LEP, SLD, and ATLAS are also included. A total of 48 parameters, including individual Wilson coefficients in the Warsaw basis and linear combinations of Wilson coefficients, are constrained simultaneously. Constraints on two-Higgs-doublet models and heavy-vector-boson models are also obtained by matching a relevant sub-set of the results with their parameters. This combined fit provides the most comprehensive effective field theory interpretation of experimental data by the ATLAS Collaboration to date. No significant deviations from the Standard Model are observed.

</details>
